Dreams

(visual-line-mode) (cua-mode)

Sun 22 Sep XIX

In mechanic arts trying to get some coffee. Except mechanic arts was of course a new place of work. ?Trying to find the proper room for something?

Mon 23 Sep XIX

Hotel

Packing up from a hotel. There were cats, dogs & guinea pigs that had to be given back to the people who owned them – the hotel no longer kept them. Traffic jam at the elevator.

I placed some stuff in the bag to go, but then we couldn't find it. We looked all over for it, through the living room and the two bedrooms that were connected off a corridor. Eventually we gave up and said it was just one of those things and that they'd turn up. Because not to do so would have dedicated the remainder of the dream to the search in a fairly tedious way. Eventually they showed up stuck between the cushions of the sofa.

Office

I was working in data entry and eating the credit cards. I was actually a secret agent, so every day I would get a message about different places. This one involved two places in texas – one of them was Houston – and one place on the east coast. I printed out the map and the information, then would enter it it.

I had a nice desk along a wall where I had printed everything out and had started to eat the credit cards when a lady came by to look at the work I was doing with the map.

I started worrying if all the eating of the credit cards was going to start affecting my digestion. They crunched up nicely, but were still of course plastic. I ate several of them at a time, so the pieces would have been > 1mm. I worried that they might tear my intestines. All this worrying was happening in the bathroom of 1377.

Wed 23 Sep XIX

There was a large field. Maybe it was the white elephant outside Mechanic Arts but expanded. All the school children were getting ready to play a game there, a type of war game. Before they started, I stood on a mound near the middle and shouted out that all people who wanted to fight were idiots. One of the teachers leading the event told me to leave, so I did.

I went to a place where the sidewalk was divided in two and there were people on each side, trying to walk past each other. I walked along with them, walking a dog on a rope leash, until we came to a corner. At the corner, the street was filled with flowing, icy water. I left them there. They said it was too cold to get in and that the water would be too hard to swim through. But I apologized for leaving them and got in. The temperature was not too bad, and I was carried along the current with significant force, because this was the type of public transport they had for people who knew.

The icy current carried me rapidly away and around a corner. When it came to the next major intersection of the city streets, it stopped. It said that I had run out of money because I had no job. $1900. I had two choices. To try to struggle uphill and forward, which would have been tedious, or to turn to the right and go downhill, which I could easily do for free. It looked like there was some kind of park with bushes and equipment at the bottom of the hill. Maybe a conservatory? I chose the easy path.

When I got halfway down the hill, I saw that it was actually a recruiting station for the army, and the equiment was military jeeps. I certainly didn't want to join the military. There was an artist community outside the gates of the military base, but they were mostly there to do ads for the military base anyway.

I met a man from the base and was talking to him, trying to see what was around the corner to the right of the base. The path turned into an old dirt path, there was a valley and then a hill that you couldn't see over. I asked him what was over the hill and he said it was the wilderness and that there were wolves and mumblines. We looked and saw them coming over the hill. They were covered in a white gossamer covering. I started to walk along the side of the base through the trees and bushes.

Fri 27 Sep XIX, Toronto

in a stream

Waiting in line for an outing

Three of us were going somewhere. We had our tickets. The line was long and moving slowly, so my mother said that she would be right back. Soon the line started to move faster and I ended up getting on the bus alone. It was on the way to some kind of a mystery solving event.

But then my phone started to act funny, so I rebooted it. I couldn't find the reboot button, but there was a reboot button on the bus which worked. Unable to find the text message function on the phone – a recurring element. But when I rebooted it, it seemed to be part of the computer on the bus we were riding.

The Canadian contingent in a school that was putting on a play

There were many groups doing plays in the school, all down a long hall. The leader led me down the hall. I was allocated to the Canadian contingent because of some loose connection. They were doing great and were in the last room at the end of the hall. In a dark room near the front of the hall I was wondering about how I would deal with it when I got new people under me. Maybe I would bring them a care package.

Sun 29 Sep XIX

Phone not working in the office

I was looking for a place to sit. I went around to all the usual places, but they were full. And curved instead of straight as they had been in dreams previous.

I needed to find the text button on my phone but it wasn't working properly.

Grades at the university

I had prepared all the grades from class, including the statistical analysis. We sat down at a picnic bench to review them. The professor said they were 'poor'; I tried to argue that they were 'ok'. One of the ladies at the table made a joke about it being the University of Minnesota as opposed to the University of Minnesota.

Clayton's party

I got off the phone and got in my car. The electrics started to flake out on the car and since I was in the back seat it was hard to drive. The brakes stopped working so I put it in first gear and tried to drive along the wall to slow it down. I drove in the wrong lane and pushed pedestrians out of the way hoping it would stop.

Eventually I decided that the car was performing no worse than normal so turned around and went back to my destination. I got to Clayton's apartment and rang the doorbell. I had set up a calendar invite over a month ago. My car was now a funny looking tricycle, which he took away. We went inside and there was a huge party, with lots of his family and other friends of his family; a very middle class midwestern party with baked beans, kool-aid and cake.

We sat down after some minor chit-chat. Other ladies who were attending the party came in with some shopping and sat down next to us. Then the whole house disconnected from its mooring and began to be towed away. I wasn't sure where we were going but since his father had been into houseboats, I assumed that we were going to go out to a lake or river somewhere. I thought it would be a great picture to take to send to Gayatri once we got there and so decided not to call her yet. I watched the shops go by as we rolled down the highway.

Sun 19 Oct XIX

The Empire Strikes Back

Trenton was in the basement. He did something wrong and I wanted to tell him that it wasn't really very wrong; nothing to be ashamed of. We had a problem with rats and I was trying to get rid of them. I went around the house and was trying to take a shower. In the middle of the shower I was interrupted because someone was doing a hold-up at a convenience store nearby. Their rifle had a laser pointer on it and they were showing who they were pointing it at, threatening them, including me. I lay down and tried to hide the fact that I was calling 911 on my cell phone (which was a feature phone). I was unable to call without looking at it. But by the time I pressed '9' a police helicopter was coming by – someone else had already called them. The police helicopter became a helicopter sized rectangle shaped like a tablet and I wondered how it flew. Then a fleet of alien ships came from another direction. The robbers had been with the aliens. We ran into the brush and trees of the hills behind the store, thinking that if the ships had the ability to outpace us in the open, we had the knowledge of the back alleys.

Sun 12 Jan MMXX

Hawaii 5 0

I was in my bedroom in 1377. I had failed at Math and was going to take the CompSci test, but I wasn't sure if I was going to pass. The test was tomorrow so I had only one day to study. I was very tired and was spending most of my time resting, just trying not to fill my mind with other things so that I could concentrate for the test.

I was in a field, trying to be sociable with a bunch of business people at a conference. After I put in a token appearance that I tried to tell myself was adequate but which I knew wasn't (I was very tired), I went and sat down in the auditorium to listen to the speaker.

It was Dan Johnson. His presentation soon morphed into a preview video about new movies that were coming, featuring mostly a new movie that Tom Baker was in – Dan Johnson was Tom Baker. Tom Baker was with some kids and they were running from some pirate ghosts. But Tom Baker was able to dive back under the running pirate ghosts without getting caught by them and lead them away from the kids.

Then the movie became Hawaii 5 0 and we were all getting into 70's nostalgia. The main character from Hawaii 5-0 was driving an amphibious car accross a bay and into a tunnell normally reserved for boats. Then we were underwater with some underwater people taking a delivery of some fruit. Some of it was from a different tribe and we apologized for our ignorance about the distinction.

Then we were in rural India in a documentary about how they make opium, with the

Fri 20 Mar MMXX

A Party

I was talking to a guy behind a counter. He was actually a mob boss. We were comparing internet browswers. I told him about my use of FireFox. He asked which browser was best for a certian purpose. I said Firefox. He said "Really?" because it was a trick question: you can't actually change the namespace of a variable. He took a sidelong condescending glance at his friend and the conversation was over. I walked away.

I sat on a bench a ways away from the others. They were talking about some play. It was a city street and it was the living room of 1377. I made a point of getting some candy since I had brought some myself (see below) but they candy I picked up was not very good and it was wet and it stained my hand. I went to the kitchen to wash it off.

Driving to buy candy & soda for the party

my rear view mirror wasn't working and I pulled over into a driveway to try to adjust it. It made it difficult to drive because I couldn't see behind me and I got a confused impression of the traffic around me.

The store didn't have stuff on the shelves (again) you just brought the sample to the cashier and they brought out the real thing. But there was nothing explaining that so I was unsure what to get because I wanted to actually have it if that was not the case. I got chocolate, mountain dew and 3 sandwiches. They had lots of cake making material.

There were a lot of other people in line and it was hard to get around them.

Sun 22 Mar MMXX

I had to go on a journey up a hill, one which I had been on before in a previous dream. I commented how the dream in fact repeated itself. I had to take an umbrella (like Dr. Who) as a walking stick with me. Sometimes it was hard to move forwards along the same path as the dream had previously, and so I had to push myself along with the umbrella like a walking stick.

But at a point along the dream, before the path wound up on a dust muddy path through some mountains, I saw a side path and took it. I clambered over some rocks and came to an area where there were lots of old ladies and the houses were next to each other and the houses were clothes. I wanted some cereal from them and figured that I could just walk in and start eating the cereal as I had in other dreams where houses are pillagable. I pressed through the cracks between the clothes. The old ladies didn't like it and I fell down into a dark cave.

Mon 23 Mar MMXX – Vernal Equinox

We were in Children's theater, which was JCI. There was an empty office and I was in there with some other people like Ajith & Rahel. Some more junior people were asking me when the mumble would get approved. I said, in a very sarcastic way, "as soon as I know that I'm responsible for getting it approved". Then Gayatri & I had to leave and I wanted to go down the stairs but she wanted to take the elevator so we went to the elevator. We saw mumble from Minneapolis come out of the elevator and we said hi to her. The elevator was an open outdoor thing. we stepped in and started going down. Someone had their young sons with him and was allowing them to climb down the cable of the elevator which was at a 45 degree slant. We said we'd never do that.

Tue 24 Mar MMXX

I was walking down a hall in a school. Ladies were walking with me but I waited until we got to the end of the hall so I never got their number.

A hallway that was like a skyway in a shopping center. Talking about how cool some kid's music was. Running back to get a cloth from him. Walking along Snelling avenue between St. Clair & Grand, talking to the other people waiting for the bus about moisturizing your ears.

Sun 10 May MMXX

I was in a chair in a classroom. The old kind like from the U of M that was all wood and metal and sloped upwards. It was somwhat narrower than normal; dark & dusty at the back. I was finishing my homework on the computer, typesetting it and sending it in. I thought to myself that this was where I belong, doing pure technical work.

But then I had to answer questions from the students. I had had my headphones on and hadn't heard them ask. It was a question I didn't know the answer to; they pointed to the question in the textbook. I tried to answer as best I could. One time I said something that they knew not to be true and corrected me very animatedly.

It turned out that that was the class before mine, a more advanced class and I wasn't even responsible for those questions. I thought I would be teaching algebra and that it was started a couple weeks ago. I thought it amazing that they were forgiving me for flaking out on them before and not finishing teaching the class I started teaching. This had happened in a previous dream. I thought that maybe they were so desparate for teachers that they would forgive.

I spent a lot of time messing around and collecting tests. I would have a lot of tests to grade that night. I thought that it was algebra but actually the professor came in and said that it was calculus and that it had just started, so I would be doing the first lesson. Why it started later than the other classes I didn't know. I didn't even have the textbook and so I was looking around to fake it as usual by doing some exercises from the book.

I needed to get home to do the homework. I decided to walk to the bus stop which was a significant distance away. But as I was crossing a bridge, a bridge that was like 35, I realized that it was 8:20 and that the last bus was at 8:20. This was a bus that went by a circuitous route to near Highland Park. I had had adventures in dreams missing it and being on the wrong bus before. I was just at the kitty-corner bus stop when I saw the last bus go by. It had gotten dark by then.

Mon 11 May MMXX

There was a virtual reality application which allowed you to see the results of google searches, like for the historical extent of metropolitan areas, and then you would see it as a model in the middle of a field where there was a development going on.

I followed a bird up as it was flying, trying to guide it left, right & up.

There was a brief moment when all the jobs were open and I managed to get a teaching job at a Mechanics Arts that was in a northern suburb as a teacher of games. I thought it ironic that I had come full circle from having started War Games class at open school. My teaching responsibilities were very light since I had come in when everything was open, but things were closed now so no one else was coming in. My friend and I walked out of the lobby into the area at the front of the building.

One of my students had a complaint against her. She had been involved in a study for the school of marijuana products but had only tried one, one provided by a friend of hers. The complaint from a friend of a provider of a competing product was that she had not been objective. I felt that although the study was weak, the complaint of unethical behaviour was over-reaching. I kept rehearsing to myself how I would explain to her in terms of lessons learned and wondered if she would understand that language.

We met the complaintant sitting around a circular picnic table outside in the front of the building. We managed to get agreement on a token punishment. There were 4 of us. I agreed to tell her. I thought to myself that I would schedule a meeting for the next day. I got up with a couple of coats and started walking away, thinking that I would get some lunch. There were lunch places all along the driveway to the school and on the parallel street.

We

Saturday 16 May MMXX

Gayatri and I were sitting on a bench in the mall at the U of M outside the Math building, Vincent Hall. I had to ride my bicyle accross the Washington avenue bridge. But there was construction going on and I couldn't get there through my usual route. I asked one of the construction workers and he said that there wasn't a way. But I saw some people going through a different entrance so I started going there. There was a very steep decline and I was concerned both that it wouldn't actually lead to a way accross the river and that it would be very difficult to get back up. So I followed a path along a curve of the hill where some other people were going and it led to a corner of a city which was actually London.

I noted that I hadn't called Nate Longen in a while so I called him and left a message. I was suprised when, while continuing to bike through the old wet brick streets with old unused trolley tracks, he called me back. I couldn't hear his answers very well but I kept asking questions.

Then we were in a bar and he again suprised me by suggesting that we get a second round. He had a simple drink, I asked for a beer and we got into a long discussion with the waiter about the different types of beer they had. First we had only the wine menu and then the beer menu wasn't the one I'd seen before at that restaurant, but rather something more descriptive and expository about their beer products.

Professor Roberts was explaining stuff to me. Like maps from C2 -> C and something that looked like a very colorful map of a town. When he said goodbye he didn't accept a covid wave but rather gave a rather warm hug.

Sunday 17 May MMXX

Papa and Trent & I were supposed to go to some fair/vacation type thing. Papa got into the elevator and went down before I could get into it. I followed him but he wasn't there when I got down so I figured that he had gone on. There was a bathroom. The mens was larger than the ladies, as usual. The ladies sign was next to the mens with an arrow pointing the other direction and vice versa. When I got inside the urinals were funny and I had to urniate over the toilet paper. The cleaning lady was there and waited for me to finish before she replaced the toilet paper with a different type of dispenser. It was very crowded.

I left the restroom and came out directly to the cafeteria, where I assumed that Papa was getting something to eat. The direction was all backwards and I didn't know where to get what I wanted. It was very crowded.

I left the cafeteria unable to find anything and started wandering along the hallways between the various restaurants in the vacation/fair type thing. It was indoor but open to the air and it was very dark with lots of old dark wood.

I worried that Trent hadn't got the message that he was supposed to join us at the vacation/fair type thing. I tried calling him but couldn't get through. And how was he going to drive there anyway? In a van down highway 13 near Shakopee?

I was in an apartment which was both the Burlington and Dennis' old place in Arden Hills. There was a large group of people from work and I introduced myself as half Taiwanese to get that issue out of the way and establish that america was a country of immigrants.

Jeremy was supposed to arrive and there was a concern whether he should sleep in my bed and I could sleep on the couch or vice-versa.

Tuesday 19 May MMXX

I walked into the bathroom in Leo's house and there I saw Ann. Except that she was ill-formed, like a doll put together from different parts and not yet sure how to coordinate herself. She scared me because I didn't expect to see anyone there and I awoke.

There was going to be a performance with Dan Smith & Paul Reighard et. al. I was hanging around to help out but wasn't really actively participating.

Thursday 21 May MMXX

Sitting in a restaurant that was a waiting area and had like upper bunk beds to sit it. Trying to find a place to sit and study in the upper bunk without interfering with others. Walking out with one of the TK employees on their last day. Their locker was the one that was always vacant and small; there used to be a cat there.

Driving back home from John's, hoping to pick up my backpack becuase there was tobacco there. I was afraid about driving because I didn't have a license. I figured just as long as I didn't get in an accident I would be ok. But then it started to snow and all the other cars were slipping all over the road. I was just barely managing to avoid them.

Friday 22 May MMXX

Sneaking into a corner in a stone building. After dark when all the people had gone, the gargoyles woke up and walked around like highly colorful vaugely chinese decorated orcs.

Saturday 23 May MMXX

The return of the singer

When the singer was at my school three years earlier I had kept her writing on the blackboard waiting for her return. She was now here again and she erased it and put a new one. At one point her grafitti started to look like a swastika and I told her she'd better change it; it wasn't deliberate and she changed it. She presented a video that she had made, it was a mash up of a bunch of different pieces with a lot of cameos from others. She wasn't actually the famous singer but a second second side of the famous singer. But she knew all these people and they helped her put it together so it was very appropriate for our school and lasted nearly an hour.

As she left I tried to give her my card but I was having trouble finding one that my contact information was written on legibly. They were all of other people and written over in different fonts.

The Iraqi POW

We snuck through the tunnel into the POW camp inside Iraq. Then we were waiting around for them to process the prisoners. They were complaining about all the beauracracy and slowness in the process. We were all milling around a triangular shaped table waiting for our turn. I asked if there was concern about the extrajudicial executions.

Then we were in a small wooden room, waiting for our taxi to take us to the airpoint. Myself, the female journalist and one other. In the taxi we sat next to each other and she told me that she planned to return to Iraq. She wanted to spend as much time there as possible. We tried to call the airport but no one there spoke English and they hung up on us.

The airport was that airport. The one you were never sure if you were going to take off.

The Hill Line

Climbing up inside the hill to a secret entrance. Then running away from someone who was coming and hiding with my friend. We snuck outside and my Mother was there. I flew along the hill line towards St. Paul.

Sunday 24 May MMXX

Looking through my backpack on Grand avenue.

Monday 25 May MMXX (Bank Holiday/Memorial Day)

Moving the factory owned by Norma Banks

Someone had died and I was now responsible for disposing the estate, which included a factory that was going to move to a place closeby. I woke up in Norma Banks' basement and started to go upstairs to the kitchen. A lot of strangers in suits were there and the wanted to talk to me about moving the factory to different locations that were better for them. I told them 'maybe' even though it was pretty well settled where the factory was moving already. Someone (Kristin Banks?) said that I should have just told them no, and I tried to explain about keeping options open in negotiation.

Getting the bus in Bloomington

I was getting the bus with Dan Johson and one other, away from Thermo King, towards Highland park. The buses in the dreams always go to Highland Park. We were waking up from camp and leaving back home. I was able to get the proper change out of my wallet, which was unusual. It involved using another's ID card.

Crossing the highway in the middle of the day

I had two jobs, on either side of the highway in Roseville. And I would go between them in the middle of the day. Which would take a considerable amount of time out of the office. I wanted to avoid the waste of time, but didn't want to have to work a full day either.

The journey between the two involved cutting through along a bridge. This time I took the wrong bridge arch and ended up where it was rough ground to get to where you needed to be. I knew because I had tried it in a dream before. So I doubled back to go along the correct bridge arch. But the banks of the river were crumbly and the branches that were there were loose. It all came down with a great finality and plunged me into the water. The rest of the branches came down on top of me and kept me under. There was no question of being able to come back up as there might have been in a different dream.

Sitting in Gayatri's office

Gayatri was behind her desk and myself and some of her junior colleagues were sitting around in front of it. She was talking about a new business opportunity and I was pointing out similarities with work we had done previously.

Wednesday 27 May MMXX

Thermo King. Talking to Kevin Eichhorst who was sleeping in the warehouse. He didn't have to be at work at any particular time. I needed to be there but could be late. My cube was set up in front of the warehouse with my special computer setup. But when I booted it after being gone for a long time it errored out. Matt Nelson had come back and was still looking for a different job. But the e-mail that he got about the other job went to a folder that someone else had unknowningly sent to Tim Walker, who was now mad and everyone was mad at that guy for letting Tim know about Matt even though he hadn't known what was in the folder.

Wednesday 3 June MMXX

Coming back from Winnipeg along the highway. Crossing over into the US have to drive on the right side of the road again. Trying to get some food in a strip mall. The games I brought to play: legos, killer bunnies/pokemon cards; and who wanted to play.

Getting yelled at by Gayatri for getting the wrong type of car insurance and not checking over the add-ons. At a big meeting for a big new project, sitting around a living room. I pointed out that there were no product managers. They blamed me for the failure. I walked off trying not to feel bad about it.

Friday 5 June MMXX

In a large house. On the top floor to the left was the parent's bedroom; I was not supposed to go. There was light coming through the cracks of the doorframe. In an open room to the right were Sally, Gayatri and Trent. I left and went down the stairs precipitously. I went around the main floor looking for food and stuff in the cupboards.

In class worrying about taking notes. One class MWThF and a different one on T. Worried about transport there and how I had just failed the last class.

Lots of running around the basement of 1377 looking for tobacco and marijuana.

Sat 6 June MMXX

Waiting at the *21 bus on Lake Street. Many different buses stop but only one I want to get to Snelling & Grand. Get tired of waiting and start to walk down to the next stop. This has happened many times before in my dreams. Then I realize I forgot my coat and run back to get it. But someone has taken it. I try to grab it away from him and end up twirling him around in the air as he holds on to it. Only by continuing to spin him around above my head like a lasso can I keep him from harming me; also he refuses to let go. In a convenience store, a young girl with dyed hair says that she will give me a blow job if I slam him into the wall. I agree and she does.

Sun 7 June MMXX

There is no concept of a girlfriend in the fourth dimension. Having to explain that to someone on a voice call as part of the PFS. It became difficult to speak as if I were very tired and mumbling.

My 500k project was being held up because of a $60 parking charge. Explaining this to a young secretary in the lobby and telling her that if she thought that was interesting she would make a great project manager. It became difficult to speak.

A brush fire was started. It was mostly working itself out but I tried to turn the hose on to see if that could help even if only in a small way. Then I got in trouble with the UK authorities for having done so. We were driving so fast on the UK highways, with lots of emergency vehicles everywhere. Some kind of competetion between the various emergency services. I thought it was not like the India culture shock because India was so different you were isolated from it. UK is close enough that the differences get under your skin and become jarring.

Mon 8 June MMXX

A girl was coming to stay overnight in my room in 1377. I told her to go sleep in the basement. I was worried that she might think it too dirty. I started working on a painting; covering over some acrylic waves with oil. The oil was to my suprise still wet. When I went and looked she was huddled in the corner and not downstairs. We decided to leave early in the morning rather than sleeping through the night.

Tue 9 June MMXX

Swimming Teacher

Art Supply Store in the Mall

The Creature in the Swamp

The Road to the Hills in the Suburbs

Wed 10 Jun MMXX

Lucky Bus Seat

I had left my notes that I had carefully prepared for my class. When I got on the bus, everyone left. I went to the downstairs on the bus and sat in the first seat. And there were my notes!

Th 11 Jun MMXX

Gayatri & I were leaving an apartment. We had gotten all our stuff there but didn't know how we would get it back because we couldn't drive. When I went to ask the driver who had gotten us there he had lost his arm so he couldn't help.

We were invited to a party and we didn't realize it was a birthday party so we hadn't brought a gift. We were going to provide a film which was on a disk (LP size) but when I went to review it I saw that there were recordings of her with my dick in her mouth, so I had to run around asking people how to erase it before anyone saw it.

Fri 12 Jun MMXX

At a fair, forgot my cell phone. Just had < $5 in my pocket. Trying to get food/sleep/rest-room. Running around the outside hall past food courts and ushers worrying about how to get back in.

Sneaking up the hallways cut in the rock to the side door by where they sacrificed to the volcano. Let by large insects to outsmart the demon somehow with this access to the side door. Not sure how.

Wed 17 JUne MMXX

On the streets of New York. I had a job that gave me a place to sleep on a bench in a room full of other kids. They had just sold part of the building to another company and we had to allow passage. I went down in the basement through a garage where others were working. I had to paste some pieces of ceramic together. My boss came back from vacation and was being friendly. I couldn't remember what he had been doing. Skiing? He had been on a beer tour of Holland. I had to go through the garage and didn't have any ID. I was worried that people would stop me but everyone was very nice.

Th 18 June

School/Work was in a basement. I had to go to Ulrich's new office, which was a corner of an open floor plan. When I got there, there had been a power outage in that area and everyone had left so I didn't know where he was.

We were all waiting in an auditorium to be dismissed from school at the end of the day. I had 'borrowed' a ladies sweater because I was going somewhere cold so I delayed my exit until she was gone so that she wouldn't see that I had it. I had all kinds of warm clothes and was planning on wearing double layers when I got where I was going.

A funeral for an animal. It started to rain and thunder. A little girl gave a eulogy. The animal was placed in a large tractor tire and rolled into the river.

The road to Winnepeg leads to Belgium.

Fri 19 June

Walking with Gayatri down the alley behind 1377. Trying to define a parade, I had Gayatri calling out a 4 beat, I then tried to bring in the strings with Am G F E7 (there weren't any strings) and was going to move on to the brass when we realized that the other band was doing a better job. Gayatri did a little dance.

In the basement of John Bank's house everyone had an instrument to give a demo, except me, I was flying though the hallways.

There was a troll, upside down. I was able to keep him away from me in a force field.

I was trying to break out of the university building. I took the shutters off but then couldn't climb out the window. A policeman saw me and started to interrogate me. There were a lot of questions about how I had been in London. He couldn't really do anything.

Sat 20 Jun

Stopping my Father's car on Summit Ave.

Tue 23 Jun

Canoe Trip.

On top of a high plateau with pianoes and Dan Smith. We fell off. I tried to make him hit first. But then we flew at the last minute.

Mon 29 Jun

Lots of dreams about packing up and going to visit my father & paternal grandmother. In cafeterias trying to get the right food and I can't.

Wed 1 Jul

Biking to Lake Street.

Th 2 Jul

They were herding us. We had to put all our stuff in lockers and then we were going to sleep in bunks. I had a lot of valuable stuff like my passport & UK visa in the locker and I didn't know if I would even be assigned that bunk. And there were no locks. Putting a lock on would have attracted notice.

We had to go around room in a school/museum and they would play games with us. Paint would drip out of the ceiling and we had to try to avoid it. The paint never came off. It was like being zombies.

They took us away and we were going to go over the Lake Street bridge from Minneapolis to St. Paul. We were planning on walking accross the ice but the middle of the river had thawed and we couldn't get through. Everyone turned around to go back but I didn't; I lay down on the side of the bridge. To fall in the water would have been death because it was near frozen. I fell asleep and woke up on the St. Paul side of the bridge.

I went to the school and was trying to avoid the worst of the games. One of the teachers who directed us through the games fell in love with me. I was concerned that people would see us hugging but she said that didn't I know, in her species the sexual organs were in the back so when people thought we were just spooning we were actually making love. I felt an immediate sexual attraction and agreed to run away with her.

We ran back over the Lake Street bridge from the Minneapolis side. There were many people coming and going, above and through a subway. It was vaugely victorian/cyberpunk. She wanted to go on the left side where people from the UK would be going to the US but I said no, we should go on the right side because anyone we met there wouldn't know us; on the left side if someone passed us they might recognize us.

Fri 3 Jul

The turtle, the mouse, the fox & the baby

We were trying to carry the turtle along the boulevard. All of these were in the baby carriage. But then the fox (dog) got out and started to chase a squirrel. I then realized that the turtle (baby) was missing. I ran around trying to find them. If I followed the mouse I could have found the turtle but I lost even that.

Music that annoyed my Dad

I was drawing. Then I decided to put staff notation in the picture. Then I hooked up electronics which would play the notes that were drawn. But since I had drawn them sloppily they were out of tune. This annoyed my father who asked me to stop.

In the Lab with Carl

The turtle was there too. There was a big picnic lunch for everyone with salad and chips, sandwiches and soda. I was talking about how similar the test equipment in my new place was to my old place. Carl was collecting a bunch of equipment in the lab while I looked around it. The lab was Cathy's room at Mechanics Arts. Finally he had a bunch of speakers set up and made a very loud bass sound. I covered my ears and went out to the rest of the party where a small girl followed me around.

Sat 4 Jul

In Leo's living room. We had been packing to go home and had bought too many souveniers and food. There was now way we could take it all with us on the plane and we were waiting till the last minute to pack it. Fortunately her mom had put all the extra stuff in boxes and would ship it to us. The stuff was all in Ann's room.

I was playing video games on the TV and drinking wine straight from the bottle early on a Saturday morning. Vic & Sid came in and then everyone else. By the time everyone else got there I was already tired and so I said that I was going to bed. In Ann's room.

Sun 5 Jul

This time my father was going to take my son, me and my maternal grandmother to the airport. I spent a lot of time in the bedroom and only got to talk to my grandmother for a short period of time. I was in the bedroom, which was like a school dorm. There were giant TVs playing cartoons all over the walls. They had ads about how you should exercise during the pandemic, and which stated that light exercise was not the kind of exercise they were talking about. So I got out of bed and went running. My running path was down 90th Street in Bloomington.

Gayatri and I were trying to adjust the microwave and get the trays in right. Then I realized that they had high medium and low stickers, color coded on them, but you could only see them when you pulled them out.

Mon 6 Jul

In the basement of 1377 listening to the radio.

Tue 7 Jul

On a long trip overnight into the north. Standing by a tree reading something love-craft-esque. People started coming as the dawn broke. On the way back they had shut down the bus and told us that we shouldn't do drugs. I left by way of the mental health clinic.

Wed 8 Jul

In the living room of 1377 with Clayton & Dennis. Preparing to play a game which was exactly like Melee except that instead of mideval warriors they were spaceships. There was a base, standard fighter and a scout as the 3 basic pieces, with (movement, firepower) (increasing, decreasing) by orders of magnitude in each case.

Sat 11 July

In the side room of the basement of 1377. Having a dinner for a large number of people. I thought some girl had taken my plate but it was the other way around.

Christmas a Leo's, except it was a hotel/cabin. Reading through the day. Then we decided to go to dinner. Showering in the couch which was near the piano. I complained that my wife didn't let me bring enough clothes so If I changed for dinner I wouldn't have any clean clothes for the trip home.

Sun 12 July

In the dungeon of 1377 smoking a cigarette.

Mon 13 July

Dr. Who. Running though elevators and train tunnels. Professing my endless love to one of the old companions who came back through time to tell the doctor that the current situation would be resolved by his sister would die. A new series of books, the 'Sky' series.

Tue 14 July

By the train bridge near University Ave. Secret agent. Had to get out of the car and go to apartment 1112B, which was in a stationary train. I found the building but not the apartment. There were lots of fancy shops and restaurants in the train, like a hotel.

Wed 22 July

In a church; they were going to summon the devil. There was some uncertainty about which side was which. It was just a big dog with a funny head. It didn't really harm us.

Exit speech for Rahel again. Getting a bottle of cider; was going to take it home but shared with his friends instead.

In the stacks of the library crawling in the dark and trying to hide. The cell phone light in my pocket I was afraid would give me away.

Sat 25 July

Gayatri and I and a colleague in the kitchen of 1377. Emptying a clear plastic water filter the size of a kitchen trash can. It was for a seminar that we weren't really prepared for because the people who knew about it were no longer there. But it didn't matter because we just had to show up we didn't have to present anything. I wanted it to at least be clean when we were there. When I pored the water into the sink to clean it the water went to shoulder level in the entire house and I was above the sink.

In the basement and side room of 1377 with a lot of dung.

Sun 26 July

Teaching algebra on tuesday afternoon. I thought I had a fun exercise with 3x5 cards – everybody would write a different name that could be part of an acryonym and then we would combine them randomly, but it didn't work out; I couldn't read my own samples. I tried to fake it through the exercises as I usually do in these dreams. I have never prepped for the class and plan on just doing some exercises to fill in time. I tried to find the place we were at and there were a lot of comparative recepies in the book. All the expamples were about food.

The class room started to fill up much more than expected. I realized that everyone was there for the concert that was happening in the same room after. I ran out of time so I dismissed the class and left.

I was in an elevator with maybe it was Charles Gormely. We went up one floor to the storage attic before we were to go down. He commented that they were keeping the dangerous chemicals right next to each other, just in different color drums, red and blue. I said it was all just turpentine, wasn't it? The elevator started to move along horizontally along the top floor where the storage was and then down a curving slope. I commented on the bottles of industrial nitrate and said that that was the one that you needed to be dangerous.

Fri 30 July

Driving my fathers car backwards I couldn't stop

Sun 2 Aug

Finding a place in the new office setup. Everyone had open seating but fixed desks by convention. The main area was the west cluster at Thermo Kind and the lab was Cathy's room in Mechanics Arts, but filled with stacks of electrical equipment. I found a room with an office but then they were moving us around again and I was confused about where to sit. One of the desks was a bed. I kept staring at my notes thinking that there was something I should be doing. I complained about where I was going to keep all my papers. We were cleaning the place. The cleaning spray created a brown foam that I had mistaken for dirt but when we scrubbed it away it was cleaner than before. I was one of the most fastidious in cleaning. Prasad came in and started talking about Graham's promotion to my level. Graham turned and looked me in the eyes wondering if I really considered him my equal.

Mon 3 Aug

Blakes 7

Landed on the planet. The people had been wiped out and there were some ugly aliens. There was mysterious discussion of the Dark Iron age. Why had their civilization declined and what were the alien's role in it? Turned out the Dark Iron age was when they built too many skyscrapers and relied too much on technology. The arrival of the aliens showed them how to live sustainably and so they abandoned their cities.

Interview

I told the story of how one guy told me he went home to program for fun but very few people go home to manage for fun. I had to distinguish between that and simply talking shop outside work. They all had red eyes as if from a camera flash.

Wed 5 Aug

Driving my Mother's car the brakes weren't working. I thought that I could work at my new job and alternate days back at Thermo King. I went to TK and the old crew from Watlow was there.

Th 6 Aug

Dogs on the corner of lexington & grand. walking along lexington to st clair seeing all the new houses. flying across the ayd mill bridge up the hill to 1377. ended up in my grandfathers bedroom in an attic. we were waiting for our flight and had to drive back from the north shore to duluth by 9. gayatri told me to not worry as we had plenty of time. someone mentioned the pink floyd song 'set the controls for the heart of the sun' and i tried to play it on the speaker system. I couldn't find my main phone.

father & grandfather were putzing around the barns doing makework as there was no need to be in the fields. they were smoking indoors and i thought that old fashioned and annoying.

the black knight was doing bad things in the basement of the school. the white knight came to put him right. they asked me if I supported the white knight. Fri 7 Aug

Sat 8 Aug

Taking the number 82 bus back from the U of M. I had decided to drop out of chemistry class but it was still before the deadline. So much distance between 1377 and the university, and other responsibilities and activities.

Getting out of the skyscraper. Down the stairs everyone was waiting, including on the railing. Mon 10 Aug

Lying down on the train to the next town to see the doctor, taking the day off work. I knew they would be understanding about my absence. Expensive ticket. Only passenger. Not sure the conductor respected me. After train tracks, went through residential streets.

The doctor couldn't see me till the next day, but I managed to get back where I lived in a glass store in a strip mall. He was able to call the prescription in to a pharmacy next door. I kept trying to count the pills out and kept losing track. Even in the passenger seat of a car.

Waiting for Wells to come visit me in a basement where I was stockpiling food. I thought to start with where we were last years ago on the St. Clair bus and see where things go from there. Cleaning up pencils lying in the hallway.

Driving out of a parking ramp. I could go up stairs, I just didn't want to get stuck behind anyone.

Sat 15 Aug

My mother and I were doing eye tests downtown st. paul in a hallway. when I looked through the grating that did the test she reminded me that she only had one eye and I could see it dark and empty.

Was going to the fair with john. I called dan to ask if he wanted to show up. It was late, so I started looking for the men's bathroom, but they were all closed. Mon 17 Aug

On a camping trip with my father. He was supposed to get the trucks to take our stuff to the next site. He was giving a long explaination of all the details leading up to the delay. I got bored and was gazing at the clock on the church tower over the river.

The buffet line for breakfast was too crowded and they didn't have anything except sweets. The cashier had an advertisement for a sugar substitute, I said if they were against sugar they should offer other options.

Down the hill a sense of peace.

Wed 19 Aug

In the offices of CelTrak, they had set up a personal download of all ambient sound and other sensor information for a teenagers house who wanted to do it with some money they got. Th 20 Aug

Down an escalator. My girlfriend went on the other one and went past. Then when it ended on the floor before, I had to try to find a way down. Talking to the PMO guy. Using water in the bottle and asking for more as a metaphor. Asking if the total amount of water in all the bottles was equal to the right number based on the number of people in the team.

Sun 23 Aug

At 1377. It was Dan Smith's going away and I had to get a bunch of suitcases for him from across town. It was down a street that was like Snelling+Ford+Lake+92nd. Getting breakfast with a Swedish exchange student. But the kitchen wasn't open yet so all they had were cold items and snacks. I had nothing to say.

Mon 21 Sep

Buying my dad's car. The wheels were badly out of alignment. Crawling over cube walls to get to America.

Tue 22 Sep – Fall Equinox

In a school. Had to leave up the winding dark staircase. No shirt. Got to the top and the guard wanted me to leave. When I told him I didn't have my keys, wallet or phone he agreed to accompany me inside (TK) to look for them. The 3rd floor of TK was the 3rd floor of Open School. There were 2 people there and they were saying how they worked in pairs and when one's heart would wear out the other's would too. This just happened to one of them and we wen't running to tell another pair that we thought might be in the same situation.

Wed 23 Sep

Getting stoned and going to school

Th 24 Sep

Walking through the halls of the school, feeling very paranoid. Was in Shell feeling resentful about not being given as much opportunity as others. I started playing with a plant and eventually killed it, throwing it in a nearby trash can and hoping no one noticed.

Fri 25 Sep

Walking with a girlfriend. Making out reluctanly under the covers. Her dad was skeptical. On the bus he is questioning me. Get off the bus go down the stairs to a resort. There is free wine to start; I refuse. I go first and get the the restaurant. The waitress asks me how many. I am trying to count my whole family and get to about nine. The waitress is trying to find a bigger table. My dad comes in and says it will only be 3.

Waiting for the rest of the family in a cabin in the Australian desert. There are dead animal carcasses on the floor and none of the machines work; they are flooding the place with water. Suddenly I realize that the animals were attacked by something bigger than me and I have to get out. I call the family to tell them that I won't be there. I get Grandma and she tells me they are all asleep. I say to wake them up. My phone is a small bottle and it only works to talk to the one person you are thinking about.

Sat 26 Sep

Putting our rental car keys back in an automated device for returning them. I pushed the buttons correctly but forgot to attach the paperwork. Then I realized we didn't have a key left to drive back to the airport.

Was trying to find a place to smoke in an office building that used to be a large house. All the doors that used to lead to bathrooms no longer did. There was a possibility that there was opium in my tobacco.

Coming home from over the highway. When I came to the school there was a big puddle of water. I had come accross this before. I was able to skim accross part of it, but it went further and eventually I was swimming. The last time I only had to swim a little bit but this time I was swimming all the way to the highway. I took a wrong turn and started down a path to the railroad tracks instead of the bridge over the highway. It was good I realized it and turned around because it was very hard to swim back uphill.

Sun 27 Sep

Riding my bike up a steep hill. Couldn't make it and started to walk it. Even then it was hard and I started to slip down the dirt. Finally I made it to a trapdoor, which led to a starbucks that was closed. I didn't want anyone to think I had broken in so I didn't wan't to leave by the front door for fear of tripping an alarm. But what I thought was a side door also tripped an alarm.

Wed 30 Sep

Trying to get a shower. My family were around. There was supposed to be a shower curtain in front of the oven in the kitchen in 1377 but I couldn't get it to work.

Th 1 Oct

There was a lady in the church who had the devil in her. All the signs were there. Someone was assigned to look after her. When the devil finally came out of her, the person assigned decided they liked the devil better. Comedy ensues. A B film targeting a black audience.

In Thermo King, they made the bathrooms equal sized between men and women. But a large part of the mens bathroom was showers which came on automatically and i started to get wet.

Maybe they had a ridiculous statement to make About something they hadn't experienced Possibly Sam had a different opinion That nobody'd ever considered important And damn it if Norman and Betty were listening Somebody would have become a phenomenal Howling lightning tampering with the electrical Evidence shown to be relevant Possibly with the exception of ivory Everyone else had abandoned the obvious Chipping away at erroneous garbage Which definitely is as exciting as pudding Deliciously spooned from the lap of the ludicrous Into the mouths of the question less idiots Licking their lips as their eyeballs are rolling And flapping their tongues as they're losing their marbles That's the way Sam's play around That's the way Sam's play Someone who wasn't related to anyone Twisted the facts till the truth was apparent And dished up a dollop of dubious doo-doo That sparkled like something folks scrambled to swallow Slipping the rich through the eye of a needle Is easy as getting a camel to heaven And granny transgressing had blubbered a bibful Of classified info on Milton's imbroglio

Friday 2 Oct

The object, the perception of the object & the model of the perception of the object.

Sat 3 Oct

Sitting outside a synagoge. Well if you don't want to talk about god then don't come in here. All the many people walking past me. Looking for Gayatri, knowing I wouldn't see her. Waiting thinking if I should just become a sage and sit there forever. Knowing I would get lost if I tried to get up and find her. Eventually I got up and pressed through the crowd to the edge of a valley. I flew through the valley and ended up on the streets of Minneapolis.

Trying to bring furniture upstairs. I was blocked by some sound equipment. Waiting.

Sun 4 Oct

Was in a house. The people who were renting it before me were kicked out because they couldn't keep it the way the landlady wanted. But I was crawling all over the walls, trying to climb up the bookcase to get to the attic where I could climb over to the next building.

Mon 5 Oct

Another B movie. We had to sneak north. Eventually we decided to do it via the old underground railway routes. We had to take a large amount of flowers for a sick lady friend and for another reason.

Wed 7 Oct

Coming home on the train, too tired from visiting friends in the north twice on different days. Wanted the child to sleep. Couldn't get sleep myself. In a big dark room, I thought it was empty and that I could go to the bathroom, but there was another entrance and people were there anyway. Trying to get food and drink; only that in my own home was satisfying. Having a temp job but I didn't show up one day and they had me doing something unfamiliar in a different room.

Th 8 Oct

Was going to run a mile in a work competition. Hadn't exercised for a long time and worried about it; also about being the oldest person there. Difficulty finding my clothes in my bedroom in 1377. John Banks was there and I was complaining to him about being late. Then Les came by and said it was time to go. The elevator didn't go up all the way and I had to walk. But finally we got to work and the event wasn't starting yet so I tried to go to the bathroom. I was glad that I decided to come to work instead of just going to the event. The first bathroom was a shower and I got wet. The second one was a urinal for both men and women. A young girl was talking about socialism and she put my penis in her mouth. Then posed for pictures with my semen running down her chin. It was the latest fashion among punks.

Fri 9 Oct

On the bus to 1377. Sally was telling me that she only had to worry about money for 4 more years because I would be retirement age then and she could get a settlement. She was going to leave the country until then.

Sat 10 Oct

I had my apartment at the corner of University & Snelling, *169, $300/month. I had reserved it and was waiting for it but I didn't know how it would go over with either my previous or next wife. I was carrying 2 small furry animals in boxes on the bus. I was getting off the bus early and walking a long way home, over two miles. I thought to myself that this was why I felt so good. Debate in the school hallways.

Mon 12 Oct

In a grocery store with Gayatri. Arguing about how to push the carts. She started eating a bananna before paying for it. I explained to her that she shouldn't do that. A maintenance worker from the store came and charged her for it, explaining why she shouldn't do that. Then we left, hand in hand, up the hill to the school in Italy.

Sun 11 Oct

I was in a hospital operating room. They were sticking something in my ears that would affect my brain.

Tue 13 Oct

Petting a cat. Talking to Muhammed and Adolfo, who were at Watlow. Giving them a lecture on how to do parallel development and debugging.

Wed 14 Oct

In Winona checking up on Watlow. Skip was wondering why I was grading papers. It was a cover.

Th 15 Oct

Lake street bridge. When young I had gotten into a semi-truck and it rolled into an intersection. I escaped but it was Grand Theft Auto and I was marked with guilt for life. The Marshall avenue hill as a metaphor for my father's disappointment in me. Trying to sneak up to a convenience store at the top of the hill with a little bit of weed in my pocket to smoke it. I thought about going back for my pipe. It was busy and I couldn't find a place to do it in secret. One of the workers, who had down syndrome, tried to offer me a bag of candy. I refused it politely and the other worker told him to accept my refusal.

F 16 Oct

Working at a new company. They were trying to debug a system. The messages had broken and were intermittent. I said that they would have to revert the last 4 changes and put them in one by one to see where it had broken. When I realized that the failures were intermittent I said it must be the CRC. one of the ladies figured that out as well at about the same time. We all gathered in a theatre for a presentation. These people were very crass in the use of language and the ladies all wore red lipstick. They were doing a demo. It was all about selling wire.

My boss got interrupted on his phone by his kids calling to show them dancing around the kitchen and then out to the bus and the park. The park was near the further Cretin/Derham where Younes had invited me earlier.

From Laptop (Richmond)

Th 29 Oct

Trying to find my baggage. The flight was actually identified at gate 11 and I just had to get there. Trying to find the way back to where I left my baggage. I couldn't but Pablo did.

Fri 30 Oct

Walking down a dusty road looking for something. Past a poor area in the city. U turn at a pedestrian stoplight.

Sat 31 Oct (Halloween)

I was playing an electronic instrument to annoy my father so he broke it.

Release and Extinguish: Anguished? Externalise.

Sun 1 Nov

Back in the house owned by macalester. it was apt 313. The door was open. it was filled with old furniture and fittings but nobody was there.

I made some commitments to be at different places on Monday. But then I was following Gayatri around and I was too polite to check my phone to see my schedule so I missed them. I went down through some passaageways to find Sally waiting for me in a suburban kitchen ready with complaints.

I was in Econ class. Mark was also there. I remembered saying that I liked Econ. I thought how vain I was to think that if I was good at math of course I could do Econ. And what about the Geometry class I bombed. The professor was asking why I was so tired. Because of covid nobody was working. I couldn't remember if I was in a week where there was shutdown or after it; I was transcending time. So I tried to give him a generic answer. He thought that if we weren't working at least we would be exercising more. I said aw you know how it is even if your work doesn't involve putting boxes on trucks if you plan to exercise 10 times more often than normal you'll only end up exercising 5 times more often than normal. My work had never involved putting boxes on trucks.

Mon 2 Nov

In a supermarket. We brought all our stuff there for the movers to take away but then we had to come back for a second shipment. I found some blue fireworks and was trying to hide them when a dog found them and I had to pretend about what they were. Then I started being able to pack them away in a box with some christmas tree balls.

I was sitting in a corner wearing my best white shirt and black pants thinking I've finally made it to becoming homeless.

Wed 4 Nov

Leaving an old house where my grandmother was. urinating all over the floor. a secret agent was driving gayatri and I somewhere and he knew a shortcut through a dry riverbed. we were very worried about getting wet. but we glided along and it became a ladder into a factory where another man greeted us.

Th 5 Nov

In a small waiting room. I had to go to the bathroom and the water ran all over the floor. I tried to clean it up with towels.

Fri 6 Nov

Stroganoph pool. We were going to a lawyer who was used to dealing with extortion clients. They were bent out of shape and constantly had to perform surgery on themselves, including a monty-python esque faux stereo brain surgery. He set us down to a fancy meal including beef stroganoff and flatbread. He would fill his swimming pool with beef stroganoff and swim in it while his guests were eating. I asked for flatbread without meat and the waitresses just started taking the meat off with their hands.

Sat 7 Nov

Dice with Clayton

We went and sat outside a restaurant. We weren't actually eating but the waitress brought Clayton a fancy drink which he shared half with me. She asked me what I wanted. I asked for the menu. She said that she wasn't going to bring the whole table out so could I just say what I wanted and she would see what she could do in that direction. I asked for ice tea. She looked disappointed and put upon. Another waiter came and was cutting up fruit to give us pieces to bet with. He asked if we wanted 2 pieces or 1. I said 1 because I wanted to get going. No one could think what to bet on. So I bet that I would get 7 or more on 2 dice. Clayton took the bet but the two others didn't. I rolled a 10 and won. Then I explained that the odds were in my favor. I think Clayton knew that, he was just being sportsmanly.

Running past airport security

They were taking away criminals for execution. Then they started taking away people indisriminantly. The trick was that if you used a pencil instead of a pen it would short the machine. We ran upstairs. It was a futuristic airport but it was also the kitchen of 1377. We ran past airport security. I had the doctor who pass that showed people whatever they wanted to see. My mother got her real ticket and we went around a corner to a restaurant to plan our next steps.

Helping with the English Election

I was helping with the UK election – but only in the reception because not a citizen. A lady came in with 5 votes, because you could buy a vote for 25k and she came into 125k. She wanted to know if she could do all 5 or only 1. I thought you could do all 5 but I said I'd ask. She left 4 with me and put one in the ballot box. The room was like an old hotel lobby. I started flirting with her and then left to walk down the hall. I saw myself in the mirror and was ugly. Yes, after I woke up I realized that one does not get 5 votes just because one pays.

Reflections on the Past

Mon 9 Nov

Party organized by the adults in 1377. All the boys were in the dining room. Then the girls were in the (room that would be there if the mirror was a door). I thought this is great, leave the boys together till there is nothing to say and similarly for the girls, then put them together so there is even less to say. My mind was a complete blank. Then I thought wait a minute do i really want to be led into a relationship with the girls my family chooses for me?

We were on a school bus and there were educational toys to play with between the seats. I started a conversation with a friend.

Wed 11 Nov

Driving Gayatri on my handlebars. We went on the side highway to 'Paul' which was a small town in Minnesota not to be confused with St. Paul. We stopped at a little roundabout to rest and check the map where some bikers were also resting. Gayatri made a joke about their leather jacket that was appropriate to some other part of the dream.

In the bathroom cleaning up she stepped into the bath. My nose hairs grew to thick braids about 4 inches long. I asked her if I should cut them. Before we could decide they had shrunk back in to my nose. I thought it strange that all that hair was in there and wondered what would have happened had I cut them.

Sat 14 Nov

In a suburban backyard with a work group. Counting pennies. A lady came over and wanted to join us. Wish I may wish I might. Never heard that before. Trying to figure out a kids toy that had some digital IO.

Trying to find a place to send a fax for mama. none of the fax machines worked. Sitting with Gayatri between me and Trent. I moved over to between them.
