Mon 16 Nov

Some guys going out for dinner. Trying to get enough rest on a day before an exam. Also a lady who didn't have much money but she's going to make everything allright. Is she going to become a prostitute? Over the bridge. Through the business I follow her. It does not suprise anyone that we can leave. She has the key and the boss hasn't arrived yet. She borrows 24 dollars. She says to meet me at a certain address. Is it the rental car place? Yes it is. The deposit for a rental car is 24 dollars. She doesn't have the money to pay the rest but that is not deterring her. The guys walk past the store on the sidewalk. I expect them to invite me to dinner but they just say 'see you tomorrow'. So I guess that means that I am following her. I put my backpack in the back seat. It is a mini. Where will we go?

Tue 17 Nov

Going to take last math test, past Summit avenue going north they suggested I go to a vocational school for tiling. On the train along 7th street I had no job and was running out of money. In class I sat down, I was an hour late but the test was short – only 4 pages – and I expected it to be easy. I went back and picked up the test after sitting down. Everyone was eating lunch.

Th 19 Nov

Eating a pancake in a mall. A lady came by and started telling me how to do it so I got tired of it and left.

Gayatri and I were in our new farmhouse. When I woke up the water was leaking. I tried to turn it off but then the whole thing broke. It was glass, and I told Gayatri, who was sleeping in a bed in the corner of the kitchen, to cover her face. Then water was falling all over the place and I was trying to find the off switch but Gayatri was just saying to wait until we called someone to fix it because we didn't know where it was.

The car went in reverse backwards along a dirt driveway and I couldn't stop it but I could steer it. I did (backwards) circles in a field until it slowed down. Then it became a bike and I was trying to get a guitar through an amplifier on the bike but the volume was low. Someone was watching me.

Fri 20 Nov

The Minneapolis airport. They were going to change the name of the city to Pantiera or something like that. It was just a row of concrete hangers before the sea. I was in the morning for a night flight and I wanted to check out the gate early. I got through with a different flight that was taking off. Then I left my carry on and went to find the bathroom. But the bathroom wasn't where I expected it and I ended up going out back past security. Then I couldn't get back in to where my carry-on was left so I had to go to the counter and explain the whole situation.

Driving in the parking lot to C2 or B3 where northwest had their slot permanently allocated. Inappropirate touching from a faux mystic who may have been professor vandendorpe. Crawling clumsily accross people's laundry placed on a wall.

Sat 21 Nov

Going to see emily in minneapolis. I had to take the bus. My dad brought both cars over and left them in a parking lot. It was like, how am I going to get them home, I am not supposed to drive – no license. We decided I could. Gas was low and I would have to get gas immediatly. I went to emily's school and started walking down the hall. But then I got a call from the service station. They needed to move my car for something they were doing. They were also going to fix the tail light and wanted confirmation. This was like a 'we wont tow you if you pay us and the excuse is we'll do this work'. I had the money so I said yes. I wondered where I got the money from and how long it would last.

I went to class. I was late. It was 1:05 when class started. There was a class at 9:05 that I usually went to but I thought I would sit at this one. It was the second floor of Mechanic Arts. There was confusion about which elevator and which stairs. I wasn't sure which room my class was in so I just guessed. It was a nice social science classroom with a lot of books and cozy chairs, like a corner of a living room with a kitchen island. I took a seat in front of some ladies. They had thier feet on the chair and I had to move it. I started to try to find my noteook. My usual notebook is always full (this is not the first time this has happened) but this time I had some loose leaf pages with me and I was thinking that I would just have to figure out how to keep them together.

I was working on a sensors web application. Gayatri was the product manager and Adam Raybin was working on the hardware. I realized that I didn't know enough about the hardware side of it and that we weren't integrating enough. It was Adam's living room. He had a place right on the lake. The tide came up and down and some people were playing on the stairs where the water was filling in. One lady with a 3 string acoustic base waded back onto shore. I started to leave and was trying to find my shoes. It was after dark already and I had to take the bus. Brad Skillicorn was there and wondering if anyone could give him a ride because he had to go to the next state. There was a bunch of food lying around and I was wondering if I should eat any of it.

I was working on a web interface for sensors.

Sun 22 Nov

In John Banks basement. I knew the way through and it was more clear this time. I went through the locked door and grabbed a piece of wood that might have brought back memories. I was going to put it at the front door to freak them out but I was seen.

Escaping through the window. They were coming to get me

Mon 23 Nov

Getting the car out from between 2 parked cars on the ice north of University Avenue. That was easy because I could just slide it but it was so hard to find the brake and so hard to stop. There was a black lady in front of me who kept challenging me to stop as I went through industrial areas filled with rail crossings.

Thanksgiving

In a church. Thinking about wearing a 93 necklace. Wandering around. Finally sitting down. A pause in the sermon. We started chatting with the kid sitting next to us who was complaining about not being able to get free information from his university. First in a whisper and then in a normal voice. I said all that stuff should be free. He said but he is in the navy college. I said that was different. we got up and went to a table in the back. He was very friendly, touching. His father came over to talk to us. There was an unopened boardgame on the table that had information about his hometown on it. Pittsburg. The back was upside down from the front.

Black Friday

Music gathering in Dhann Poulnau's upper attic. Only one person came, a lady who brought a drum. John Banks was there. He said that everone wants to be the class president. I said there was only one class president but I thought he liked many subcommittes. I thought John could play keys and me woodwinds and her percussion. But of course I couldn't get any of the woodwinds to work properly – they all had too many holes in them. The girl gave us a cassette tape of her work and we played it. It was labelled 'Hardware First'.

Then she started in on a tirade about how someone had cheated her. While flashing a bunch of monopoly money around on the table. I complained that I couldn't understand what her complaint was. So she turned invisible and left. I could just barely see her outline ripple as she passed.

Grey Saturday 28 Nov MMXX

At the state fair. There was a guy with a tee shirt and a list of names of drugs on it. Was that what he had taken? No, that was what he was selling. Oh, really must get some of that some time. Later.

Trying to go to the bathroom in the dormatory. I thought the bathroom was empty but the corner stall was occupied. Then it turned out 1/3-1/2 was full. I finally couldn't do it.

Waiting to drive off in the car. I was going to leave the house and I had no place to go but was going to live in the car. I was trying to pack everything into the 'basement' of the car and the top. My mother was on the phone and I had to say goodbye because otherwise I wouldn't have had enough time to pack. I thought maybe I could just keep some of my stuff in storage where it already was. I knew the place where it was kept, it was the last door on the left and then through all the stacks of books.

After sleeping a night in the car I was in a european city and I was thinking that we should publish all economic transactions so that the global price of everything was known. The free market reaching its ultimate efficiency and everything being at its fair price would be the closest thing to not having currency that you could get while still having currency and would make the next step – the removal of currency – immanent.

Beige Sunday

Constantly worried about not having any money or any job. Was thinking I could borrow from John Banks but he reminded me that I already owed him 2 days pay. Riding down a highway a pengiun flew out of a truck and was caught on the hood of the lady driving behind. From her dashcam you could see her slowing down to give the penguin a perfect soft landing. Was there a parade of children behind? Yes!

How do you do it? I go to camps and I get the kids kicked out of the camps. They don't know it. Then we tell them they are being punished but they all end up here at this uber building fun camp. And its time for the big end demo.

With Pablo in a shopping mall. He went into a store and bought a rare book for > 200 USD because he wanted to show me one picture from it. I'm thinking like 'where do these people get their money'? Then we sit down in the park and he drops something into a hole and nearly hits the lady who is down there in the basement cellar.

Cyber Monday

Hacking a microsoft Application

They were trying to get the customer ID and code for a microsoft app. They had it on a TV in the upstairs bedroom of 1377 and were on the phone to several friends to try to figure it out. I put everything on mute. It wouldn't go on mute so we had to disconnect. I explained that Leila had set me up to be a microsoft reseller, so I was the one who technically sold the app. Leila had signed me up for that. Dennis looked at Leila askance. If it appeared in the list mis-allocated it would trace back to me so they needed to stop trying to hack into it.

Mining Sprint

In a large hall; was it a church or was it a field; there were a few of us and we were planning an application. Easier for me if it was mostly UI. We outlined it and I said some words about quality. Just mom and apple pie, right? But they started to rankle at that point. One of the team expressed concern that we wouldn't make the deadline. So I scheduled a meeting to go over the schedule. It turned out to be similar to a sprint planning meeting where we would divide the stories into tasks and estimate each task. I tried to write on the blackboard but it was low quality chalk and everything was blurry. I wasn't even sure if it was my own handwriting.

In the lunchroom with Gayatri she was explaining how she got this project. They had originally given it to a transport company who couldn't do it, then another company. So now it was a great chance for us.

3 Dec MMXX – my birthday

Was in Lake Crystal. They were building a new garage on the house next to ours. There was a dirt alley in back that curved around. What would happen when we inherited the house. We went to the edge of town. We were informed that they didn't like strangers. For evidence we were told to push the walk button on the street light. An indian lady who was crossing the street pointed us to it eagerly. The street lights came alive in some kind of comic robot effect and pretended that it was looking at us and saying that we looked funny. We then had to look into its eyes and it wouldn't let us cross until we did. It displayed pictures of the Beatles and you had to pretend to look into thier eyes. One of our party wouldn't do so but it let us accross anyway eventually.

In a modern concrete room in the mountains with Gayatri. She pointed excitedly out the narrow low horizontal window at a peculiarly colored duck that was flying by. Then the duck flew in through the window and we admired it amusedly while it was trying to fly back out again.

Sat 5 Dec MMXX

In a restaurant in a shopping center. Sitting down to eat with some strangers. Will covid get better? Yes, by next year it will all be over. But look out for the next pandemic after that. Oy weh.

Got up to get some water. Wasn't sure whether the water was cold or hot, sparkling or still. Couldn't find my seat on the way back. They had left. Everyone was leaving and the restaurant was closing for the afternoon.

I noticed the sky; it was made of foam. The foam started to come down and I clawed my way through it. Then above it was in the form of a waterfall and I was taken by the water fall down, unimaginably far down. Eventually it landed near the s-curve and I was back to the place I started.

In Norma Banks' house except the ground floor wasn't just nice; it was museum-like.

Mon 7 Dec MMXX

In an elevator trying to get to the 4th floor. The elevator only went to the 3rd floor and then you had to go a circuitous and sneaky route to get there as Dr. Who was explaining. We didn't have our badges even though we had a right to be there and so were waiting for someone to let us in or go to the receptionist to get a temporary badge.

Wed 9 Dec MMXX

On my way back from vacation. I was going to check out my old place of work, Zycad, even though I still had my job at TK. It was going to take me a long time to get home from the airport and then there, and I didn't know how I was going to explain to my other work.

With a bus of school childern going to a science museum. They had escalators timed to the extingtion of species. The presentation was beneath me and I didn't know how I was going to spend the rest of the time. I thought about going back home but I couldn't find my backpack or remember the group I was with. I was supposed to share my badge with some who had come on the bus but I didn't know who they were.

Mon 14 Dec MMXX

Getting divorced from Sally again. Wondering how I fooled into marrying her again and why I was leaving her to marry Ruth.

In a forested area. The markets were substituting inferior meat.

Going to the train. I couldn't find my ticket in my backback even though I just had it.

Wed 16 Dec MMXX

Driving home from [Lake Crystal]. The car in front of us started to swerve wildly in the wind even though it was a clear day. Then we did as we came to the same point. There was no explanation for it except nuclear blast. Then the blast hit us and pushed us way to a northern suburb with the cyborg conspiracy.

Th 17 Dec MMXX

In a theme park waiting for the mini-golf to open. Long lines.

18 Dec MMXX

Library. You couldn't come back in if you left. I went to go to the bathroom, and then remembered that there were bathrooms inside, so the lady at the counter let me back in. Doing some work for spock=ulrich. I was going to do it on paper but then realized that it could be done on two spreadsheets. It was a project calculation. Sat 6 Mar MMXXI

Sitting at a swimming pool. The angle was very steep. A kid asked me where sitting and standing heights were. He could only go sitting height because of some illness. I showed him. And you see cars parked on the street that aren't actually used by anyone but you never see the busses parked so you think there are more cars than busses. Started counting the people going by on the buses and realized that everytime you see a bus go by you need to assume that it is a full block of traffic. Got on the bus and had a seat of my own. I was continuing to listen to the songs from before on a walkman. It was supposed to be the band Yes but they had a slight reggae sound and were doing covers.

A bus passed us and left many people off at the corner of Grand & Dale, Then when we stopped there many people got on. I moved my backpack onto my lap in case someone wanted to sit there but no one did. I was about the only empty seat in the bus.

Then we all had to get off and we were taking grocery carts through a small convenience store in a shopping mall because it was lunch time. I had a lot of toilet paper in my shopping cart that I had gotten from other places. I had gotten friends to pay the store for them so I didn't owe the store but I still owed the friends. I was wondering how this store was going to keep them apart. I organized them in the shopping cart. Moving all the loose toilet paper rolls over to one side. Some mis matched bottles of coke and some other stuff.

I let everyone else go in front of me because they were all on lunch break and had to get back but I wasn't. There was quite a line and we were hardly moving.

Mon 12 April MMXXI

I went into one of the rooms to grab a vase. Then I thought that was a silly idea.

Th 15 Apr

Family vacation with smoking driver

It was northern Minnesota, near Duluth. There was some snow coming and we weren't supposed to be travelling but we were. We were in a large van. A family in front of us had a small car. Their kid lost a stuffed animal in the snow and I went to pick it up for them.

We got in a van with all our suitcases. I was crushed up right behind the driver. He had a lit cigarette. Finally I couldn't take it any more and told him to put it out. How can you have that thing inside the car? When he didn't, I started to hold my hands over his mouth. How do you like not being able to breathe? This caused him to veer all over the road, crashing through fences and nearly running a worker over. When the van finally stopped, I got out, said I just want my stuff, took my suitcase and backpack and started to walk northwest into the forest. Sat 17 Apr

Changing the Wiring in the Basement

We had to change the wiring in the basement so that we could have new lights. We had re-wired the basement before and there were detailed instructions involving 2 long plastic bags of green wiring and various clamps and screws. These had to be connected to the right places in various locations in the L shaped basement. We got a whole bunch of people to help us. I started to open up the bags, read the instructions and get the equipment sorted out and prepare the locations. We had done it before so we should be able to do it again. It was confusing where everything was and what order things should be done in.

Suddenly I realized that all this wiring was for the other end, betwen the outlet and the fuse. Just to put new lights in was wiring up to the outlet. So we didn't have to do any of that. Emergency over.

I was standing in a room off the main area of the basement. There was a big workbench there like a hut. We had invited the whole public to come in and see the work. A couple came by. The guy was really big. Football player type. He mumbled something I couldn't understand. I asked him again. Still couldn't understand. Again. "I'll have a bud light. Might as well while waiting for this thing to start." I had to explain to him that we didn't serve refreshments. "Well maybe you should." He walked away and I wondered why we had invited the public as if it was a convention.

Dog Food $59/lb

I went over to the far corner of the L shaped basement where it was more like a fair and a stand was selling tea and buscuits. They were also selling dog food. Well not really; their branding was that they were the dog food farm and they were here for a demo of their product but they were selling tea. She showed me the chart on the wall in the back room. $59/lb.

Mediaeval Courtyard

I had to go to the bathroom and there was a mediaval courtyard where all the privies were. They were segregated by country, so I had to go into the one for Americans, not the one for French. There were two for americans – one for regular americans and one for those who dribbled when they urinated. I was happy to get the one for those who dribbled even though they both had seats and not urinals. I had earlier been able to go into the one in the corner but now it had a sign on it 'For Holy People Only' and when I started to go there the floorboards tripped me up so I didn't go in.

Then my friends came. It was a D&D game. They were planning an ambush. Two of them were chasing 9 cavalry and a wizard or two. The rest were after the 30 or so infantry in a different location. They were planning to force them all together at a point. As a prince in the story, I felt a premonition that I would die in the battle. I was very excited about this and started to prepare.

Sun 18 Apr MMXXI

The 999 Chip

I was in a basic office room. They were explaining that the new chip that the hardware team was going to use because of obsolescence of the old chip was not compatable with our software. You had to add in a bunch of peripheral chips and the special software for those.

I went into the meeting room ready to explain this. But then they explained that the chip manufacturer had guaranteed forward compatability – it was with the 999 chip which was a little more expensive, but that would be acceptable.

Exclusive Chapter Book

You couldn't be in two different chapters of the book. So if you wanted to get away with something that you had done in one chapter all you had to do was write yourself into the other chapter and then you couldn't have done it in the first chapter.

Combining Telematics Offerings

Illustrating combining of telematics offerings was done with a band of ribbons cut zig zag on the ends like paint samples. You would select the options that you wanted and match them up along the zig zag.

Stockinged Winter Park Walk

Gayatri & I got ready for a walk through the snow in the park. We were wearing open toed sandals but with a couple layers of winter socks. There was a concern that the socks would get wet.

Long Meeting

We were all in a large auditorium listening to the meeting. It went on for a long time.

Ice Tea Recipe

He led the ice tea out on a trolley and I followed past a hallway into a department store area. I snuck behind some piles of boxes to try to observe him.

Work

We were sitting in a library. One of us was a lawyer and was explaining that they had 365 days of vacation remaining. Then they were going to resign. But there was one meeting in the middle of her next year of vacation that her company insisted that she attend. And it was in the middle of the night her time. I said that was funny. You could just call in and say you don't know why you are there and be done.

She explained that her company had lots of rigourous rules. Like you had to use a certain kind of eraser. I asked if that met six sigma. The younger lady sitting accross the table said that it did not. I was pleased with myself for giving her a victory in the conversation. I said that according to six sigma if you wanted to prescribe something you should require the result not the method. So in this case, you should say that you wanted documents to be erased completely. Not dictate the tool used for that. Then the employees would have the freedom to find a better solution.

We were concerned about the upcoming vote. It would, again, center on facilities upkeep. The area that we were in was actually very nice and modern but half the company still had to deal with the old building which was run down and leaked. I thought that the problem would be solved if we could just set up cubiles in the factory space but that was against union regulations.

Rock & Roll

I got tired of sitting at the table in the library and decided that the best thing to do was to go into work and work on the long calculation I was doing. This wasn't a thing that really needed to be done, it was kind of a background task, but it was one that was interesting from a technical perspective (irl: the mks port).

To get into work was a video game. It was one I had played before and I was quite good at it. But it was a new version of the game, so I had to start over as level one.

I still had my rock/brute-force power so I was able to get through the door that previously had been open but which was now too small for me by battering it repeatedly. It changed form each time as video games do. All clown-like animated faces in unrealistic imaginary colors.

Once I got in I needed to get up to the appropriate floor. There were rail lines running everywhere and people walking around like proper British gentlemen. With hat and umbrella. Now you had to pay to use the line and there was no way I could do that. But I still had my roll/wheel power so I was able to travel the lines myself, even uphill or upside down. I worried about how I was going to get out on the other side without being able to prove that I had paid.

When I finally got in to the office, I had to manoeuvre my trolly with my computer past the cleaning lady and then through the portal into the work area.

Fri 18 June

Driving

I was driving a car. It was old and I wasn't sure how much gas it had left, but it was my car and I was driving it. Old country roads. There was snow on them. I told her that all the big cities like New York or San Francisco had the same thing where you would have to go from above to below. That seemed to placate her.

The road, which was dusty with snow, went up the highway bridge over the train tracks. It then devolved into twisting forest paths. The car was the same but it was a bicycle or walking.

Dinner and Dan Smith

We were at a large dinner, white tablecloths set over row tables with benches. Each of the moms had 2 circular slabs of putty on thier collar, which they could take off. They said that you would feel like you were spinning around and around and the whole world was spinning around and around. I said, "Ah, so they are hallucinogens." Trying to sound knowlegable. I don't know if it worked. Nor am I sure that being knowlegable about hallucinogens is a quality you want to broadcast.

Dan Smith was there and he asked why I wasn't happy. He was quite adamant about it, almost angry. I had good food, a wonderful lifestyle. Just look at this banquet we were sitting at. How could I explain to him that I had no money, no place to live of my own, was failing in school, didn't know where my next meal would come from or where my next place to sleep would be?

Moving

We were at Leo Abbott's, or perhaps it was Paul Abbott's. We had been staying there and we were going to be leaving, taking our suitcases to our own place. New video game rules

You have a strength point, and front, back, up, down, etc. points, going two or more out. The closer number always has to be greater than the further number. The central item is defence. The first in front is a normal attack. The second is a special attack. Up one would be ability to jump; up two would be ability to fly. And so on.

Fri 2 July

The bouncer

The establishment was an all you can eat. It was run by the Japanese Mafia. You had to pay the entrance each day. It was about $90. They were very nice to you once you had proven that you had paid the fee. It was very important to them and they made a big point of it.

The first day I paid and left something there. So my father paid for me to go back the second day. Everyone was so nice and made me feel like I belonged there, once they had seen my ticket valid for the day. The boss would come by and he would enforce the fact that you were their guest – if you had paid for the day. He was very Japanese mafioso.

So when on the third day I remembered that I had left a mess, I went back to clean it up, because I felt like I was on the inside. As I did, I saw some nice things like pails of frosting and started to pick them up to take with me. That certainly would have been accepted when I was a member.

The waitress stopped me when she saw me carrying these things to confirm that I had a ticket. It was OK as long as I had the ticket. But I had gotten wet, could the ticket in my back pocket have become damaged? Because of course I had the ticket, right?

At first I said that I did, hoping they would leave me alone. But then I decided that I couldn't keep up the pretense. So I explained to them that I had just wanted to clean up the things from yesterday. The waitress, who had been so friendly suddenly turned cold and explained that she couldn't be friends with someone who wasn't up front about things.

Her and one of the other helpers guided me down the stairs while I tried to apologize for my mistake. I wanted to know if there was any way that I could bribe them to let me go. They didn't respond to the offer.

At the bottom of the spiral staircase were the doors to the outside. It was a beautiful bright clear sunny day outside, you could see through the glass doors. I saw the boss leaving by the door. He eyed me knowingly but said nothing. They let me to a door to the right of the main door and left me. But it was too small to get through. I would have to try to get out the main door.

And there, sitting on the steps blocking most of the doorway, was the bouncer. He looked at me and I could see that there was no pity in his eyes.

No you cant go home

Well I finished my work. I picked up an umbrella that someone had left lying on the floor in the lobby. It was slightly damaged but still servicable. I thought about what I would do next. I realized that if I walked a little ways east, I could catch the #4 bus home on Snelling.

As soon as I made up my mind to do that, the entire lobby lifted up, spun into the air and went twisting off to somewhere unknown.

Saturday 24 Jul XXI

In a hallway which was a bedroom with a girl. She had two children. I was looking through some of her old photographs and there was a cute animal. To flirt with her I said that now I knew what I wanted to come back as. She came over and sat next to me but wasn't ready to kiss.

I was at work. We were detectives and we were in a long hallway sloping downwards with old machines. Someone came in with a problem. The Japanese were producing a new device that didn't require the auxilliary chip. It turned out that it was at a premium so there was no problem, you either got the premium version or the normal with the auxilliary chip. Standard decision.

I didn't know what to do with the rest of the day so I went to the corridors to have fun. I was gliding on a raft. I had to break through the doors and push away furniture because they no longer supported this. That one guy from TK was there and he was surprised to see me go into the corridors. I went to where they were storing the food. It was the guards last day and he said he was going to report me. I recommended that they store all the milk products together.

We had to fight the jabberwok. This involved going into the underworld. I was armed with a magic spell and Gilgamesh was there to raise the armies of the stone soldiers. But by the time we got to the jabberwok these were all used up so I had to use the one ring and a sword.

When I came back from the underworld the girl was there and I complained to her that I had won the battle but lost the war because I had had to use the one ring and violence and that had woken up the master. I had also lost her love. Two wars.

Sunday 25 Jul

That one girl from high school was mad at me because I was late to meet her. She said I wasn't even answering her phone calls. I couldn't get my phone to work properly.

We had to smuggle secret stuff past the guards. I had carefully prepared all the documents and hidden them as well as I could. This was in an apartment like Dennis' in Arden Hills with a secret agent type lady.

We were doing war games and poring paint over each other inside a department store. Finally I snuck behind their lines and smeared paint everywhere. I don't think they were taking it as seriously as I was.

Monday 26 Jul

In a basement. That one magician. He did an act with staves. He would spin them so fast it would look like he was walking. And then he looked like an alien carrying another alien on its back; all wooden skin. Then he lay down like Dali's persistance of memory.

Dimensional weaknesses. People were coming from one dimension to another in a movie theater sized box of light. This was in the Highland Sr. High area.

Sat 31 Jul

In a basement. Hiding. Went out and it was raining. There were cardboard buildings set up to be like the UK. I went inside. No one was there. It was an auditorium. The stage was set up like a living room. I sat down as if I was going to play the cello. I started poking around to see if they had left anything but everything abandoned was useless. I went downstairs and it was like a children's room with big fabric covered books of Blue's Clues and the like.

Sun 1 Aug

1377

Cleaning the bedroom at 1377. There was a lot of clothes piled up and I was moving them around. They were hard to organize. There was a thing that cleaned and it looked like an elephant. You had to put soap in it but the soap was chocolate powder. You had to blow in its tail to power it.

I went down into the basement and lit up a joint. I lit a q-tip with a match and then lit the joint. The flame spread almost an inch down the side. I felt high in the dream for a brief moment.

Watlow

Brad Skillicorn was driving me. I thought he was going to drop me off at TK but he stopped at Waltow. Then I realized that I couldn't get to TK because I didn't have a car so I was stuck there for the rest of the day until he drove me home. I sat in the first meeting; we were sitting on benches and tables like it was Open School. I couldn't remember the details of the projects that I was working on. I said that I had to go to a meeting for a different project, but even that was one that we were working with them on.

I needed some paper. I borrowed the lady's notebook next to me but she drooled on the page. There were no other pages blank so I gave it back to her and went to the office to get some blank paper from the copy machine. As I was opening up the copy machine to get the paper, someone came in and said that there was recycled paper. He went to get the box of recycled paper and took some. So I went through that until I found something suitable. I went and sat at a small desk in a corner of a hallway and tried to organize the papers. It was very bright.

Street Food

I was in the middle of a street food fair and I was worried that I had peed myself in the night so I started taking off all my clothes and flying away. I grabbed Gayatri as I started to fly away but she kept struggling and so that brought me down.

Mon 2 Aug

I had a Math class to teach, 1 hour, Tuesday at 1:00. I went for the first day, I was ready for the first day at least. I had trouble parking my bike but I still got to class just in time.

As I was walking to the class, the boss commented on how close to late I was. Then asked if I was ready for the 8 hour class. I didn't realize it was 8 hours. I thought it was only 1 hour.

When I got there, it wasn't a math class it was a physics class and Mike Turnure, who I knew knew more physics than me was in the class. So I had to treat it like a seminar. I wanted to investigate the theory that compressing helium made it conducting and that bubbles of helium in the upper atmosphere were what caused lightning.

Wed 4 Aug

We were making food in a big marketplace/cafeteria. We had a big black cast iron cauldron and my mother and I were making tapioca in it. We were debating about putting more tapioca vs. more water. We thought we had way too much because we thought that the cauldron was full. But I discovered that actually all the tapioca had floated to a thin layer on the top and the rest was just water. So really there was just barely enough for the two of us.

Dan Smith had a sophisticated game/CD/DVD player and he left us to look after it for a minute. But I had to walk away and I was afraid that someone would take it. It was also a vape device. I decided that was too personal so I didn't use it.

Thurs 5 Aug

Driving home. Through country roads. At first I was just going to sit at the crossroads but the sun was setting at 8:00 so I decided to go home. It was a game where you had to avoid the pedestrians and I wasn't doing so well. Including going up on a dirt road on the side of a hill.

We were waiting for class to end and then we were going to go home. There were four classes. It was in a modern, multi-level building, with wide open spaces and domed ceilings, adjacent a shopping mall.

Gayatri left before I did so I decided to sit in on a class. The subject was whether you could unintentionally flirt. I said that you couldn't because any interaction would immediately be understood as flirting. Saying this to the girl I was flirting with.

It was way after close of buisiness in the shopping mall. I saw Bob Rajala walking away, having worked late. I went to take a shower in a convenience store amongst the candy. I dried off partially and put my same clothes back on, slightly damp.

I walked accross the street near the library in Blooomington. Mariela asked me if we could work on Saturday. I said we could but that I would check, meaning that we had been authorized to do so in the past and may be again.

Sun 8 Aug

It was the Tuesday after a long weekend. I had two meetings, one at 9:00-11:00 and one at 9:30-10:00, both with priests. I was going to go to the 9:00 one and then the 9:30 and then come back to the 9:00 one. The 9:30 one had been scheduled before the other – by Ajith. I was sitting in my office, which was a cube on a road in a forest, trying to be sure I knew which meeting rooms I was in for the day when Dave Banks came in and asked if we could talk a little before the 3 day meeting on WBS. I explained that WBS was just a list of tasks.

I had to go to a shower in the basement of Open School 1885. Someone got me dressed in green velvet pajamas. I looked for my underwear in a drawer but was out. This was the second time this had happened. I decided to go commando. I thought I knew the way to the showers but everything was different. Some younger kids were telling me it was one level down but I thought I knew better. I went where I thought it was. There were rows of bicycles. I turned back before the turnstiles at the exit. I was worried about how much time I was spending just running up and down. There were incredibly large people exercising to music to my left and they were sweating profusely.

Wed 11 Aug

Tube to the sky

NASA had an exhibit where you could walk up a staircase, into a spaceship and along a cooridor to a different star and then back again all in a couple hours. I was asking them how they made the tube that comprised the space elevator. They explained that although the distance of multiple light-years was too great to be done linearly, by wrapping the tube up in a coil and then connecting the pieces of the coil it could be made in parallel. I tried to understand the math behind it because it didn't seem to work – the supplier of the coil would have to make it linearly anyway – but eventually gave up as the NASA guide was obviously convinced that it did work out.

Sally's Kitchen

Sally had started a restaurant and the items on the menu were all obvious passive agressive digs at a hypothetical ex-husband. We just sat there not really looking at each other and didn't have a lot to say.

Sax Reunited

My father was driving me in a semi to a house like the Sheer's. It was down to its foundation. Over stones and a bumpy road he got it parked in the narrow driveway. I wondered if he would be able to back it out after they had put the house back up. A lady was there and explained that they could take away the corner of the house or the semi could try to go forward up the hill to get out.

We went inside. They had recently combined the house with the adjacent trailer home. I asked, jokingly, how the merger of North and South Korea was going. They didn't seem to think it was funny. I went in the other room where a cat had just had babies and was feeding its kittens. It was kept in a big glass aquarium along with another cat who was sick and needed the humidity kept high.

The Hunchback

I went out in the street. It was a long straight road in the night. Red lights with numbers came flashing down the street very fast, showing how little time we had left. Like ambulances flashing red lights but like informational signs used by road crews. I fast forwarded to see when it got to zero. It went on a lot longer than expected and then there was nothing. Then after a long time with nothing, a single motorcycle came by. I backtracked to find out what the lone motorcyclist was. I zoomed in on him and he was a question mark, and alien. He was a sick and deformed sperm. At that point I awoke as from a nightmare.

Th 12 Aug

In an apartment on the street with Gayatri. Had to triple-lock the door. Someone on the TV was doing some anti-war illuminati thing and I thought it was really cool. Really fine detail in the border with lots of whitespace. Trying to go to the bathroom when two ladies came in and they wouldn't let me alone. I wanted to finish reading my phone. It turned out she had to go really bad and wouldn't leave. I got off the toilet but my clothes got stuck and we ended up ripping the seat off. We could fix it though and I left them to it.

I needed to get to a major airport. I was on the tube and I took the wrong route. I started to get off but someone was in my way so the train left before I could get out the door. I sat down next to the door and waited for the next stop but the train went past several stops. I was getting farther away from where I needed to be even to turn around to get to my next destination. Other people came and sat near me waiting to get off. By the time it finally stopped we were in a semi rural location.

Sat 14 Aug

Was going to the store. The checkout counter was down the stairs in a library. They were selling weed legally now. You had to ask and then go pick it up. Because you rolled in it so that it got on your clothes. I didn't ask first and so the ladies at the checkout counter were wondering what weight I had on my clothes. But then Clayton was there and he helped me pick out some buds and flowers. I had just had stems before. He didn't have a lot left. The stems were there to protect the buds during the winter and he was worried about the coming winter.

April 26th 1992 by Sublime had a different part in the middle where he recounted all the different drugs he had taken. "I've got so much chlorine in my veins that every time I flush the toilet it gets clean." Something like that. And a metaphor for herion.

I had a video interview for an internship. I was physically there but they could only see me through a TV screen. I did well with the team but the main boss fixated on the way I left Johnson and I looked nervous in the video. I had to move the camera all around and it was pointing at me then not pointing at me then pointing at me again.

After the call ended I was able to go behind them and listen in on their converstaion. Because I was in cyber space and they were in regular space. They were angling toward a younger candidate, more recently out of college. It was an internship after all and in retrospect I wondered why the talent agent had sent me for this interview. I put a good face on it saying I wasn't so unhappy that they didn't like me if the reason was that they were going for someone fresh out of college.

Sun 15 Aug

I was walking up a hill and around a path. There were a lot of soldiers camped out there. I thought boy I wouldn't want to be like that with no life of the mind. It was cold and I was overdressed. But I didn't care because now I was comfortable and it was actually quite pleasant to walk out in cold. A black gentleman carrying his young son came past me the other direction on the path. He was overdressed for the cold as well and that also made me feel better even though he had the excuse that he was protecting his child.

As I went along the path behind where the soldiers were camped, I saw that far from engaged in mindless pursuits, the soldiers were all looking at maps of the earth and sky, studying geography and astronomy. Many had pictures of the stars of the southern hemisphere, upside down.

I thought this was great, and would be a great way to teach people, if there was this shared interest in reviewing maps. Just put information as infographics in maps.

I walked further along the path and came to the top of a tall hill. I was struck with the beauty of the scene even though it was just ordinary trees it was almost impressionist. I decided to take a picture but was then having trouble with the camera. There were four settings on the camera and then an empty area. I kept putting my fingers on the lens. The sight was not the same as the lens. It got stuck in zoom mode and I zoomed in on the temperature dial on a stove from somewhere.

At the bottom of the hill was school. I was teaching but it was more like I was trying to recruit for my seminar. There were a number of students in a class – someone elses class – and I was trying to think of activities for them afterwards. I thought of having them all make bulky clothing and stage a mock battle. One student came by with and interest in reindeer milk. We got in a discussion about how much of the reindeer was eventually used. This discussion happend in a hallway. We went back to the reception, which had a large glass window in front and couches, in front of trophy displays and the entrance to the auditorium.

I was trying to look at my schedule. I was always rushing even though I didn't have a clear idea of what I was doing. Or maybe because I didn't have a clear idea of what I should be doing. A young girl was helping me, one of the students. I looked at the schedule, Tuesday & Thursday afternoons. After the real class that the other person was teaching. the students might come to mine. I had two separate hours on those afternoons pencilled in for different things. Then a two hour class that I had forgotten what it was. I had a list of all the students and was going to try to write down the different project that each of them was going to do.

Mon 16 Aug

"I don't need to know what makes a woman love a man I don't need to have money to know what I don't have"

– So sang the singer and all his fans were in awe of how melancholy it was.

I was on top of the stadium trying to fix some mechanical part. It had a phillips screw on top and a flat screw on the bottom. It turned out the bottom part was the one that I needed to adjust. I had the right size for the phillips but the flat was oversized. I had to insert the screwdriver into a little plastic tube that bent away from the metal device.

I was on the train going south, away from work. I wasn't planning on going to school. It was Wednesday and I hadn't been to class on other Wednesdays so I thought it best not to complicate things. It takes so much time to get the the university and back and it would interfere with my schedule for other things. I thought about how this was a train of giving up and running away for me but others used it for a regular communte. The train was expensive and not much used. Thirty Euros. It went down by 35W. I went one stop to far and determined to get off at the next stop.

I followed the other people off the train and onto the bus without realizing it. It was the number 10 bus going towards downtown between Cleaveland and Snelling. Other passengers were talking with the driver about what number it was. Because it used to be called the 10 but now it was called the 4.

I got home to 1377 and went into my room which was very messy. There was an old woman there who I hugged. There was some concern over whether I still had a girlfriend or not and if I should flirt with her.

My mom came in with a big bowl of mashed potatoes with lots of butter. I said I didn't want them because potatoes weren't really my thing. Brighteyes was standing in the open back door. There was a tub of plain vanilla ice cream on the floor but I didn't want that either. I had a couple of power bar in my backpack which I really wanted but I was saving them. There was some Ethiopian bread on the shelf but the back had been left open and it had gone bad. There was another burger there with it and I took a bite but had to spit it out because it was next to the Ethiopian bread that had gone bad and so was probably contaminated as well. There was then a bunch of spinach etc. that I had spit out in the trash.

I turned on the old black and white television.

Tue 17 Aug

Sitting at a table in the corner of a library. We were there with Peter and Brad Skillicorn. We were talking about Peters work. We spent the whole day there, eating and leaving a mess on the table. At the end as we were getting up I asked if we were going to talk about my project. I couldn't even remember the name of it.

We were going to a chinese restaurant with .. from Watlow. The other got wine and I got beer. The glasses they had were small and from a cafeteria machine like you would get milk from. We went and sat down at a table. It was cramped. Someone bumped the table and most of the beer bubbled away. I didn't care and figured I just wouldn't drink it anyway.

Fri 20 Aug <lindos>

I went to work even though I had been let go. I was talking to people but not letting on that I was no longer there. I was wondering about how to clean things up. Finally I realized that I had nothing to do and that I might as well leave. This place was like the florists on Snelling near St. Clair.

I was trying to clean up my work. It was like a refrigerator with a cable connecting the computer to the top. I had a lot of stuff that I rearranged. Bottles that were intended to be use cases. I thought I needed to git rid of a lot of it. A lot of it I had pirated. As I was cleaning up and rearranging, the computer started complaining about power and network problems. It didn't turn on except in degraded mode. As I was trying to fix it they said that since you wouldn't be coming back there was no point. The refigerator was in a place like Thermo King that was in a place like a department store.

As I was leaving I had to get accross a highway that was under water. Some others were coming with me. They kept telling me to wait until the cars had gone by. Finally I went. There was one car that was coming and I made it before it came. But when I went, I pulled the earth of the side of the highway behind me and the car had to slow down for that before it went back. This was the northeast side of the interesction of 35 and Snelling, leaving from a department store that was Rosedale.

Sat 21 Aug

I was working at my desk, which was a long bench which was in TK which was in the basement of 1377. I got interested in looking at a fuzzy speck. I wasn't sure if that was part of my job or not but I figured I was going to do it. The workstation to my right had a professional microscope and no one was using it so I went to use that one. In my login, I had been configuring the operating system, so some things were hard to access, like the web browser didn't have a border so it was hard to move around. I thought about cleaning the system and resetting it but I couldn't because it was also used for the microscope workstation by others. I thought it strange that my main machine was also being used by others and that that was why I had started using the lesser machine to the left.

In open school (Linwood), everyone was singing "Friends of 'P'" – except it was a Metallica version. Someone in the hall asked me if I could call them on the phone to check if their phone was working. They expected I knew their name because I was their friend but I didn't so I asked for the number. He gave the 4 digit number to me. Not really sure if he was testing the phone or testing to see if I remembered his name. If so I failed. I got distracted and when I finally got around to finding a phone – in a classroom under a table – and started to call him, he came in to explain that he had already fixed his phone. There was some discussion over who was the 'P' that everyone was so excited about and the implication was that it was me!

At school I crawled into the air ducts. Previously the way had been blocked but workmen had come in and opened it up. I thought that it was going to be greatly to my advantage when I got to the spirit world that I had spent so much time practicing in these places. I thought that I would be able to fly, but I could only proceed at a normal pace.

Sun 22 Aug

I went to Chrissie's house, which was Dan Smiths place on Randolph. She was having problems with her husband and I ended up staying the night and making love. I was walking back home through the alley behind 1377 and worrying about how I was going to explain to my wife. I decided that I couldn't outright lie but I would try to prevaricate.

Mon 23 Aug

A film was being made. It was a very complicated film and the actors were reharsing the precise order in which they were crossing the street. One was crossing Snelling at St. Clair on the north side and the other was crossing St. Clair at Snelling on the west side. This was complicated by the fact that you had to account for the other pedestrians, who were public, not extras. The actors were in the green room discussing the whole operation.

The director was trying to get a special actor from India. The mentor of the actor was a veteran singer. The student of the singer was an actor who was playing in a new movie about a kid who tapes himself on his home equipment and becomes a star. The music was such that it was taped over so many times that it became a sort of drone in the background. I felt a great envy because that was something I wanted to do and it seemed grossly unfair that I never had decent enough equipment to do so properly.

The next scene was where the doctor was in the surgery. His friend was the lawer. The doctor bungles the surgery and the director informs him that he is dismissed. He goes into her office and murders her with a knife very graphically. The sequel is how the lawer helps to get him out of prison after being convicted.

We are in the upstairs bedroom of 1377 thinking about the sequel. I am trying to sneak to the bathroom but there are people coming in and out, flirting with me homosexually. I go back and sit down on my bed. Everyone comes in and starts to try to figure out the dialog for the sequel that we are working on. They get wrapped around the axle debating different lines. I put down a rule that if they can't agree, everyone will write down their idea and then we will pick the best one. I am wondering to myself how that differs from what is already going on except for the extra step of making everybody write it down. Yet they agree to it. They put a time limit of 10 minutes on it. I say 9 minutes to emphasize the time sensitive nature of it all.

I am trying to find paper to write on. I find some old computer printout paper and wonder if I was saving it as a memento and therefore shouldn't use it. It didn't have enough room on it so I tried to find something else. I tried to write with a carbon pen on some old cast iron pans that were stacked up but someone else already had; mostly a list of names. When you touched the pan with the carbon pen a bunch of the carbon would ball up, held together electrostatically. This eventually turned into a little mouse shape that would run accross the pan. The person next to me did this and then I did it and the two mice started playing and chasing each other.

The way the lawyer was going to get the doctor off depended on falsifying some evidence around the timeing of events. This meant having a car's emmissions testing redone with a different result. The lawer was driving and I was in the back seat. We went up a big bridge to the emmissions testing station. The lawer started to ride up against the righthand fence. This had something to do with the way he was going to fake the emissions test. Then we broke past the fence, off the bridge, and went flying onto another bridge, made of wood, that his accomplicies had been building. It went up and down like a roller coaster and then came back to the ground. We went along the wooden planks that they were laying down like railway tracks for a while and then they petered out because the men hadn't finished. We got that far and the lawyer said that it would be enough.

We were on our way to the airport. I was very worried because the last time they had been full and I had been the last person so I couldn't get on the plane. We got to the last step where they had a cafeteria we could get food. Gayatri stopped to get some food and was taking a long time about it, unconcerned that we wouldn't be allowed on the plane. I went straight through the line, didn't pick up any food, and tried to get past the checkout at the end. But there wasn't any way past. The lady at the checkout counter asked me if I was really just going to have raisins and nuts on the plane. I broke down crying about how I hadn't been let on the plane last time. She assured me that there was room this time; that they weren't oversold. I went back to find Gayatri who hadn't gotten any food yet but was sitting at one of the tables.

Tue 24 Aug

Jimmy Turnure, Dennis and I were at 1377. We decided to go to Fort Snelling, which I knew was on highway 55. We got in the car and I was driving. It wasn't too hard to adjust and use the brake and accelerator (like it sometimes is in dreams). I went straight up Snelling because that was the way I was used to going. When I came to a sign for highway 51 I realized that I had gone the wrong direction, so I turned back down highway 51 which connected with 55 and I hoped that they wouldn't notice the huge detour. But 51 stopped at a fence and you had to hop over it to get to 55. So I left the car there and went back to 1377 on foot. I sat there cross legged in the middle of the living room floor waiting for them to come back feeling bad that I had wasted so much time and left the car up north.

Jumping on a train. Smoking in an abandoned house near a day care. Making love to a little girl.

Fri 27 Aug

I was lying in bed in my apartment. It was a double apartment. Someone came in and woke me up. It was a young black woman. I was like, 'Do I know you?'. Then the rest of the group came in and I remembered what it was. It was a complicated scheme to rescue (kidnap) a child that we felt was at risk. Caroline had figured out a way to get in to the house without making noise and taught it to one of this group. Put water on the basket, insert the basket and that opened the door. So they were able to get in and take the baby. Then they planned a complicated double-back in the apartment building to avoid being followed. They succeeded and had come back here with the baby as agreed previously.

Two business men – Professor Roberts and my dad? – came by. They were also part of the scheme and were planning to tell their company that they didn't like where they were staying so that they would have an excuse to move closer. Dennis was explaining to the other guy that it was called 'the burbs'. 'We will complain about "the burbs".' We knew that we were all accomplicies to kidnapping but we felt it was the right thing to do.

Then we were in court. We had taken the baby because it was being mistreated by the mother. The father was mostly absent and said that his reason was that because of her deep anti-abortion principles he couldn't force her to abort the child of the son. The lawers asked, 'well if you had been forceful, like a macho guy in a movie…' and then the name of the guy went down the line of laywers seated there, each one mentioning a different macho guy until it came to our guy – the one who didn't know that 'the burbs' was slang for the suburbs. He suddenly realised that you can't force a woman at all and said so. The message went back up the line as a sudden realization. There was a big questionmark hanging over the statement about the son. Then she came in and it was revealed – acutally the child was a product of incest with her older child (queue suspenseful music)!

She was in the balcony and the older child was being led by police. He gave her the finger. She smirked and turned away. The commentator said he was like a badger who only new one trick – to claw at everything around him.

Sat 28 Aug

Running through a park between 35 and University west of Snelling in the rain. Singing a song about a conspiracy theory based on Helter Skelter.

Sun 29 Aug

Leaving John (Norma) Banks' house – we couldn't get a band together. I tried to fly up in the air but everything was darkness. Then there were little specs of light and then a big light in the distance. I thought 'Oh no, this isn't going to turn out just to be falling snow in the streetlight and I am a bum!' But that is exactly what it was. I couldn't fly much past the streetlight. I didn't have many clothes on and I didn't have anywhere to go but a nearby forest park. I thought it was going to be very cold, but that was what I asked for.

We were in a lab for a class. I was taking a long time to pick out a mosaic tesselation pattern. My friends had were already on their way. We were all boyfriend and girlfriend with each other but pretending to be boyfriend/girlfriend with a different person than we actually were. Even to the point of one of the ladies pretending to be a guy.

The professor handed out early grades before the final. Mine was a D because I had missed one of the tests. So I needed to talk to him to see if I could make up the work. But he was talking with a lot of other students after class and it was taking a long time.

Tue 31 Aug

Flying into the jaws of a tree

Th 2 Sep

Up in a balcony, helping some girls down to the floor. Had to do walking in the forest (?)

Fri 3 Sep

After a night of chills and fever from UTI

Software Development Manager

Shitting in a balcony over the bookstore at Snelling & University. The cleaning boy had left his unicycle in the stall and I had to try to get around it. There was just a hole in the ground. He kept looking in so I didn't want to do anything. He went to the next stall thinking that would make me more confortable. Then an older guy came in and was looking so I couldn't do anything. Finally they both left and only a lady was looking in. So I felt comfortable enough to do it with her outside, only putting a curain beteen us. Then It started to come out and made a mess everywhere. I was afraid that it had come out in real life and that my diapers would be a mess. So I went to the shower and started to wash. Fortunately everything cleaned up and I left.

Driving with John Banks

We went to a seminar at the Minnesota state capital which was actually the civic center. It was about YC incubation. The discussion got wrapped up around procedural issues because of some internal politics. We left and we were driving away. It was me, John, a friend of John's and the driver he had hired.
