Last 14 Days on an Asteroid

It was a movie. We were all on an asteroid in space. There were only 14 days left. And there were 14 of us. But we couldn't leave; we all had to go down with the ship. The whole movie was going to be the debate over whether to declare an emergency and leave despite the fact that regulations didn't allow it or blindly adhere to the regulations and die when the asteroid did. I was arguing for declaring an emergency and leaving. It also seemed like there were more than 14 people there. Apparently some of them were ready to leave because they weren't part of the skeleton crew list that had to stay behind so they were all preparing to leave before the end anyway.

At work, need to take a class

I was trying to get to my first meeting of the day. Up St. Clair and through the hallways of Linwood. I used a stick – an unusually long drumstick, shorter than a regular walking stick – to propel myself along while continuing to float above the ground. I wondered how everyone thought of me floating there. I wondered why at a certain age you had to start walking with a stick and if I was being pretentious.

I tried to get to the meeting room but I went past and into a grocery store. I thought I would be lost in endless grocery stores, but I turned around and went back through the door to see memble from TK go into the meeting room so I followed him in there. He was giving a presentation, scoring people on some funny quiz that they did. He had a lazer pointer that projected unicorns and constellations on the walls and ceiling. There was a dragon above the clouds and it blocked out the projection where it was.

I thought to myself that I was so out of it and I needed to take a class or something just to get my mind working on a different track where I could relate to people more.

Tue 19 Oct

Biking to Work

I was biking to work. This involved going along Standford to Warwick, then turning left. The street was no longer a street but a grassy hill that went up. I glided to nearly the top before it became difficult to pedal. Then I turned left again and started climing an even higher hill. There were many other, quite serious, bikers on this hill and several of them passed me. We had to get a ball up the hill and I let mine slip down. But I didn't go back for it; I went on to the top of the hill with intention to go back down and do the whole thing over.

Kitchen Work

It was a large field. A park like Hidden Falls, near the 35 that never was. I got thirsty so I scooped up some sand to make a bowl and went to a depression in the park where John Banks had a kitchen and was washing dishes. I filled my sand bowl with water from the tap and drank it. Clayton was there and he intimated that there might be a party nearby where people were handing out joints, some of them with angel dust. I thought to play it cool and didn't rush right there. But when I got there everyone was gone. I walked back home past the liquor store on Hamiline and Pascal but there was nobody there but bikers that I didn't know either.

Wed 20 Oct

The long night

I was sitting in a place across University from the Midway shopping center. It was late at night and I wasn't sleeping. I was eating peyote. I wondered if I should go to class the next day. It was dark and you couldn't see anyone out the window. Then the drugs started to work and the sun came up and there were so many people walking by on the street. I wondered if I should go to class or skip it. I was afraid that if I went to class I might mistakenly think something that would send me in the wrong direction. I had no money and I planned to just run myself out until I had nothing. I could see from the people rushing down the street that if I had no money that would mean that there was less that I could do. So that meant that money was just a way of speeding things up and I had no need to go fast.

Making Change

Trent and I went to a sandwich shop at the mall. The clerk was out from behind the counter. The bill was 2.97 so Trent took 3 dollars out and laid it down. But the clerk mistook his payment for that of another customer whose bill was 2.94. He started to redo the calculation over and show us the menu with the prices where what we ordered was differetn by 3 cents from what the other customer had ordered. So I pulled out a nickel and handed it to him. He wanted to redo the calculation but I said that I didn't have time to worry about 3 cents. As we left, he said that he thought it was the principle of the thing. I said, no, the amount matters too. I would negotate for 10 months for a million dollar contract but only 1 month for a hundred thousand dollar contract for example.

Th 21 Oct

From a billion years ago

We were in a valley. This valley was surrounded by metal walls that held the water out. There were some rocks there. The rocks had funny shaped fossils on them. When you looked at them it was clear that they were some small pest that had some kind of poison foam sprayed over it. It died there because of the foam and it and the foam were fossilized in place.

We were discussing this and realized that there were two possibilities. Because it was a billion years ago, it couldn't have been any modern life form we were familiar with. So either life evolved twice independently on Earth or these formations came from an alien species.

I thought to myself that I didn't like to think about what it would mean if it was an alien species. It would be totally alien and independent of any hierarchy on earth that we were familiar with. It would just eat you without even thinking about it. Then a giant creature like a squid with a shell came down the river from the other side and started to swallow us. I had to unthink the dream. I didn't like it.

The eye in the sea

We went out to the shore. As you started to swim into the ocean, you could see that the patterns in the sand under the water made the image of an eye. I soon started to sink under the waves and realized that I could breathe underwater.

I was then in a room, like a school gym, filled with water. There were many other people there doing things with ladders and so forth. I asked someone what it would take for them to destroy the big power. They said they wanted a staute of themselves built 500 feet high. I then started to design the statue, asking details about how they wanted the carring case that hung off their pocket designed and so forth.

Fri 22 Oct MMXXI

Left at the Elevator

We were all packing up. I took longer than the others and when I got to the elevator they were already gone. I couldn't believe it and I went off to look for them. I was going around the university.

Looking for papers

I kept trying to find the right papers in various backpacks and in the back seat of the car.

Dad cut his finger trying to get the car to start. It was a really bad cut on the thumb and I told him to stop working on it; that he needed to take care of it right away. I went back to looking for the papers but they were nowhere to be found.

Sun 24 Oct MMXXI Wk 43

The Swiss Pikers

We were sitting in a restaurant. A large circular restaurant with glass windows. In a depression with grassy hills all around. The Swiss pikers came with mechanical horses and a new larger version of a pike that was like a small oil pipeline and which took multiple people, on horseback, in a line, to carry. We thought they were just playing but they actually crashed into the glass windows of the restaurant. This involved them falling over and losing control temporarily in the process.

We all ran and scattered. I got on my horse and started flying over the planes. They were ready for people to flee and had flights of arrows prepared. I thought that I would be able to dodge the arrows but they came over in a cloud. Fortunately my armor protected me. I stayed ahead of the next volley of arrows. They arrows were little sparrows and were flying behind me. My horse started to fly up into the air over the trees.

Still the sparrow arrows came behind me though there were fewer of them now. I had to find a way to hide fropm them. There was a long bridge, with a tree covered walkway in the middle. I flew onto that and they were unlikely to find me there. As I walked along I came up to some dogs. My horse was worried that they would be hostile but the first one, a small puppy, came up and sniffed me and it soon became clear that they would accept us.

Don't show your face

You couldn't show your face in public. If you did, the other person would have to shoot you. There was a competition going on and I was part of the competition.

We were driving up to an old factory that was a secret prison where all the most dangerous and insane mad scientists were kept and had been kept for 50 years. There was a conspiracy afoot as some of them were due to be released after 50 years. It turned out that the warden had been subverted by them on day one and had been part of the planning all along. She was wearing a funny helmet.

King of the GDT

I was sitting at my desk trying to organize things. There was a lot of paper for recycling. I could move distant objects with my mouse and I wondered where the energy came from. As I moved things away from my line of sight it revealed a medeval town square.

Someon wanted to crown me the king of the GDT and I wondered if it really shouldn't have been Joe Glentz. There were lots of engineers sitting in cubicles across the way doing engineer things. They were all staying focused just on the problems they were given or themselves discovered and not expanding the scope of their inquiry.

Mon 25 Oct

I was riding my horse into work. I rode past the other children from school playing a game in a field. There were two circles of children, one on the inside and one on the outside. Like in musical chairs, they walked in different directions while the music continued. The ones on the outside would try to run as fast as possible to get ahead as far as they could. When the music stopped, the person on the outside ring who was farthest along would win, and also the person who was opposite them in the inner circle. We thought about the strategy of this game since it seemed mostly randon, but it was really about knowing your skills when you chose which circle to get into at the beginning.

To get in the building, the horses had to duck their heads. The horse of the person in front of me ducked their head without needed to be guided, but mine only ducked their head when I ducked my head. This meant that I almost hit my head on the ceiling. The inside of the building was like the hallway in mechanic arts and there was a gymnasium inside.

Dennis Fischbach came out holding some posters in German. I explained that I had been working on these for a project with Tim Hinricher. Except I was mistaken and it was actually Brad Pierskalla. I felt very embarrased that I had gotten the name wrong. Management wanted to change the posters to English but I was emphatic about remaining international.

Wed 27 Oct

Showering before work

I was trying to get to work. Work was at Linwood. Sort of. I was in my Father's house, which was an older house out in the country. He was gone and I wasn't sure when he was coming back. He had gone to New Orleans/St. Louis. He had been gone there for longer than expected and we hadn't heard from him.

I went into the bathroom but the shower was in a separate room. The clothes that I had brought were all disorganized and all over the floor. It was hard to tell which were mine and which weren't; which I had brought with me this time and which I had left from before. Finally I got my clothes figured out. I was trying on different shoes until I found some that didn't look silly (like boots) and were comfortable (not dress shoes).

I went into the kitchen to get some quick breakfast before running out to work. There were dishes and silverware strewn haphazardly everywhere. Some of them clean and some of them dirty. My mother came in. I explained that I usually had cereal so would have peanut butter this time. I took the last piece of bread. I tried to find a clean knife. The peanut butter jar turned out not to have much left in it; hardly enough for one slice.

Virus on my laptop

I got to work and was going to my first meeting. My boss took myself and one other aside and stared asking some questions. He wanted to see the metrics that I had been preparing. I started to boot up my laptop but there was a virus on it that made it search for pictures of fat naked women. It was a separate application, but I couldn't find the exit button. The menues just went on and one with silly and frivolous things done in a childish and cartoonlike manner, for example Beatles trivia. I started to worry about whether to contact IT and how I was going to back up the data and wipe the operating system to start over.

Homeless Refugee

The refugee arrived at the shelter. He was wearing a red coat with a hood. There were others there, some of them for overnight stay and some on other business. So it was a long wait. He and the others settled down to sleep overnight in the chairs and benches of the waiting room of the social services facility. In the morning he started to complain about having to wait so long when it became clear that they might all have to wait a second night. They finally started to lead him in to start the work.

Th 28 Oct

Kissing Gayatri in the Street

We were kissing in the street. The street was full of water and we were half underwater and we were still kissing.

Hotel Room #4

A man came and led me away. Suddenly we were in a place I'd never been before. Hotel room #4. He wanted to show me.

The Nigerian Businessman

Then we went to his father's place. We were hanging around the kitchen. His father was a businessman. He was talking about getting a place with a little land in Nigeria. We talked about looking at different developments outside Legos vs. living in Legos, how far away they would be from the city, which ones would be any good but not too expensive or too far and so on.

Fri 29 Oct

We were on the train. I thought I would get on a bicyle and meet them back at home. I left them playing in a place that was Minneapolis but also unfinished 35E. Earlier I had been able to put the bicyle together from the parts that were left on the train very quickly. But this time I was unable to and missed my stop. I tried to text them but my phone was in a different mode and all I was able to send was 'at 0' instead of 'at home'. Home was north of University, but more rural.

I thought about how I would get back. Taking the train back would be the most obvious way. I thought I might buy a small bicycle for $100 in the town and ride that back over days. It would be an adventure. I didn't have any money and I didn't know where I was going to get any money from.

The train was just supposed to go to Shakopee/Taylor's Falls but this one was actually going to Fargo/Thunder Bay. So then I had to wonder how I would get back from there.

Sun 31 Oct MMXXI (Halloween)

It was the first day of the last quarter of school. I was in the hallway which was like the Mechanic Arts hallway outside the auditorium. I had already passed all my classes so I was at liberty to do what I liked. It was Tuesday at 2:30 when I had had a class that I went to last term so I assumed that I would go to the smae class but hadn't checked the schedule. I sat down in the hallway to do some independent study. I was trying to organize my computer.

There was a side hallway and I started to hang out with this girl. Eventually I ended up in her room, which was off the side hallway. At first she was quite posh and had half empty bottles of wine in her room. But then she was quite plain and a little geeky. We just kept sitting close to each other on her bed.

Mon 1 Nov MMXXI (All Saints DAy)

I was a graduate student. Except that I had finished all my courses and had given up on my thesis. But I was still in college waiting to find something. I started going to teach my course. I was just taking a class and teaching a class and it was all beneath me. But I was hardly ever on time for my students. I was walking along the road and along the fence. It was a new road in a northern town. I was glad that I was going to be on time for class for once and that I felt prepared enough for the class in the sense that I could just wing the examples.

I was getting some equipment from the lab. The lab was just south of the factory in TK. Except that it was registration time so there were lines and lines of students also getting equipment. I had to leave past the cashier. I wanted to explain that I had a legitimate reason for taking the equipment away from the lab but there was no one to explain to and no one asked about it as I left.

Tue 2 Nov MMXXI

Gayatri and I were going through some rooms. They were in order from most holy to least. First we found some whipping cream. We were stepping on the tops of the furniture in the church that had been stacked up so close together you couldn't walk between them. First some old wooden furniture then some stone. Other people were there and we had to side step to avoid them stepping on us while we walked over the stone slabs and they passed us on the way. Then some newer furniture and finally a liquor warehouse with barrels from ale to hard drinks. We sat down at the restaurant.

As we walked along the street we saw a business that was closed on Sunday from 1:00 to 2:00. Gayatri told me that this was very popular among the religious right wing. There was a radio host who told everyone that they had to drop everything and listen at that time. And they all sang this one song. The song was supposed to have some kind of vauge watered down religious meaning. But the most striking thing upon first hearing it was that the words were very difficult to understand and it was very easy to imagine them replaced with curse words. Every chourus ended with mumble-mumble-UCK! for example.

Wed 3 Nov MMXXI

I went into a room to urinate. But there was water everywhere and there were frogs and fish in the water and it was hard to find a place to stand comfortably.

Th 4 Nov MMXXI

We were at a restaurant which was my bed from 1377. Gayatri wanted some finger fucking so we arranged our bodies on the bed. I was afraid we would get noticed but she was sure they were all asleep. As we did it another lady came and lay on the bed with us, holding Gayatri's head. Then I was doing it to Gayatri and looking at both of their naked breasts.

After that I went back to the (picnic-esque) tables from the restaurant. All the food was non veg. I grumbled and sat down to resign myself to my fate of not having much good to eat. Someone came by with a pumpkin pie in a plastic cup. I was like, really? Is that a pumpkin pie in there? They assured me that it was and moved some of it aside with a knife to show the layers inside. I was like, wow, that is so kitsch its notable. I should tell Trent about it. So I got out my phone to take a picture and send to him but I couldn't get it to work.

We were at work which was an office which was the dungeon of 1377, but raised to the second floor like Mechanic Arts. We were cleaning stuff up and walking on top of all the cabinets. There was a name for something and I asked who called it that first and it was Carl Withey.

I went into an adjacent room which was the auditorium of a school. It had very steep walls and a curtain at the back. I took the curtain down and the room grew less quiet. Then we tested the sound in the room with and without the curtain.

After that it became a Blake's Seven show. We were getting in a spaceship with some new ladies.

Fri 5 Nov MMXXI

I was in a saloon. It was a cold winter and it was on the northwest corner of University & Lexington. There was some question about getting some shoes. I got the shoes by right and that helped me walk over the drifts of snow that where there. There were lots of people milling around. The snow was slushy and wet the way it gets when lots of people walk over it. But it wasn't very dirty. I got a t shirt as well and almost a jacket.

We were the police and we had arrested a man. But he was actually the reincarnation of Hoagy Charmichal so I thought we should let him go as that was so remarkable. So I had to prove it which meant that he had to be able to sing the Hong Kong Blues. So we sat down on some benches behind a barrier and I played the song on one of those little metal cups from India. It was hard to play it and I played some wrong notes. I also did too much of the singing for him but he got it in the end.

Then everyone had to leave but I was late leaving so I couldn't get my jacket. It was very cold outside and I didn't know what I was going to do but at least I had my shoes and t-shirt.

I went and sat at a pub with a friend outside. Then a mad gangster with a large automatic weapon came and pointed it at me. He insisted that it was his t-shirt. Since he was pointing a gun at me, my friend and I agreed that I had just made a mistake. I took the t shirt off and gave it to him. He left. Then I was sitting there without jacket or t-shirt but at least I still had my shoes.

Mon 08 Nov XXI

I was driving a truck as a second job and I got back at 10 PM. I had to pick up the semi but it wasn't there. Some other people from the company were there and they called me ten-o-clock because I came in late at 10. I said that sometimes in India I had been as late as that but usually I was earlier.

I hugged John Lennon's mom. Her son strutting around in nylons and long hair had driven her crazy. I said that all the joy we got from all those songs wasn't worth her pain; we would have found something else to dance to.

I was in an important meeting as ambassador. I always made a point of having a cigarette and then spending some time reading before the meeting, which made it a little late. The place was a giant auditorium and I flew there headfirst. To get the the next meeting you had to dive in head first and fly around a corner. It was a leap of faith. I had done this before quite successfully and the manna was strong. But this time I spun and went feet first which broke the manna. I ended up outside zone 5 and in zone 4 where I was not supposed to be. Fortunately because I was an ambassador someone let me back in the door to zone 5. So it wasn't that I had so much power to fly it was that the place was giving me that power and when I accidentally went outside the power dropped.

I had to find my way back to the meeting and I was going through a bunch of hallways and cafeterias in the basement. The manna got weaker and weaker and eventually flying became slower than pushing myself along with the chairs. And then that became slower and I just ended up walking.

Tue 09 Nov XXI

I was going up a mountain. I had been tripping and was up all night. I thought that it would be easier to get over the mountain than it actually was. I had to turn back. There were a lot of skiers at the top.

Th 18 Nov MMXXI

At work, I had to reboot the computer and install a new tape drive. It resulted in a complete wipe of the system. I hoped I had a complete backup! This was on a large televsion screen in the living room of 1377.

We were on a hill. It was a steep sandy hill and there was no water. We (mama & I0 sat down and started to worry about becoming dehydrated over the night. But there were animals there. It was a skunk!

Dan Smith and some other school children were there. We were in a park by a lake. I was pouring paint over itself to make 3d sculputres. I was following another kid into a convenience store near Hamline & Snelling.

Fri 19 Nov MMXXI

We were going to a working place far in the north. Driving along roads I was unfamiliar with. Soemone was driving me in their truck. I thought it was up near Duluth, but really it was only Maplewood Mall. He drove us into the parking lot and restaurants of Maplewood Mall. I asked if this was Maplewood Mall and he said yes. There were others with us in the truck.

We were working on this really cool project and I was sitting around the table with two of my clients. I was asking if they got developers who commuted in from near Duluth or mostly just north of the cities. Mostly just north of the cities. It was like working with Watlow, except in the north instead of the south.

It was an old gentleman's club, repurposed. I had to go to the bathroom. All the old wide wooden hallways were empty and I found it. There were places to sleep and wooden ladders and lofts.

At lunch the guy kept handing me food. I thought he was giving me a coke bottle so I drank from it but really he meant to share it.

When I got back it was time to leave and we all started to go out. We all had to go to the bathroom so I went with them. Now we had to put all our pocket contents in a tray and get scanned by the machine. I complained that all I had in my pockets was my keys and that I had already been to the bathroom without any problems but they insisted. I was worried about just leaving my keys in an open wooden tray but they insisted.

At that point I got mad and stormed off, throwing things, strangling young brunettes and trying to fly through an opening that was too small and I got stuck.

Sun 21 Nov MMXXI

Tue 23 Nov MMXXI

Wed 24 Nov MMXXI

Beer in Thomas Lake

I was in the apartment at Thomas Lake. I had to go drive somewhere. Someone wanted some beer. I didn't want any beer because I had do drive, but I pored him some and pored myself a small one and took a sip. I immediately felt drunk and I was uncertain of my ability to drive.

When I pored the beer into hot coffee, it became frozen and made a slushy ice cube the shape of the cup and a little less than an inch deep. It tasted good and had a funny chewy consistency to it.

Dog Jumping for the Clouds

I had to go along a twisty path in a park beneath some hills where some houses were. It led through some shops and restaurants. I turned back around after going through some shops. There was a dog there. A big dog, almost the size of a pony. It ran past me. Was I responsible for it? It had gotten confused for some reason. There, on the path that led directly away from the shops and back through the park, it started to jump up and bark. It could see the clouds. They were highly varied. It thought it could jump up to reach one of the more lower lying strands. Maybe it could. Someone else also came out to attend to the dog.

Ulrich driving at the test track

Ulrich was driving to the test track. It was in Germany so he was on his home turf. There were a bunch of little bridges with railings after a boulevard. He drove through and around the bridges, but ran over the corners of them, causing the car to bump up uncomfortably.

Then we got to a clearning where other people from his work were arranging the test tracks for the driving tests. They had tracks made of many many balls that they could lay down and arrange in different shapes and angles. Th 25 Nov MMXXI

Negotiating for grades

I was in a class, except that I was taking the class. There were a handful of us who didn't do so well. I was sat down at a table in a corner next to a door to the outside street with the teacher and an advisor. I had done OK in the first term but had really slipped in the second term. We were about 2/3 of the way through the second term now. They were saying some vauge things, implying what could happen. I was all like, well that's not so bad, it is something that a college recruiter might be able to overlook as a single black mark. On the futility of automation

We were sitting at a picnic-esqe table in a road like a food court under some machinery. The other people at the table were complaining about how you used to be able to fix stuff yourself but now you had to take things into the shop and it was more expensive and took longer.

I interrupted them to reveal that that was my job; analyzing problems that people had in order to devise exceedingly complicated ways to overcome those problems that then just made things more difficult instead of simpler.

Mon 29 Nov MMXXI

It came up very very close and stuck its beak right in my binoculars. You see, if I hadn't had the binoculars it would have seen my human face and been scared. But with the binoculars it didn't know what I was. Maybe I looked more like another penguin to it.

It flew right up to the landing and stood about a foot or so away from where I was sitting. We were just sitting there together being warm. Then a lady came in, said the penguin couldn't be here and started leading it forcefully away by the hand/flipper/wing.

I was in school, sitting at a table, tying my shoes. A younger kid came up to me and – as a joke – took my shoe away. Then they brought it back. I said something to him. An adult was there and said that I was being to harsh.

Sat 11 Dec MMXXI

The Windmill

We were going into a place where you had to solve a bunch of problems to get out. I had been there before. The trick was that you had to go through the forward door. This led you around outside and back to the same place and only then could you open the side door which was the goal. I was with a different group of people this time and I was less confident that we could solve the problems. We didn't have a generalist like Ken Allen. Someone who didn't have specific deep skills but somehow catalyzed the skills of those around him to come up with a solution.

I went over to a coin operated machine that took a nickel. I had a dime and I thought it might work. Might give change. But it just gave me back my dime. And then a quarter and then a 50 cent piece and then a collectors 50 cent piece. I kept pulling coins from the machine. Troubleshooting

There was a giant tower of electronic equipment sitting outside a building. It was supposed to be receiving signals and producing an output but the output was garbled. Dennis Fischbach had already hypothesized that it must be a baud rate issue. I looked it over. I was feeling sleepy and thought I could just wait for somebody else to solve it. But then I hopped up and asked if we had the manuals for each of the pieces of equipment. If so, then we could find the input and output of each and how the input and output baud rate get set. We could then trace where the baud rate was incorrect. One of the people thought that was a great idea and ran off to get the manuals.

I sat right outside the white painted stone fence, pressed up against it. I thought this is where I belong, as close to the telematics group as possible without actually being part of it. Because Gayatri.

There was a guitar that people were playing. Except that the strings were all funny. Some of them didn't go all the way up and then new ones started after those ended. It was a pleasant sound if you played it the way it was supposed to be played. I was trying to play it like a guitar. At least the lowest strings were tuned the same was a guitar was tuned. But it didn't sound very good that way and there were only a few notes you could play like that.

Plan A

I was working in an office. The office was high on a hilltop, overlooking the city. There were some tables that I was sitting at and there was a reception desk where some others were sitting. Th 16 Dec MMXXI

Then and Now

My father came in and said that he had just played a computer game using AI that used only 800 bytes and was amazing. I expressed skepticism that a nontrivial game could be done in 800 bytes. I explained that it didn't count as AI unless there was some kind of emergent behaviour; unless it knew or did something unexpected by the developer.

We went down to look at it. Jimmy Turnure and a couple others were sitting at a table next to a large picture window in a room like a rec room. A laptop was open on the table and it showed a game with 8 bit graphics; decent, but old-fashioned. I was skeptical that it really fit in 800 bytes or that it was really AI rather than regular programming.

Jimmy Turnure had a game book. I was trying to read the title. It was called Then and Now. The title was written in those funny gothic heavy metal letters so it was hard to read. Every play had two aspects; the past and the present. So you would draw a card that had two cards on it, one for then and one for now. There were – as is common with these things – a whole sequence of rule books and Jimmy was having a discussion with the player accross from him (on the same side of the table as me and my father) about the Then One rule book, which was the first extension.

We started to play and I started to lay my cards down on the table in front of me as instructed. The player accross from me, sitting next to Jimmy, started to criticise where I lay the cards. I explainded that topologically they were layed out the same as the rest of the people, but they didn't buy that and I moved then into a more traditional arrangement.

Getting ready for School

I was in the bedroom of 1377. Dennis was in the basement. He came up to tell me it was time to go to school. I started trying to find my socks in the pile on the floor. I also started cleaning some things up. There were two bicycles there that I moved over to make more room. There were also a number of small clear stones that I started to arrange into bottles.

I desperatedly wanted to masturbate before leaving for work or I would be bothered all day but I never got the chance what with people coming in and out of the kitchen at unpredictible times.

I put on my socks and went off to school/work. The school was on a hill up some steps. Water was poring down the steps and I wondered if my socks were really appropriate for the environment. I tried to wait until between waves of water running down the steps so that I could minimize who wet my socks got. But the water just came out ever more strongly and ever more deeply and there was no way to get up the stairs and avoid getting completely soaked.

Crawling over Pianos in a warehouse

The Beatles' unique sound was not caused by the fungus on the piano, but rather the unique curvature of wooden slats on the floor of the Abbey Road studio." We had to conclude only that this experiment showed no evidence in favor of the piano fungus theory and no evidence against the floor board curvature theory.

No Shortwave

Wed 9 Aug MM XX III

I went down to lake Michigan. The waters had been too cold to go in in the morning but they had warmed up a little by now.

Th 10 Aug MM XX III

I was trying to get home. I had 2 bicycles, a large quantity of groceries and some frozen items. I was going to stop at a rental company and split it into 3 delveries. I made an extra point about how much I valued their services to try to soften any disappointment that I wasn't using them now.

I drove away. The car became a bicycle, with 2 balls that rotated at the bottom of each tire. The balls looked like ear buds. The tires didn't rotate; the balls at the bottom did. Navigation was very smooth at least while I was going downhill.

Eventually the bike degraded and I was just holding the ear bud ball rollers on the bottom of a cylindrical metal bar.

I was going uphill and I didn't see the sign that said pedestrians only. An old lady stopped me and guided me back through the pedestrian area to the street.

Shortly I came to a place where I could see the city accross a river valley. That was where I wanted to get to. The city was Minneapolis/St. Paul except it had landmarks like the London Eye and the Shard. I started to go along the river road to get back to the city.

My mechanism of holding the roller balls completely broke down and I started to look for alternatives to the cylindrical metal bar that I had been using in junk along the side of the road.

John Banks was there with a friend and they were just walking and encouraged me to do the same. I eventually got something like the roller ball mechanism working with a large pole tapered to one end like a torpedo and was able to glide along the sidewalks of the river road with John and his friend, at least downhill or on the level.

I was trying to think whether I should try to organize work or dive in to something deep because I didn't have much time there and other people were depending on me.

Driving

We were driving. A young girl was at the wheel. Gayatri and I were passengers. The girl was talking about climate change. I said if you were really concerned about it you wouldn't even be driving this car. She got so mad that she pointed the car toward a cliff and then refused to steer anymore. I grabbed the wheel but it was to late to stop the car from going over the cliff. I was able to manuver the car while in midair to land in a lake instead of the ground so we all survived. I swam over to the side of the lake where they were selling drinks for the swimmers and asked to call the police. "For what?" the bartender asked. "Justifiable homicide," I said. We had a discussion around how 'justifiable homicide' was a legal term and maybe we should just say 'attempted homicide'. I called the operator on 0 as was put through to the police.

The art collector.

In a mix of Lovejoy, Dr. Who and the Lincoln Lawyer, the criminal wanted the fourth painting (as per the Lincoln Lawyer). We had an actual copy of it for sale (unlike the Lincoln Lawyer). As per Lovejoy, it was an exact copy and looked to be the real hand of the original artist. The criminal showed up at the exhibition to look at it and was taken away by the authorities (like Dr. Who) with a long lecture about how they would have been ok if they had stayed put. How was the fourth painting such a good copy? Lovejoy/Dr. Who was the original painter of all the paintings! Voila!

Sat 06 Apr MM XX IV

Going to a fancy party. Beth Gladhill was flirting with me. Like, right in front of Gayatri in the car. We were going to a supposedly really fancy place but when we got there, it was way less fancy than a lot of the places that Gayatri and I had been to together.

We had to get out of the clubhouse. Pete Townsend was leading us. The exit looked like it wasn't big enough to crawl through But it extended on some strings and springs if you pushed it up and I crawled through.

A large furry animal sat on me. I was afraid that it would kill me but it just went to sleep.

Th 11 Apr MM XX IV

We were all going to the movies. We were taking some of the grandparents which included Jagi and Nomita. But first we had to clean up a board game that we had been playing. I insisted on putting it away all proper, so I sat on the floor and put the pieces away in little bags. But even so, the black and white stones (like go pieces) were all mixed up. This made me late and I couldn't find my phone. I ran out to the car, where everyone was.

The living room where we were playing the game was large and square, with a big fireplace in the west wall, basically Georgian in style. There were large windown in the north wall that looked up to a garden. The table that we had been playing on was against the south wall. The corridor led east and then turned south to the main entrance where the car was waiting, like the entrance to a hotel or apartment building.

It was a big white car, almost like a limo. I noticed that 2 of the seats were empty, mine and Gayatri's. I asked where Gayatri was, she had been taken to the dentist. I wondered how they managed to drive her all the way to the dentist and back in just that time. I also wondered if it was she who had my phone. We concluded that she must have. I worried what would happen if I went off without my phone and she needed to reach me. But I knew that if I went back in to the house, It would take just so long. I wondered if I should have them take me to the dentist to sit with her.

They started to drive the car away, even though I was still holding the door open and I had to tell them to stop. Eventually we agreed that I would just come with them to the movie, for which we were now very late. Just how late I never figured out because what I thought was a clock giving the time wasn't. I suggested that rather than being an hour late for the 4:00 showing we should just go to the 6:00 showing, and they acted like that was their original plan all along.

Sat 13 Apr MM XX IV

Exam with Communism

I was at Emily's house. I was supposed to be taking a test there. I was dressed in full business casual because it was an exam. Her father came in and put a box set of three books on the coffee table in front of the couch on which I was sitting.

The couch was facing west in a narrow living room which opened onto a small kitchen to the north. The entrance was in the east wall, between the couch and the kitchen. It opened out into a mud room that led to a garden. There were windows in the south wall of the living room, but they didn't let any light in because it was night.

They were about communism. One was supposed to teach you how to get by in Germany as a non- German speaking communist. I paged through it while waiting. I noticed that it didn't really do a very good job of teaching elementary German. It had a not of colloquisms in it. It also had Polish and Russian language interspersed. But the pictures and diagrams were effective from a pedagological point of view.

There was a cart with bread on it to the left of the coffee table.

I went over to get some bread. I got flour all over my nice clothes. We tried to brush them off. Then we went out to the garden.

Second chance

At some level I was aware that this was a dream. The premise was that I had an effectively unlimited budget to set up the engineering department for a small electronics manufacturer. So I was going around trying to order supplies and equipment, and hire people.

There was a smaller room to the furthest south. This then led, through a corridor on the west to a somewhat larger room just to the north. North of that the corridor led to the reception area, where the entrance led out to the east. Further north was the rest of the building.

I decided that we would not put dev in one of the two rooms and test in the other, but would rather organize by product. So our premire product, still under development, would have dev and test teams in the smaller room. While dev, production and test for our other products, already in production, would be in the larger room.

I was leading someone I hired as the quality lead. I was explaining to him that his role would be mostly on paper, deciding what good quality looked like, even if we had to cut corners for expediency. I wondered to myself why I had to explain this to him on his first day and if I would not have already said this during the interview. Someone else was in the south room, it may have been X from JCI.

Then I went off looking for places to buy equipment like lab equipment. I knew that I wanted a lot of equipment but realized that I didn't really know what kind of equipment we needed or where to get it. I started walking through the other rooms, asking the people there.

One of them explained that the cleaning lady had retired and was moving into a retirement home. I couldn't really understand his accent completely, but the upshot was that she wanted to retire in Israel but now was not the time. I agreed that now was not the time.

Sun 14 Apr MM XX IV

The Tuesday AM Meeting in the room alone

I usually just ran the Tuesday AM meeting by the seat of my pants because we had already covered stuff on Monday. But today I wanted to review the data from the project tool that we used. I tried logging into my computer. I was in a room in the corner of a building. It was like a large classroom in Linwood, but bigger than any of the rooms there. The ceilings were much higher. There were classroom tables arranged haphazardly. There were old computers and other electronic equipment on the tables. I went to the table in the far corner and tried to log it.

Trying to get a sandwich before the Tuesday PM Meeting

Since there was time before the PM meeting, I decided to go to the cafeteria to get a sandwich. The cafeteria was a large space and the offerings and stations were laid out in a large circular arc rather than in straight lines. They advertised lots of vegetarian options, but when you went up to them they were either already gone or were only non food items. I asked somebody and she pointed me to one of the areas but the selections seemed similar.

The Tuesday PM Meeting in the room with people

So I went with my sandwich to the other room where there were already some people. We had to rearrange the tables. All the tables were like school chairs with the little desk area for writing, except some of them were cut in half into trianges. They were supposed to all fit together properly, but they didn't fit together properly in practice. I arranged my chair next to a colleague. I then went over to sit on the ground next to a tree and eat my sandwich. I had to hide the bottle of wine what was in my basket because I was not supposed to be having that at work. I started eating the sandwich and it had some meat on it which I picked out. I then started eating the cucumbers that were in it but even they had some kind of meat sauce smeared on them so I gave it up completely.

The Back Stairs

There was a tiny little entrance to some stairs going up where Gayatri used to play as a child. I went up. They were very small and I was worried about getting stuck in them or being able to get back down again. When I got to the top of the stairs it was a landing with doors to two apartments. So these two apartments had a connection that they just kept closed. I peered through the crack in the door to the right hand apartment. There was a young family having cereal for breakfast. The father noticed me and opened the door. He stood right in front of my looking straight into my eyes. I tried to explain to him that my intentions were harmless.

Halloween at Leo & Virginia's

Well Halloween isn't normally a national holiday, but it fell on a Saturday that year so everyone was treating it like it was.

I was trying to comb my hair and it wouldn't behave. I tried spraying water on it with a little spray bottle. That didn't work. I sprayed more and more water on it. I replaced the water in the bottle. The bottle kept spraying when you held the nozzle down even when it was out of the bottle. Finally I gave up and decided that I would have to take a full shower. In Leo and Virginia's shower. I had taken a shower there before. When I turned the water on, the shower head sprayed outside the bath, but mostly on me so It didn't make a big mess. When I finally got in the shower and washed my hair I discovered why my hair had been so unruly. I had candle wax from birthday candles in my hair, at least the bottom parts of the hair. I went down to the basement to get a tee shirt. The basement was the basement of 1377. At least there were clean pants and shirts there. But I had painted on the inside of two of my Pikachu tee shirts that had sentimental value for me. I thought to myself that I really must have been drunk the night before to do that and get wax in my hair as well.

Monday 15 Apr MM XX IV

Boys School

We were in a class. We were supposed to be going through a case study/simulation. Everyone had assigned seats. I looked for a seat out on the far left. But my assigned seat was closer to the front and center. I sat down in the seat. It was a large padded chair. There were four of them right next to each other for the four people in the team. The information for the scenario was on a table in front of us and the chair backs were so high that I couldn't see or reach over them in order to look at it. So I contentent myself with sitting in the chair and looking at the other materials that were there. They had given us each a very nice backpack filled with a lot of merchandise. But the merchandise was stuff live travel kits for toiletries and regular stationary. Nothing that would help prepare for the scenario.

The Tuesday AM + PM Meetings execept this time someone else was doing them.

We were in a large hall where the meeting took place. People from the client company kept going in and out. They were always talking on the phone to their colleagues in other countries. I thought to myself that they were really moving forward on a strategic level. The project, which was ending, had led to a lot of strategic change and wasn't all just about the completion of the project tactically. I had very little to do so I just sat cross-legged on the floor in front of a low table and waited.

Then we were in a different room that had a large classroom table and a project screen along one wall. I had given the meeting before but now someone from a new fancier company was coming in to do it. He didn't have a regular computer with him, but rather something like a tv remote. It could be connected to the projection equipment, but to do so we had to move all the wires closer to the screen and ourselves with the wires, so we all ended up scrunched close to the screen in a tangle of wires.

Wed 17 Apr MM XX IV

In the beginning

I was trying to close the doors to the apartment. But a bear snuck in the back door. I gave it a big hug. It crawled through the apartment dragging its bottom and leaving bear shit [ https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bereshit_(parashah) ?] on the floors. It went out the front door. I closed the front door behind it. Then I ran back to try to close the back door before he came around back in again.

I closed it from the outside.

In the playground

Maybe 2 people couldn't afford an apartment but maybe two sets of two could. Working on creating a startup. Over the fence and into the playground.

Th 18 Apr MM XX IV

NASA Attic

We had to all leave the attic. It was like a NASA thing. Except we were all kids. We left and got it all sealed up. We went out to the street in the town. But then one of the kids remembered that they forgot something there so I had to go back and get it. You had to be clean climbing up the stairs in the tube to the attic. It was a whole process to unlock all the seals. I got up there and got what I needed. Then they had to help me getting some large items back down. It was a little like a camping trip.

Newspapers

There was a newspaper stand at the end of a cave like corridor that led out to an underground lake. I needed to go to the bathroom and that was the bathroom so I started urinating on the newspapers. Then I realized that that wasn't it, I was going to disappoint the other people who were around. it was next door in a different wooden booth where they had a dirt floor that was water in one corner. So I went there.

I had a drink and I went to the cabin where the facilities were and I washed out the last of the drink and then filled the glass with tap water.

Fri 19 Apr MM XX IV

Pablo's Studio

I was in Pablo's studio which was a single floor in the sublevel near where Cheapo records used to be on Snelling Avenue. It was early in the morning and the sun was just rising and I was thinking how this was not the time to be doing some kind of rock song.

I was thinking about using the equipment, which was distributed haphazardly accross the bare floor, but hadn't actually started yet.

A lady who was also using the studio came in. Pablo asked her what she thought of his song. She was very unappreciative and just said it was 'OK'.

White Magic

I was walking along a sidewalk among little houses. I was going to the house where my shaman was. I heard another group chanting "Hate the dark magic!". I thought to myself that they were wrong because as soon as you have activated hate you are in the dark magic.

I continued walking along the sidewalk. The area soon became flooded. At first I just tried to tiptoe so as not to get too wet, but then the water got deeper and deeper. Next I was standing on the metal fence that ran along the sidewalk to stay out of the water. I went to the end of the sidewalk, where there was a high cliff, leading to more little houses below. The water was just rushing over the side down to the area below. It carried me off to the left and spun me around so that I was facing backwards. There were so many beautiful flowers and plants along the path. I wondered if I was dying that this is what you saw then.

Cool Sculpt

Gayatri and I talking to the cool scuplt lady in a room similar to Pablo's studio about pain management post surgery.

Thursday 2 May MM XX IV

I was in class. I had missed the previous class. I was taking notes. Other people were worried about the upcoming tests. I just planned to do a lot of studying. They had split our group up into three and had changed the names and had really cool posters for them.

One of the girls and I started talking about alternative schools. She had been in one for one year and didn't like it. When she found out that I had gone to open school she came over and hugged me and stayed hugging me.

I had to get the car out of the garage parking lot so that we could catch the ferry.

But I didn't know where the car was because someone else had parked it.

Finally they came and took us to the car. It was through some narrow curved stairs that I hadn't even seen and didn't know about. Then we were waiting for everyone to get ready. They weren't going to be ready in time. Which just meant that we would catch the next ferry – ferrys came each half hour so I just went back to waiting.

I was walking back to my dorm room. I had passed my two tests and was wondering why everyone else didn't want to party now the same way I did?

Saturday 18 May MM XX IV

We were going to a concert.

I had been at the election for 12 hours. Going to the concert was similar in terms of having to stay awake for that length of time.

We got into the bus, which was a boat. The bus driver stopped, double parked, at a stationary shop on Grand near Lexington.

He needed some invoice slips because he was an independent contractor. He didn't take long to run inside and by them.

We went along. We were sitting in the upstairs of the bus. It was a double decker.

I was sitting in front with one of Gayatri's colleagues, who was a younger man. He was like Steve Larson.

I realized that I was making too many silly jokes. I turned around to face the rest of the group.

At that time, he got up to do something, but fell out the window. I rushed over and looked down.

He was lying half out the window of the floor below. I asked him if he was OK and he said no. He thought that he had broken his leg.

It was a good thing that he had fallen into the window, because otherwise he would have fallen into the river.

We had gone up a little channel past the fork where the Minnesota meets the Mississippi.

We were going somewhere in Minneapolis to pick up the last of the colleagues of Gayatri who were going with us to the concert.

The bus driver stopped the boat immediately and we all got out onto shore. Four of us started to call 911 on our cell phones.

There were some other people milling about as it was an island that was a little park. There was a pay phone there and some of the people were using it.

All four of us connected to 911 at the same time so each of us thought that the other would talk and we all hung up.

This made me very angry. I called back and was still yelling at everyone else when the emergency services operator came on the line.

So I had to apologize for yelling. I explained that our friend had been injured and that was why we were upset.

I explained our location to him including the number on the pay phone.

He said that the river we were on was a dead end. I said yeah, that we were only going to pick up our colleague.

The emergency services eventually came and took him away.

Then we were in a building, still waiting to go to the show.

I had taken a nap and was still sleepy. Gayatri was making fun of me for it.

I was worried that we wouldn't have ear plugs and that the show would be too loud and I wouldn't enjoy it.

Gayatri went to a waiting room for a pharmacy clinic which happened to be in this building and got some ear plugs from them.

Sunday 19 May MM XX IV

Roger Montgomerys room

I was in a class. The class was in Roger Montgomery's old classroom in Mechanic Arts.

The class was split in two. The popular people were in the other part. I didn't go there because the lead popular guy just led everything his own way too much.

There was only one other person in the class with me. The interaction was mainly between the teacher and the other person. I was listening in and just commenting occasionaly. And I was OK with that.

Packing for another flight

We were packing for another flight. I woke up just in time to start packing. There were two suitcases.

One was shaped normally, a little small. The other was irregularly shaped. There was plenty of room still in the normally shaped small suitcase.

So I was able to get all of the stuff from my backpack, which was overfilled into the suitcase.

For the irregularly shaped bag I removed all the guns and just put musical instruments in it.

I then went down to see how my mom was doing with her packing.

I saw that she was loading dishes one at a time onto a conveyor belt.

I wondered how that was ever going to be done in time for our flight.

Wed 22 May MM XX IV

I was leading a meeting. The dream was particularly vivid. I was going to expose at the meeting how the financials didn't add up. This was because I didn't have any other agenda. Unless he gave me some other agenda items. He was running around talking to people. I didn't know if he was finding a new agenda working on the financials or just chatting.

I opened the meeting. We were sitting by large glass windows on a high floor of a building. There were many long tables. Like tables you would have in a schoolroom. I had gum in my mouth. I tried to get the gum out prior to speaking, because I didn't want people to see me over the video with gum. But every time I took it out there was just more there and it stuck to my face as well. I finally had to just speak with 'only a little' gum instead of none.

Sun 2 June MM XX IV

I was in a class. The professor made up a word by taking every other letter of two words and intermingling them. Like LOREM IPSUM becomes LIOPRSEUMM.

I made a joke, 'Hey professor, do us a favor and don't join the team responsible for creating esperanto or other contrived languages.'

The other students thought it was funny but not as funny as I had hoped that they would.

I had had to ask the student sitting at the table next to me what the name of esperanto was.

The class wasn't ending as soon as I thought. I took out a third page for notes and started to take notes.

Then I had to get back home to study.

Kew

Then I was back at 1377 sitting on top of the refrigerator. Except it wasn't my house, it was the house of a little half-black girl who I had agreed to keep busy for a time.

We talked for a bit. She said that she had always wanted her mom to take her to Kew gardens. I said we might do that sometime.

She may have thought I meant that we will do it right now because she went away and didn't come back for a long time. Maybe she was getting ready.

Finally I couldn't wait any longer just sitting there on top of the refrigerator with nothing to do so I had to go back home and study.

I started to leave. She came back and was dissappointed that we were not going to Kew gardens. I explained that I had to study and that we would go some other time.

She sat down and started to cry about the times she had been left all alone.

I gave her a big hug to reassure her. Then I gave her little brother a hug as well so that he wouldn't feel neglected in the matter.

Monday 3 June MM XX IV

Grandpa Misico and the Turkish Wedding

Gayatri and I were in the Pike Street House. There was a whole lot more room in a couple extra rooms in the basement. They were all empty. But the rooms that were being used were filled with junk and dust.

We were sitting on the second floor of a house that was maybe like the Sheridan house or maybe like Open School.

There was a small folk wedding going on. Some of the ladies had put on these leather vests over their dresses and were doing a little folk dance, quite lackidasically.

Gayatri and I were sitting on the floor with our backs against the wall watching the dance. The TV was on in the background.

She was explaining the need to clean up the Pike St. house including throwing things away. I pointed out that there was all that other space and if we reorganized it there would be space for everything. I was afraid that she would get mad at me for suggesting it of course.

Debugging Downloads

We were at work. It was a long wide hall that was like the temporary area at Thermo King but more corporate.

I was the leader. I had an office at the end. I was getting some coffee and some sweet snacks. The syrup got on my cup and I tried to clean it off.

Some computers were set up on a picnic table in a tent outside in the parking lot, which was a lot like the TK parking lot.

One of my reports, who was a cross between Dan Smith and Trenton, was debugging the download.

I was also trying to set up a computer in the lab, which was also the break room, to debug the download.

I checked with him and one other lady who was working with him. I just wanted to make sure that they had a plan for what experiments they were going to do. I didn't want to push them to a specific promise because I knew that there were uncertainties.

Tue 4 June MM XX IV

The third bird.

There were 6 snakes/lizards and 6 ducks born all at the same time. 3 times we met them. Each time, 2 of the lizards and 2 of the ducks were there. The lizards each ate one duck. The ducks never struggled or put up any resistance.

Finally on the third time after one of the lizards had eaten one of the ducks I couldn't take it anymore. We were standing on the corner of Hamline and Pascal in St. Paul. I grabbed the last duck and decided to take it home with me. I knew I couldn't keep it forever and I wasn't sure what I was going to do in the sequel. I thought that babaka would think it was just like when I had ducky-duck.

Fri 7 Jun MM XX IV

I went farther east (except it was west) on my bicycle than ever before. I went down the river and along the shore, till the shore turned into bedclothes and a narrow path. I got to the end of the path and jumped accross a fence. The fence was very low. It was the fence to a childrens backyard in an urban residential neighborhood. It was all bright pastel colors like animation.

We went to a church event. I didn't really want to be there. They had their relics at the door, which were links of sausages. I picked some up becuase I was supposed to use them. There was a square hole high up in the wall with some asymetric lettering around it. I wondered what it meant.

I got tired of holding the relics and set them down on the ground. Someone from the church came and picked them up and took them back to the entrance where I had found them.

Finally we were able to go in. Everybody started running. Gayatri ran ahead of me. I thought I saw her sitting in one of the rows but it was someone else.

I was sitting with Clayton and someone else. Brad Ludwig was in the other room. We heard him speaking loudly. I couldn't make out what he was saying because others were speaking at the same time. I asked Clayton and Q. to tell me what he said. He came out and started talking to us. The upshot is that we all had to be 'broader', which was the consequence of them trying to do the same amount of work with fewer people.

Sat 8 Jun MM XX IV

IBM Workspace

I was sitting in IBM. I was on the floor in the middle of the u turn of a hallway. I was trying to do some work. I had lots of pens and drawing equipment all around me. Except that I had ripped two of my jeans already and the one that I was currently wearing was cut off above the knees, at an angle.

The Halls of Macalester

I wanted to get some coffee. I went looking for it. I went down a hallway that was in a U shape. It was like here the auditorium in Linwood was, was the outside hallway of the fine arts building at Macalester. I walked through and they had lots of art from their current students class. They were all pictures of gladiators fighting. They were all certainly better than me at figurative work. One of them had put a picture of someone doing thier makeup in the mirror and the gladiators were fighting only in the reflection.

Coffee in IBM

I had a jar of instant coffee under my desk. I went to get it. Water had leaked and made a coffee stain under the desk. The stain had spread accross the whole carpeted floor of the room. The room where there were some cubicles. I grabbed the jar of instant coffee wrapped it up in some rags and went to throw it away.

Under the catacombs

I went down to the basement. There were puddles of water in the intersections of the hallways that I tried to avoid. Someone else was there and I tried to avoid him as well. The ceilings got lower and lower and more rounded. There were metal gates in some areas. Eventually it was so small that I couldn't get through so I turned around and went back. I didn't get stuck.

Breaking through the Ice with an MG

We all had to leave. I went to get my car keys. I didn't know which car I had. I went out to the parking lot and the car key fob activated an MG midget at the end of the parking lot which was close to the building and far from the entrance. There was snow everywhere. There was ice over the car and I broke through enough to get in. Someone came and told me that I had to take some others with me. It was like a family of Porto Ricans or something. I backed up and tried to get the car to plow through the deep snow.

Mon 10 Jun MM XX IV

Snow

I was trying to make a path for mice to crawl from the outside through the door. We had some duct tubing bent appropriately like a periscope and we were packing snow around it. I sent my mom over to the other side of the house to get some duct tape that I knew I had there. She never came back. I continued trying to pack the snow around the ducting in front of the door and hold it up above the ground with the help of some kids who were playing in the snow.

C++

I was sitting at my computer at work. The room was like an elementary school classroom. There were benches with chairs. The computers on the benches in front of the chairs were crt. I did some refactoring of some templates. But when I changed the window size all the tabs became misalinged so I had to rebuild. I sat there the whole morning wondering if someone was going to be upset because I was wasting so much time rebuilding. But when the afternoon came around everyone was into team building activities and nobody asked me any questions about the progress of the delay.

Lunch

So I went off to lunch. But first I packed away my little weed pipe. It finally fit into a smaller case and I was pleasantly surprised. I got some change in case I had to pay something in the cafeteria. I actually had 2 $5 bills, which was more than enough. Also, when I am looking for change usually I find these oversize coins that are memorabilia only. This time I was able to get them all together and pack them away in storage.

I went to the cafeteria. They had some fruit. I guessed I would just get that. There was a baggy that in addition to some nice nuts and raisins also had grapes and a half a zucchini, but it was what was on offer so I picked it up anyway.

Rahim Allana told me that the pizza was free today so I figured that I would get that. I went ahead of the people at the counter because I didn't want anything from there. Brad Ludwig was talking to someone else but he knew I was there and handed me some silverware. I told him about the superstition of handing people knives.

Golden Chains

I was chained in the water to a rock. I tried everything to break the chain. In the center, at the ends of the chain. But it wouldn't break. Finally I dived under the water and pulled on the chain. Slowly the rock that the chain was tied to slid out of the wall that it was in. I then had to swim away with the weight of both the rock and the chain. It was all I could do to keep afloat but I managed it. The person who had chained me was very cavalier about my ability to escape.

Friday 14 June MM XX IV

Hold on to the paper

I was in a class. The teacher was giving us a business use case. She wrote a bunch of instructions on the blackboard. We were supposed to start putting our impression of it. The instructions led me to believe that we should give great attention to the format, layout and appearance of the document physically on the paper. I spent a long time thinking about it. It was hard for me to read the blackboard. Then I started putting a basic use case with a sequence diagram onto three sheets of 8 1/2 x 11 paper, landscape.

I didn't get very far by the time the exercise was over. The teacher asked me to show my work. But I had put the last two pages at the bottom of a pile of blank sheets. I was using scratch paper and so some of the sheets already had printing on one side and I was only using the other blank side.

I couldn't find the other two pages even though they were the ones that could show that I was thinking about content rather than just introduction.

Not even a footnote

We were in an old building. I found a latch in the wall. We let a drawer down on a string and brought it back up. When it came back up, it had lots of copper and many many cups and bowls of pottery. I thought we had made a significant archealogical discovery. I ran to get the archeologist lady who was giving tours in a different part of the building.

She said that these were all the work of one master's studio. And that they had a lot of other examples so it didn't seem to be that big a find. 'At least a footnote?' I asked.

Don't miss the boat

I had my admission forms to Macalester. I gave them to my father and I thought he had them. I went to get my suitcase. By the time I got back a huge line had formed. I waited in line. The line went quickly. When I got to the front of the line I couldn't find the papers. I looked for them but by that time the boat was leaving the dock. I had literally and metaphorically missed the boat.

Clayton was there waiting in line. Except that he had transitioned and was dressed in girl's clothes. He asked if it was OK. I said he looked quite sharp; it suited him.

Sun 16 Jun MM XX IV

Downtown St. Paul

I had to get downtown St. Paul to find the oyster card with the bend in it. I was going to ask the lost and found. I thought that I could identify it by saying that it had a bend in it.

I started walking down 7th street to downtown St. Paul. John Banks started walking with me. We talked about taking the bus or just walking. We decided to walk. We got about 2/3 of the way there and John was tired so we stopped to rest in an alley. I read some magazines that he had until he was ready to continue. We got to his work and he sat down at his desk. I tried to find a place where I could sit and there wasn't anybody. But everybody else from his work was starting to come in so I left on my own. Even though there was security getting in no one stopped me on my way out through the cafeteria.

Finally I decided it was just easier to buy a new oyster card.

Homeless with Fish

I didn't have a place to sleep. Sometimes I would check into a hotel but that was expensive. On weekdays there was an abandoned factory that I could sneak into but this was a weekend so I went to a shelter. I went upstairs. It was all wooden and they kept fish there. I didn't like touching the fish but the blanket was just big enough. In the morning they just had a small amount of bread and water for breakfast. The others got more but I figured since I hadn't paid I couldn't complain.

Finally I got a job and it was just enough to pay for an apartment downtown. My apartment was small but it looked out on the office buildings of downtown St. Paul.

Low res motorcycle

Got in my father's motorcycle from the garage at 1377. He had fixed it up so that it did have a key so I had to go back and get the key. I went away and came back. I came up the gentle slope. Then I went away and came back but this time I took the ragged slope and then I was spinning and falling. It was all like a low res 3D game.

Mon 17 Jun MM XX IV Week 25

Tue 18 Jun MM XX IV Week 25

Luke Skywalker and the butterfly

He was surrendering himself to the empire. The empire had pretty much defeated the rebels through sheer numbers. So he walked into their camp alone to surrender himself and was taken prisoner. As he walked into the camp you could see a single butterfly float away from him.

Prior to his surrender, he had been studying self-replicating machines. The butterfly was a robot with monitoring capabilities and the ability to make more of itself. They would be monitoring all the activities of the empire and reporting the activities back to the remaining rebels.

As they took him away on a ship to an unknown destination we only hope that some of the butterflies made it with him so that his position could be monitored.

Wed 19 Jun MM XX IV

Looking for gum to get back in the movie theatre

I left the movie theatre that my friends and I had gone to. The movie theatre was on the top floor of the complex. The complex was a little old and industrial. Not a modern shopping center. It was an article of faith that to get back into the movie theatre I had to have chewing gum. So I started to go down to the ground floor to buy some chewing gum.

I got lost a little on some of the top floors, as they had mazes of hallways, ramps and stairs going up and down in confusing order.

There were maintenance people pushing long carts at dangerous speed and nearly hitting myself and some of the others there.

Eventually I got down to the bottom floor where the concessions were.

I tried to get some gum out of the vending machine. I struggled to find change. At first I thought there was no gum in the machine. Then I thought I found it but when I got it it turned out to be something like jelly beans.

As I left I wondered why I needed chewing gum to get back in the theatre rather than my ticket?

Buying junk food at the british convenience store

I was in Britan. I was living a lone in an apartment on the main street. Across the street was a convenience store. I went over to get something mostly because I was bored. The shelves were unusually low; waist height. Not able to store as much as the head height ones in a regular store. It was as if they didn't care how much they were able to sell. There wasn't a lot there that was particularly interesting. For example, there was no pop.

There was even a large section of a shelf dedicated to books. But they were the kind of books that you used for staging like old readers digest rather than stuff you would actually read.

I looked at one of them and it was like an old cookbook and helpful hints for housewives. But it wasn't really, I was only the top half of the pages from that book and it was made to look aged which made even that half almost unreadable.

I noticed that they had a bar and I could have ordered pop from the bar but the owner was behind the counter helping other customers so I didn't want to interrupt him.

I thought about buying tobacco but resisted. They loose tobacco was on the shelves but the cigarettes were behind the counter.

Finally I picked up a bag of potato chips for want of anything else.

When I got to the counter I saw that they had toaster pastries behind the counter so I asked for that. It wasn't the regular brand name and I couldn't quite read it so I asked about it.

It was 'French' something. The owner added up the price in his head and told me GBP 1.45. I was going to give him a 5 pound note at first but managed to find exact change: two 50p two 20p one 5p.

Sat 22 Jun MM XX II

I thought that I had gotten a job. It was something mystical. I went over to the office. The office was on the second floor of Mechanics Arts in the southeast corner.

I went there. There was something to do with witches. The main warlock was there. I had to move a big chair around him. It turned out that I didn't get the job. I left the room and sat in a different chair.

I thought to myself I need to get a job. Or at least look like I was looking for one. I'll have to find the paper. But it's Saturday. I went looking for the Saturday paper.

I went down by the airport. I saw that there were some lights trailing behind a plane coming in to land.

At first I thought it was just the way the clouds were trailing behind. But then I realized that it was three planes that had crashed together and were falling. One of the planes was smaller than the other two and was a DC-10. It very clearly said DC-10 on the side.

I turned away as the planes fell and tried to get out of the area. I followed a number of people who were also leaving along the fence, and into the tram.

I tried to go up a hill. It was a very steep hill and there was a rope to hold on to as you went up. A voice was saying something about Monaco or some other country.
