Sun 23 Jun MM XX IV

No Fight

We were fighting giant letters. Symbols carved out of stone. The battle would be 1-1; there would be one person removed on each side. First the Americans went. When they were done, the UK went. The UK were almost finished when the Germans started. I went under the water and found a sheet of plastic. I lifted up the sheet of plastic that was stopping the water from receding. The water started receding and the Germans realized that they didn't have to fight after all.

Future Nazis

This was all happening in a far future where the goals of Nazis and other anti-semites were being realized to create a genetically engineered culture. Ostensibly for the improvement of mankind but horrible to live in.

We were on a ship. There were many of us captured and sitting like prisoners on a troop transport. The nazi captain came in and started to show us the effects of their genetic engineering work. One of the prisoners, a Scotsman, had been put through their machines. There was now skin hanging off his face like a veil, He was many pounds heavier and twice his width. And he had fur and hooves like a goat now. He was clearly not happy but the captain made out like this was great.

The lieutenant came through and started to explain how we were all going to be organized into different fighting units. There were like six ranks above us and were were being organized into the bottom three ranks. But he made it sound like being selected into the first of those bottom three ranks would be a priviledge. To be a robust goat man like the Scotsman had been made into. He had a name for it and tried to write it on the whiteboard but it was too long so he just put an abbreviation.

I whispered to the person next to me "fight and attack?". There was no answer. Then one of the guards came over so I didn't say anything more. I thought that if they asked me what I was saying I would tell them that I said "warm in the back".

Then Dan Smith and I escaped through a side door. We went running down many corridors and rooms. They were all decorated in black and white only. Everything was black and white only and I commented on this.

Eventually we came to a room. On the left was a door and on the right was a window. We went through the window into a greenhouse type area that was open to the outside. The outside was all desert here. And there were guards. They were genetically modified to be like collections of rocks that could fly. Like if the rock guy from the fantastic four was compressed into a flying saucer shape and some of the rocks at the edges were only held together loosely.

I flew through the window. I was able to avoid the flying rock guards because I was able to fly higher.

The desert gave way to grass. There was a caravan of a noblewoman (in the future nazi regime). I flew down and grabbed her dress. I flew away from them and started to put the dress on for a disguise. It was easy to get the first part on but hard to get the left arm on. My left fingers got caught in a piece of string and the wrist and I spent a long time getting them loose.

Finally I flew away in the dress. The grass started to give way to woodlands. I flew down to the ground. I decided that I shouldn't be in the most rugged, dirty parts because it wasn't likely that a noblewoman would be there. So I stuck to the flat grassy areas but stayed by the trees for some sense of being hidden.

I then came to a more residentail area and was going up and down sidewalks and small trails past houses.

Someone else was in the same area and it was the noblewoman whose dress I had stolen. She would be able to recognize me so I had to avoid her.

Mon 24 Jun MM XX IV

Cat on the fence

I went to Thermo King even though I no longer had a job there. My cat came with me. Because the cat always did and that was its routine. I would go into work and she would go back. But this time I didn't go into work so she was confused. We sat there on the lawn next to each other for a while.

Then we turned around to go back home. My cat always went back along a little wire fence. So we did it that way again. She was confused because the timing was different. She got halfway and then I climed on the fence to help her and together we got most of the rest of the way.

Rajni

I had also stopped school. I had to explain to Gayatri's mother that this was an unusual situation where I had a double loss. But I hadn't left Gayatri financially destitute yet. That was in our living room in Netherford.

Looking through my fathers papers

I went back home to my apartment which was like Clayton's Father's apartment near Como park. I was reviewing his papers. There were written on yellow legal pads. There were some notes about how we could SQL into his investment information. I thought that he didn't have anything left in his investements. I thought that I had done that before on the computer but couldn't remember the details. There might have been more information in other papers. All the papers were piled up in disorder on the side of my bed.

Field trip cancelled for rain

I went to school only for the field trip. When the field trip was cancelled because of rain I just went home. We were in a glass 3 season porch looking out over a creek and some woods. The street was to the west and exit was to the south. It was the same place Thermo King was that I had taken my cat to.

Wed 26 June MMXXIV

Brad Retires

I went up to a table where Brad Ludwig and Les Rustad were sitting in a large room. Brad asked me a question I didn't understand. He said "Didn't you go to the 10:45 meeting?" I said no. He followed me as I walked away from the table and he explained that he was retiring.

I went out down the hallway to the library. I thought about how I didn't actually know any of the people who were walking around the halls. Everyone was part of the new regime and now the old regime was over.

I thought to myself that I'd better stop just hanging out in the library and actually sit at my desk and do some work.

Th 27 Jun MM XX IV

TTY

I was explaining to someone how we used to connect on a tty over dial up modems and how there were still some places that had retro support for that.

At the dentist

I was at the dentist. He was working on my teeth. I could see my teeth laid out like a keyboard. One of the teeth was missing. One of them was near where he was working. I could see in the display as he put extra pain killer on the exposed tooth. Then I said that I had to go to the bathroom. When I went to the bathroom I took out some nicotine gum and put it between my gums. Then I realized that it was silly to think that I could go back to get dental work with gum in my mouth.

Fri 28 Jun MM XX IV

Sat 29 Jun MM XX IV

Heavy Metal High School

This was a TV show. It was washed out color. A young girl was complaining about how boring her school was. It was like faded ashes. That is, until the heavy metal band came. Then the scene went back to full color. One of the band members was in full costume. They were helping out the science teacher; helping to teach the class. They were interspersing just enough science lesson in what they were saying to avoid the science teacher stopping them. But mostly what they were talking about was their heavy metal version of the Kabalah. He had a tee shirt that showed thier version of the Kabalah tree of life. It was basicallly upside down. They had God-above-man as Malkuth on top and God-within-man as Yesod below that. Then the three triangles corresponded to soul, mind, and heart. They called them chakras.

Transport Testing

I went to work. Work was in an old field in Bloomington. I thought it ironic that I was working near where my aunt and uncle used to live. I went out to the factory floor. They had a new trailer set up to do testing for people who were training. I climbed up on top. There was a spray can there. The person who was showing me around explained that it was used to cool the place down below freezing when they were doing the tests. There were curtains all around to try to keep the cold in when they did the tests.

We went accross the street and looked at the setup from the sidewalk. There was a manikin set up to look like a technician. I made a joke about how the guy who was showing me around was better looking.

View from a Castle

I went north from that place. You could see a map of where Scotland had connected to mainland France because of all the immigrants who had settled there and the channel had been filled in with housing. The map was in multiple colors. Then I took my bicycle up a grassy hill to an old castle. When you looked down at the same place it was just a little stream and there was an old bridge going across it. Some people were fishing and there were fishing lines running accross the grass that I had to run across with my bicycle.

I turned back north to a busy street and then went back west along the busy street and around a corner where there was …

Spagetti in the Auditorium

… an auditorium that had a kitchen in it.

Gayatri and Li Xun had been boiling spagetti in a big pot. There were lots of small children running around. They were talking in the adjacent room. I came in and saw some spagetti in a pot so I thought that they had already eaten and I started to get this for myself. I pored the leftover noodles onto my plate. The water that they were boiling in had taken so much starch that it started to congeal. I thought that I had invented a nice dessert if you added sugar and something else to it.

Fri 5 July MM XX IV

I went over to a cave to smoke a pipe. This was in a forest a ways away from the road. A lady came over and started talking to me. She said that she was glad that I actually kept talking; many left. She had a fancy car and said that she needed me to upgrade her seat belts as they had been lost. They used to be Jade. First I confirmed with her that she still had seat belts in her car and that it was safe. Then I confirmed with her that I could put gold foil on the new ones that she bought. It would be my first design commission and I was very excited. I told her it would take 24 hours after start so the total time would depend on when we started.

Sat 6 July MM XX IV

lost luggage at open school

I had left all my pencils and was looking for them. My backpack was empty and was in an empty suitcase that I was carrying around with me. Open School was like the second floor of Mechanic Arts connected to a basement in 1885 that was like an elementary school area in Linwood.

5 PM math EXAM

The math exam was at 5 PM. Who puts a math exam at 5 PM? You can obviously only do math in the morning. I was worried that I would get tired by then but I was keeping up pretty well so far. My father started driving me. We were driving away from Macalester along Macalester avenue towards St. Clair. Then I started to feel sleepy and I decided it would be OK if I napped a little in the car on the way to the exam.

5 PM civil Rights Meeting

The house was old. It was like a late 60s/early 70s stereotype of a working class house. There was little furniture because it was only used for meetings. The kitchen was servicable and had the kind of things you would have for a community meeting – plastic cups and so on.

Past the living room there was a door to another room. The door was closed because they were organizing in there. So I didn't try to go in.

There was a bulletin board near the entrance. It was pretty full but they wanted me to add a flyer for information about our 5:00 meeting. All I had was old pieces of scratch paper and a marker but I tried to use those.

The person, Bob Ferguson, who was speaking at the 5:00 meeting was following behind me and telling me what to write. He had been someone important in the civil rights movement back in the day.

They thought that his presence added gravitas to their meeting but he obviously thought it added even more gravitas than they did.

Flying from Nazis

It was large wide halls. Like the shopping at Covent Garden but even larger and with a more French feeling design.

It was like 1984. I started to fly away. I was able to fly up and break through a window. But then I started to fall again. I hit a corner of one of these large French shopping halls. I continued on foot. Unfortunately the party that was searching for me happened into the same room just as I was getting there.

Australian Ambassador at the Hotel lobby desk

The desk at the hotel lobby was a place that could get us to escape away to a different country. We had to interogate this lady but she wouldn't tell us anything. It turned out that she was the Australian Ambassador.

Sun 7 Jul MM XX IV

Track King no longer has an ID

Q. from Thermo King called me up to tell me that TrackKing no longer had an order number. You wouldn't be able to get it through service parts. There were a lot of multi colored ribbons in a drawer and I took some of them.

I walked along the hallway. There were some trails of water in the hallway that I tried to avoid. Gayatri was walking alongside me going to a different room to the right instead of the room at the end where I was going. I wanted to tell her that TrackKing no longer had a service parts number but she kept talking about her stuff so I decided that I would try to tell her later.

The Coffee pot is broken

I got to the room. It was bright and clear and a little yellow. Like the music extention at 1885.

There was glass all over the floor. Someone had dropped the coffee pot and Brad Ludwig was there trying to figure out who had done it. I got down on my knees to look at the pieces on the floor under the table. There was one metal piece missing. We were wondering why someone would have broken it and taken that piece.

There was also a bunch of little toys that we used to play with. Fidget gadgets and the like. Including a pear shaped yo-yo that was mine. I decided it would not be the right time to take it back so I left it there on the floor under the table.

The Printer is broken

Outside the room, it was like somewhere in northern Minnesota. There was some equipment on a table that was like a picnic table. Including a printer. The printer wasn't working. Someone had been messing with it and had taken the cover off and put it back on incorrectly. I put it back on correctly and then it started working again.

There are eels in the filter

Then I noticed that there was a bunch of weeds and other growth in a big plastic basket. So I decided that I should clean it out. I dumped it over but it didn't all come out. I shook it and it fell apart completely. But at least I got rid of the weeds and fungal growth and eels.

Mon 8 July MM XX IV

Playing Ditch; a glitch in the matrix

I was running through some large white rooms. Some of my friends, maybe Blake Medelman and Tony Dunlop were there. They were throwing a little piece of paper folded up in a triangle as a game. I grabbed the piece of paper and I ran out of the room.

I went out the back gate of 1377 and west along the alley.

I then turned south on Albert St. Accross the street where the house on the corner would have been the dream curtain failed to be placed. Behind it was just black and white pulsing tubes like trees all intertwined in multiple dimensions.

Free Jazz McDonalds

They started the free jazz mcdonanlds thing but then never got past the first line. Then it was a happines and cyanide cartoon where they were just going to 'take over the lower four'. Meaning that they were going to spread their values to all the other fast food services.

SPI

They just said 'Sun'. Then when I kept asking they just didn't say anything and turned around and started leaving early.

Sat 13 July

Flooded Indian School

I was visiting a school in India. There was flooding. And this meant that everyone was walking around on the paths between classes with water up to their necks.

I asked if some of them wouldn't just use the first level. They said that they had many clever ways of avoiding the water. I watched as some of them emerged from underground tunnels.

I got a little wet in the process.

We then had to go feed snakes.

The people who never stop moving

I was sitting on a bridge looking out at a lot of fast moving traffic. I was thinking about how AI was accellerating everything. Imagine what you think life would be like in the year 3000. Then imagine that AI will allow us to accellerate to bring that about by 2200.

I then had an idea for a story, which I explained to Gayatri as she was driving me around through parks.

In the future, everyone had to keep moving all the time. It was a crime to stop moving or sleep. Everyone had to stay distracted at all times so that they could never pose a threat to the elite. Only the elite were allowed to sleep but nobody else even knew that. They were able to go without sleep because medical science had advanced so much that they had drugs that allowed it.

Then one day, our hero who was working on the machines that they used to keep people moving. Conveyor belts and drones and the like. Discovered a way that he could appear to keep moving but actually be sleeping. He told his girlfriend about this. Together they started to sleep at nights. Together they started to understand how the elite were controlling their society. Together they started to craft a plan to stop it.

Trying to teach class with Gautham

This was the second class, the following week. The previous week's class hand ended with a fun quiz including questions like what hell was like.

I wanted to start this time by repeating that.

There were 7 categories of questions, with a handful of questions under each category.

I wanted to start this class with a repeat of that quiz.

I wanted to choose the questions to ask randomly.

There was of course no time to prepare a tool to create the random selection so I just hoped that I would be able to wing it. I also had very little idea what to do for the rest of the class.

I thought I had some dice. I looked through my backpack and overturned the pockets onto the table but all I could find was a few mismatched six sided dice.

We started to write the questions out on the whiteboard. Or at least the high level categories because there wasn't really time to write them all out.

But the whiteboard markers didn't show up very well and I had to go searching for better ones. I didn't find any. Gautham found that they would show up if you wrote on the varnished wooden pegboard that was behind the whiteboard. I was concerned that it wouldn't be able to be erased from there. He was like, what to do?

I finally gave up on trying to randomize the questions and just picked one to ask of someone in the class. I had also wanted to randomize who to ask but that couldn't happen either.

I noticed that there was another class being given in the same classroom behind some glass dividers that had been set up. It was hard to tell who was in our class and who was in the other one.

Sun 14 Jul MM XX IV :Bastille Day:

X

I was going to meet my father. But first I was going to get my pipe from my secret place that I had hidden it.

To get it I would have had to go around three sides of a square: East, then North, then West again to meet him. But I didn't have time to pick it up so I just went straight north and figured that I would get it later.

I didn't have a lot of time for sleep because this was all happenning in the middle of the night. I was trying to think when I would be able to catch up on sleep.

Being Driven by my Father

I got into the car. I was in the backseat on the passenger side. Dennis was driving. I was concerned because he was so old, and dead. Should I allow myself to be driven by a dead person? We drove down a highway that went downwards on a long curving slope. The road was cut into steep cliffs. If the cliffs had disappeared you would have seen into the dream fabric.

King of the Hill in a Parking Lot

We were on top of a building in a parking lot near a shopping mall in the winter. It was like being back at open school.

We grabbed somebody's car. We started to drive them away. The others stepped out for a moment so I convinced the driver to take me where I wanted to go.

At work without Pants

I was at work. Work was a one level office building north of Rosedale. I woke up there and realized that I shouldn't have come in so early. I had to go all the way back home and come back in again because I needed to put my pants on.

Winona on Wednesday?

I was thinking about the next things that I should maybe do. I thought about going to Winona to ask them what their projects were.

Then I realized that they would think that was strange and be hesitant about giving information.

Becuase I should get information from my own company first. Asking Watlow for information on what they were doing was a poor substitute for not myself knowing what my own company was doing.

I was driving around the countryside toward Winona. Or maybe it was near Rosedale. I was recollecting how I had thought about getting a job in Watlow. But my wife would never agree. The cost of living there was nice, if you had income like for the Twin Cities. But of course your income would be correspondingly smaller.

Wed 17 Jul MM XX IV

Party with S. W. Emerson

I was on my way to a party. I was taking the bus there. My phone got stuck in some music/video mode. A kid in the seat in front of me told me to turn it off. I said that I didn't know how. He said to swipe right and then use the 'power up' (swipe up) move. It worked! The phone entered a mode where I could adjust what the cursor keys and other special keys did. The cursor keys were minor indentations in the plastic of the screen. So that they didn't interfere with looking at it. But you could feel the indentation if you wanted to use the keys.

A Japanese man got on the bus and handed me a sheet of papers in a folder. The folder opened at the narrow end of the papers instead of the wide end. That was my phone now. I looked at the papers but they were mostly in Japanese. So I put the folder in my backpack in the hope that it would turn back into my phone. It did.

I got off the bus. I went up the elevator of the building. Then I realised that I had gotten off the bus one stop too early. On the East side of the Washington avenue bridge instead of the West side.

So I went back and started walking to the correct building. Sarah Emerson got off the bus behind me and started talking to me. At first I thought that she was mocking me. She was going to the same party. She was like, 'Oh, who are you going to be there with, like Dan Smith and Sean Kelly?'

I let her catch up to me and we held hands.

She was lying on the floor in the building. Her head was like a glowing green jelly and her face was just painted on in thin black ink.

A man came up to us and gave us something.

Th 18 July MM XX IV

There was an earthquake. We were watching the reporting on TV. They were showing the waves coming in with repillian monsters just under the surface rolling over the rocks because of the quake.

Fri 19 July MM XX IV

Luis Camacho

Luis Camacho and I used to go walking along the road near the water when we wanted to take a break from work but didn't want people realizing that that was what we were doing.

His leg was hurting. I asked if he wanted to take a pill for it. He said he couldn't because he was already on another medication. I suggested that he use arnica. He had never heard of it before.

We went closer to the shore where there was a food truck. The food truck started to pull away as I jumped to the dock. I burned my hand.

Watch in bed

I was sitting in bed. The bed was in a restaurant. It was early in the morning so the restaurant was nearly empty. The waitress was able to devote a lot of attention to me. She brought over my watch. She said that she had set the time. She apologized because it was off by less than a second. I joked that her tip got smaller by a cent then.

Saturday 20 July MM XX IV

Taking a shower in the dorm

I was in some kind of a college dormatory. It was very open and there were several places where water ran through it. I went to take a shower and was walking past some of the other students.

Turkey Sandwich with Gayatri

We went to the cafeteria to get lunch. Gayatri went into the sandwich section. You went around a U-shape to select your sandwich items.

It was a very narrow space between the outside edges of the U and the island in the middle.

I started to follow her but soon realized that all the options were nonveg. So I left and went to look for what else they had.

Gayatri asked if I wanted some juice. They had a plastic bottle of orange juice and a plastic bottle of grapefruit juice sticking up out of a bench in order to show their options. After a moment's hesitation I said that I wanted the grapefruit juice and she picked it up for me.

She came with a small bowl overfilled with some dark pocket breads. I went to get another for myself. She said that we should just share that one. I went to look for what else they had. But all they had was just different kinds of bread, most of which were too large.

In the same corner, made of shelving, in the middle of the cafeteria, there were offerings of dinner settings. They were all pretty much the same. They were supposed to be some kind of mexican design but they didn't look mexican in any way.

Password changed to 'LOVERS'

I was in a class at another school. This was the kind of school that you were only supposed to go into for a couple of years but it was looking like it was going to take me a lot longer. I didn't feel like I fit in there.

I was in the back left of the classroom. I was tilted 90 degrees to the rest of the students as if I was lying in bed and they were all sitting in chairs.

I was a senior student but I was nowhere near where the teachers were and I wondered how I would ever get there.

The professor was giving a talk on some cryptography thing. He stated that the password in the system was (whatever it was) and wrote it down on the chalkboard with each character filling a place shown by underscores:

X Y Z W _ _ _ _

Then he opened up the system and checked the password.

I had been working on the system and had changed the password, not realizing that anyone else was going to be using it.

When he checked the password in the system he found that it had been changed to 'LOVERS'. He wrote it on the board.

L O V E R S

I had to confirm from the back of the class that indeed that was the new password. I felt very embarassed both for being the only one to speak in class and for having changed it on my own.

Sun 21 July MM XX IV

Running home at night

I couldn't sleep and went far away from home. Home was 1377. I was near downtown St. Paul. I started running back to home to try to get there before the morning.

It was uphill. I went past some streets in the Crocus Hill/Selby-Dale neighborhood that I wasn't familiar with.

Soon enough I was near Hamline Avenue. There was some water on the road but I passed it easily.

Call from San Francisco

I went back to bed. I woke up to a call from San Francisco.

I had been working with ¿Shell as a contractor. On Friday I had been involved in some meetings that discussed the company meeting with a third party supplier in San Fransisco the following Wednesday. I had said that I would be available because I was pretty sure that the company I was working with was not going to go trough with it or in any case was not going to keep me on the project.

I figured that I could give a response for the time of the meeting on Monday, since there was a good chance it would be cancelled by then. But sure enough, here was the person who was coordinating the meeting calling to say that they needed at specific time. So I told them 11:30 thinking that if it did go through, it would give me the maximum time to get from the airport while still being a convenient morning time for them.

She was there in the same room with her boss. They discussed it and confirmed that 11:30 would be acceptable.

I thought that would be the end of the phone call. The connection kept going in and out. They kept talking in the background. It was pretty clear that they were talking about something that didn't apply to me. But they didn't say goodbye.

A great wind started to blow the back door open. I had to try to close the door with one hand while holding on to the phone with the other hand.

The third, heavy wooden door was half off its hinges.

Explaining Telematics

We were sitting outside on the slope of a hill. It was a meeting of all these people involved in the San Franciso project. They were talking about how all their remove device were going to be updated. They were thinking that each device would have to talk to every other device. I was thinking that they could each be independently updated from a central source.

I stared to speak critically, but then stopped myself and started over with how important the issue that they were bringing up was and how there might be other ways to address it.

I still didn't think I would end up going to San Francisco on Wednesday.

Mon 22 Jul MM XX IV

Grading papers in the living room

I was grading papers in the living room at 1377 in front of the stereo.

As I started to grade the papers I realized that I had gotten the first question wrong. It was much harder than I thought it was. I had thought that it was a question about logarithms and that the answer was about 0.91. But you were actually supposed to take the sum over certain groups of divisors of those logarithms so it could have been something else.

I felt bad that I had not realized what a hard questions the students were probably stuck on burning up a lot of time in the test.

Nefarious Germans in the bedroom

I went back to the bedroom of 1377. It was completely dark. I was sitting on the floor with my back up against the wall. The window was open, in the sense that it was missing the glass and was just completely open to the outside. Some strangers started milling around outside. They were speaking German. Then they saw me inside and came in through the window. They said that they were hoping to have sex in this deserted building. I told them that they had better talk to Leila as she was the owner. They didn't wait around for her to come home but she eventually did come home.

Copy/Paste, with Aliens

I was typing. I was able to type so fast. Everything was clear and free and easy. I was just flying with my typing speed. I was typing so fast that my fingers couldn't keep up with me.

I was creating fields out by a crossroads in the north of town. It was summer and there was a lot of pollen and insects in the air.

Some aliens got into the scene. I did undo, revert, cut and paste from a previous version. But if I missed even a single one, They would grow and come back again.

This is how they came into our world. Through the intersities between the scenes in stories.

I had to go all the way back to a version where there were none of them.

Community College

I was in a community college. The classes were really full. Nobody there was particularly exceptional. Nobody was particularly wealthy or well-dressed. They were just there to get a degree and move on.

Autofascism

Wed 24 July MM XX IV

Debug

I was sitting in a room. The room was like the living room of Garnet + Sophie's in Lake Crystal. I was sitting at a small table surrounded by papers. I was working at a computer. I was trying to get the application running so that I could debug it.

Then I went to the room next door, which was where the kitchen at Garnet and Sophie's in Lake crystal would have been. This was larger, like a common room at a school. There was large table there that sat several people. I sat there.

There was a young man who was looking into some management training that the company was encouraging. The company was a little ma + pa shop like Access Specialties. I knew I couldn't stay there very long. I recommended that he think about what he was trying to accomplish with his training. If it was just regular project management, the brochure that he was looking at even referenced them. We finally settled on 'Logistics Management'. I asked if he knew linear algebra. He said no. I told him that he would have to learn it if he was going into logistics management!

There was a lady there, an older French lady. She came and stood to the left side of the table. She really liked lavender and put a little jar with some lavender on the table. I – somewhat jokingly – covered it up with a piece of paper. Well really it was too much for me. Then to recover, I made out like I just wanted to use the piece of paper to get the smell of lavender.

An eastern european gentleman was sitting at the far left corner of the table, working on his computer. He was further along in understanding the companies programs than I was. He asked me if I could help him debug a problem. I said sure as this was a good way for me to learn. He explained that there were two objects in his code that were supposed to react to an event. He knew that one of the objects was not going to react because of a different problem that he already knew about. But he didn't understand why the other object didn't react.

Escaping Nazi Prison Camp with a Stolen Watch

Fri 26 July MM XX IV

Elton John Concert

We were at an Elton John concert. He was going over all his old standards. Or at least a rendition of the chorus of each, not necessarily the whole thing.

We left in the intermission. The others were complaining that it was too loose, too informal and that they were dissapointed.

Sat 27 July MM XX IV

Smoking Weed in the Morning

Clayton was coming over later that day. But I got up in the morning and took one hit out of my pipe. I had to blow the smoke out of the window in the living room of 1377. I felt very high for a very brief time. By the time he came over I had pretty much come down and didn't feel off center because of being stoned.

I was waiting on a road in the dark under trees.

Going to Lunch with a Coffee Machine

I had a coffee machine under my arm. It was a square box with a couple of buttons and knobs in it. It was bulky and just a little bit larger than convenient to carry.

I was going to go to lunch. I decided not to go to the vending machine on the floor that I usually go to. I went down one floor to where there was a full cafeteria. The coffee machine started to make noises. Loud enough to bother the people around me. I twisted one of the dials to release the pressure and it stopped making noises for a little while.

I went past the seats where chinese food was served to the vending machines at the far end.

I stopped to pour the coffee into a sink. When I poured the coffee into the sink, I was also urinating into the sink. A lot of urine came out and it was bright yellow almost green. I thought to myself that I shouldn't have drunk so much mountain dew the night before.

Some people came by and I rushed to button up the blue, white and red knit jacket that I was wearing.

Swapping Rental Cars with the Turnures

We were getting a new rental car. We were in a large room, like an art supplies area. There were tables in the middle and shelving around the sides.

Mike dumped the keys out on the table. Specific keys, which were tagged with plastic tags in different colors were critical, and the rest were just there. I undid the keyholder and then started putting the keys back onto the keyholder, taking care not to lose the critical ones.

I went over to a different table. There were pictures and business cards on it. I started to collect some of the ones that we might need. We needed some of them for the rental car but not necessarily all of them. Jimmy was standing by the table and we discussed some of the pictures of his family that were there.

Beside another table were some of the paintings that I had done. We had to decide which of them to keep and which not to. Most of them were too large and didn't need to be kept so I set them aside.

I then went over to the shelving. One of the people who was helping me was going through some art supplies that were on the shelving and deciding which of them to take for the new rental car. I told him I would do that and he could go over to some other part.

Traffic Accident on the highway

We were in an apartment. It was like it was on the north west side of Snelling and University but it was a little more upscale. I had to go get a rental car.

I was driving back along the highway with the rental car. There was a loud ding! alarm and the car indicated that there was less than 10% gas. It also told me – because it was a smart dashboard – that the nearest gas station was at the second exit. I decided I would take exit and fill up. It wouldn't do to run out of gas on the way back to them. The lanes started to merge. The rightmost lanes of the highway were closed off for construction and the highway was down to one lane. I had to suddenly merge over. I was merging blind because I had failed to adjust my left mirror properly. I could only see in the rear view mirror. I made it to the leftmost lane but then through no fault of my own someone hit me from behind and then I bumped the person in front of me. There was a large number of cars pulled over on the left side of the highway all in the accident. I pulled over as well even though I could have driven on because it was the right thing to do.

I dreaded the thought that I didn't have my insurance with me because we were travelling and I had left it at home. If anyone asked I would just have to tell them that I would get it for them later.

I did a quick check of the car and could see that there was no visible damage so I at least wouldn't be in trouble with the rental car company.

I tried to use my phone but it was stuck in ads. I got mad at it. It started to bend and warp. A kid came along and threw it in the river that was running just next to the highway.

I realized that I was in a foreign town without identification or a cell phone and I was naked down to my underwear.

There was only one thing to do in a situation like this. I stretched my arms before me pointed them at the sky across the river and started flying.

Flying through Tunnels

Instead of flying up I flew down into a tunnel. The tunnel just went down and down. It was square and painted green. It could have been in a high school if it had been in a different place.

I got to the bottom where there was a little landing and the tunnel got too narrow to get through. Someone was sitting there.

I turned and stared going back up. They were now full hallways like school hallways.

In a room off of the hallway some people were fighting. Except it wasn't a fight like a fight; it was like a cartoon fight or in batman.

I looked back along the corridor to check that my mother wasn't watching because I didn't think she would understand the fight.

Sun 28 July MM XX IV

Eating the sweets

It was the end of the hallway where they send you after the dream is done. It opens up on a high floor of a skyscraper over a futuristic city.

In the last office before the elevator, we were in the back seat of a car. We had to squeeze together four of us in the back and two or three in the front. Gayatri was next to me and the rest were all women.

On the shelf in the office were sweets. And not just little mints and hard candies like you have in offices. I wouldn't have felt bad taking one of those. But rather large pudding and mousse. Like something you would buy for a special party you were going to have at the office after work.

I turned away from them because I saw that they weren't just for causal visitors. But Gayatri picked up a spoon and started eating the largest one.

She pretty much finished it and left me only to lick the bowl.

I called one of the people in the front seat 'Alex'. Her name was Alexandria and she didn't like being called Alex. I paused, and then thought to call the other person in the front seat. But I accedentally called them Alex again. Faux Paux.

Mon 29 July MM XX IV

John Banks.

I went to John's house. He and Norma were both very sad because they couldn't afford the house. I asked if they had paid off the mortgage. He said something that led me to believe that he didn't understand the concept of paying off the mortgage; it was more like rent you paid in perpetuity. I said that they had been in the house so long that I had just assumed that it was already paid off. So don't get mad at me for asking; it is a reasonable question because there are people who do that even if you haven't.

He asked me to go into the next room. He said I had bad breath because I had neglected to brush my teeth. I asked him if he had any toothpaste.

Sat 3 Aug MM XX IV [Detroit]

Alpine Holiday with Swimming

We went up a winding snowy road in the mountain. Then finally when you got along one turn of the road you saw the whole vista before you. It was a beautiful scenic mountain view with the mountains and chalet going off into the distance. It was unbelievable how much of it there was. The chalet were slightly east asian rather than alpine in character.

I turned to Gayatri and made a joke about it not seeming real; they had just put a big billboard of a postcard in our way because it looked so perfect.

Some dogs came up to us and greeted us at the corner where the road turned. And other people were coming to help us.

We went to a swimming pool. Gayatri got in to the pool with all her clothes on pushing her large grey suitcase in front of her in the water. We were all supposed to meet at the shallow end of the pool. I jumped in the water and started to take my sweater off while under water. I went a long way down while doing so before coming back up again.

Shopping for Onion Soup with Lazy Attendants

We were in a grocery store. It might have been the old Red Owl on Grand. Gayatri was looking for a can of cream of mushroom soup to make some dish with. But the only can of cream of mushroom soup that we could find was nonveg. I went over to the next aisle and found an off brand can of cream of onion soup that appeared to be vegetarian. I brought it back and asked Gayatri if that one would work in a pinch.

The attendant who was helping us was moving very slowly. And when we heard her talking to her colleagues she was complaining about how much work she was expected to do. Apparently they were hiring more attendants in order to be able to do all the work. Because every single one of them moved about 30% slower than in any other place. So rather than just hire people who moved at a normal pace they were hiring more people. I didn't want to tell her that she should probably just pick up the pace a bit.

Cleaning the Kitchen with Racist Chef

We were in a kitchen. It may have been Aunt Virginia's kitchen, but the dining room in the next room was much larger and longer than hers was. And the dining room led to a living room and then out the front door instead of turning to get the living room like Aunt Virginia's did.

The chef that they had hired

Clearing the Sidewalk of Ice

.. while listening to my Father talk about his retirement.

Thursday 8 Aug MM XX IV [Midland MI]

Old World Pizza

We went to visit Old World Pizza. The walls hadn't been painted. Eric was talking about making a mark on the wall near the door for each day of operation. I said he looked tired. He said I looked tired too. I offered to paint the wall. We could put a calendar on the wall and instead of just marking the days he could indicate each day separately. He said he already had different plans for the wall. I had been going to just get some primer and paint it thickly white then paint the claendar over.

I went flying through the kitchen. There were so many people cooking so many things. And that was all just the prep; they hadn't even opened yet.

As I left they had put wallpaper on all the walls. It was a nice wallpaper but it made the place look more enclosed.

I went out to the parking lot to get my car.

Wind elemental

I was in the bedroom of 1377. I saw that the Neuenfeldt's garage was on fire. I ran out to warn them. There was a little twister – a djinn – a wind elemental – in the yard that was causing the damage. I determined to fight it with magic – pure will – until it subsided. Then I ran to the front to go to their door and warn them. But someone else had already informed them and they were off to take care of it.

Aftermath

Somehow the fire had burned down Old World Pizza. Everyone from the town was gathered outside to throw items into the recycling trucks as they went by on the street. They took their recycling very seriously.

Fri 9 Aug MM XX IV

Office Visitor

Some dignitary came to my office. I had an office in the university. It was very messy and had many books piled up as well as clothes that I hadn't taken home. I wasn't expecting him. He was supposed to judge me for some kind of award. I hosted him but I didn't expect the award as I was unprepared.

Office Cleaning

I started cleaning my office. I was able to put a lot of the books back on the shelf. One of the books had some old cigarettes in it. It had a reference to an interesting subject. I thought to myself, "No, I can't start going down another rabbit hole." and closed the book.

I piled a good amount of the clothes into two backpacks. Including a lot of socks and two pair of gloves.

There was a bracelet with a design of pearl shapes. Two or three pearl shapes in a row, and then two coming out on each side. Then two or three more in line and another two coming out on each side.

Then I left for home.

School Bridge

The office led to a bridge accross an open courtyard like a shopping mall. It was winter. One thing I didn't have after packing all those things from my office into the backpacks was headphones. So I had to just go over a song in my head. I had to be careful not to click my shoes on the ground in time with the song in my head or people would think it strange.

The bridge led to an elevator.

Train

Down the elevator and then into a train. The train went down a hill and then along a river. There was a story of how there had been some kind of labor action involved on the train line. It was famous in that neighborhood anyway.

Hindu Story

We sat on the square wooden bridge platform where the train and the road met up with the river that came in at an angle. Someone who was sitting there with a group of us, cross legged on the bridge, told about a story he attributed to the Hindus. When you pass from the heaven of fire to the heaven of earth, the God [mumble] gets notified. And when you pass from the heaven of earth to the heaven of air, the god [mumble] gets notified. But when you pass from the heaven of swimming (water) to the next heaven, the god [mumble] doesn't get notified. Which is why hindu families pray every day to that god letting them know that they are passing from the heaven of swimming ahead of time.

Under the Bridge

I went under the bridge. The ice was staring to melt so it was very wet. A lady came up to me and showed me the design on the arches that held up the bridge. It was exactly the design on the bracelet that I had. She asked where I got the bracelet. I said that I thought one of my aunties had given it to me. Then I paused. Either that or you gave it to me? She looked at me and said "Tweleve years ago we thought you were a quick thinker. Now we are not so sure."

Sun 11 Aug MM XX IV

Shop on University

Getting off the bus with Gayatri

Then I turned to follow but the door closed. I ended up inside the bus as it went to the next stop. I hoped that she would realize that I would get off at the next stop and walk back to her.

Working with Gayatri

Tablet Training

Sat 17 Aug

Phone Fix

I was sitting outside among some padded concrete benches. We were working on a project. One of the people who was supposedly working on it with me was apparently nefarious.

Math Test

We were taking a math test. I expected to do well. The teachers assistant came in and handed out the tests but she didn't have enough. She went back to get more. Half of us started the test. Car Door

Then I realized that the main key chain that was holding everything was an oversized safety pin. I undid that and grabbed my keys. I left her to redo her key chain because I was in a hurry. She didn't seem to mind.

The Line

I was in the library. Someone asked me to get a book that was on the other side of the table. The side of the table where they were. I pointed to it. I wondered why they couldn't just get it themselves. But I has to get it. I was tired and it was very inconvenient for me. I crawled under the table to go get it. When I did I saw an old book that happened to be there. It talked about 'the line' which I thought meant the spine of mountains through North and South America. But there was a picture of a cabin in the woods during the four seasons. Where the cabin had been repeated four times so that the right end of one side of the image of the cabin was the left side of the next image. And each image was the same cabin but the yard in front showed the changes through the different seasons.

Thursday 29 August [Michigan]

PMP Thank You

I was supposed to be giving a talk. I had prepared some notes. But then I thought that it was the wrong thing. So I just tried to write down some people to thank. Notes in Math Class

I was having a hard time organizing my notes in Math Class. I had a bunch of home work from other people but I hadn't handed in any of my own. I didn't have any full blank pages to take notes on and when I tried to write on a half sheet it would split in half again until I had just thin strips of paper that were useless for taking notes on.

The teacher came over and gave me some of other peoples homework because they saw the names of the people whose homework I had for some reason. I had to explain that it wasn't me and tried to give it back to them.

They were teaching us about

A -> A(x)A -> A (a, b) -> a - b

But they were doing it the other way around to the way that I was used to. Instead of telling us what and then having us figure out how for ourselves, they were showing us how by writing out all elements of A(x)A on the blackboard and having us write down how they combine together.

This made it harder for me to understand so I had to think about it mote.

Sun 1 Sep MM XX IV

Learning to be a bird

The bird was sick. It was on its feet on the ground in the morning. Later that day we saw it on the top of the roof. It was watching all the other birds go off to the field. One of the other birds stopped to explain that this is what the free birds did. They went to the field in the morning, ate as much as they wanted, and then just did whatever they wanted for the rest of the day. They had some notes on the ground in different locations asking questions about the new bird. They would be asking them when they got back from the field to get to know the new bird better.

I was listening to an old bird, he was saying important things that I wanted to hear.

I couldn't fly straight up but I was at least able to float around the tables. They asked if I could fly into the trees. I looked at them and decided that it was too much.

Another bad work preso

I was supposed to give my thoughts on a design. The product owner had asked for it to be more complicated than normal and I was going to have to explain how that would significantly increase the timeline.

I was waiting in the pub and I finished my two beers before leaving for the bus.

I got to the room and started setting up the presentation. But I couldn't open PowerPoint. I couldn't find the file. There were other videos playing.

We only had 1/2 hour a day for these discussions. For some reason I didn't spend any time prepping for them. All the work was done in the half hour meeting.

Finally an hour had passed and all but the most hard core attendees had already left and we gave up.

Friday 6 Sep MM XX IV

Squatting

We were sitting in a messy kitchen around a table. There were some crackers on the floor and I helped to pick them up. Then we went into the meeting room for the regular meeting. Brad Ludwig was leading it. He complimented several people for their work, not me. The lady who I helped pick up the crackers spoke up for me. Then the meeting was over and it was early, only 1:00 or 2:00 PM. So instead of going home we could just do whatever we wanted with the rest of the day. I decided to do what I always do, which was go to the library on one of the top floors.

I started walking through stairways and hallways to the library. But I saw that they had a picture of me – I was wanted for having been in the wrong place at the wrong time. They didn't know who I was, they just had my picture from a survellience camera. But somebody might recognize me if I went there, so I quickly turned and went a different direction down some stairs.

We got captured and had to escape from some bullies. I explained to the person that I escaped with that I was wanted for squatting. So he felt that it was too risky to be with me and went his own way.

I had to climb outside down girders and iron lattices. Finally I got to the water level. There were pirates who chased me but I managed to make it accross the street. Pretty much everyone here was a risk for being attacked. I managed to cross the water in the street to a place where there was dark, dirty water up a hill and police were there next to it.

Sunday 8 Sep MM XX IV

Chalkboard

We were in a classroom doing a presentation on a chalkboard. When it turned out that I was going to be working with Gayatri, suddenly she started being much more demanding about the level of detail. She got that way she does where she's not listening and nothing you do is right.

Escape

We had to get past the authorities at the border. The border was the corner of the parking lot at the former Wards shopping center on University avenue near Snelling.

I had gotten out once before with a very small load. But this was a major shipment. I wondered how we were going to get past. It turned out that the answer was that the driver was one of their own cops. Gayatri and I were lying in one of the wagons. I had a face mask on. Gayatri was quite agitated. I took the face mask off and put it on her. Then she relaxed and slept, lying in my arms.

We got to the border and were told to wait. We were nervous about getting through but had to calm ourselves becuase if we acted nervous they would suspect something.

While we were waiting one of the other groups that was waiting came around and told us that it was all routine.

Brad Ludwig was there and we talked about various trips into France and England.

Tue 10 Sep

The Good Fairy

We were visiting the vatican or some similar place. We couldn't go in to the inner sanctum because it was closed to the public at this time. Except that I could because the good fairy was flying next to me. I just flew up into the gallery in front of the inner sanctum. The good fairy was flying with me on my right and was part of the reason I was able to fly as well as I could. There was a door. We took off the door. The door slid down the stairs and we lost it. It split apart into pieces. There were four children there and they were going to have to pay for it. It would be $100. I told them that I would pay for it and they could owe me the money divided three or four ways. Because I wasn't certain if the fourth child would be helping with paying. I didn't necessarily expect to get the money back nor did I care.

Friday the 13th of Sep MM XX IV

John's Bed

I was lying in John's bed. Which was in the hallway. He came in and said that it was 3 in the morning. I told him I didn't like to know the time. He pointed out that his secretary was around the corner.

Lost Cards on the Piano

We were on top of the upright piano. We were playing with some cards. There were the regular ones and the extra ones. Then when we were done we started packing them all up. I had been shuffling the regular deck and now I couldn't find it. It was odd that it would have gone anywhere execpt that the place was pretty messy. We stared looking all around. Eventually the other person whose cards they were found them along the edge of the wall. They had already been put back in their box.

Infants Rights

"How much rights does an infant have, anyway?" She asked. "The rights of infants were laid out in Jones vs. State of New York, 1971, section M.33," the cab driver said. "How does a cabby know so much about infant law?" She asked. "All us cabbies are studying to be lawyers. Is there another reason to be a cabbie?"

Irish Countryside

We were in a bedroom. The little girl had to go to the bathroom. The main bathroom was being used by the guest so she had to use the second bathroom.

The second bathroom could only be reached through a crawl hole low in the wall.

She stared to go into it. As she did, the guest started to come out. The guest had been using the second bathroom.

"Oh, I'm just an Irishman from the countryside," he said. "We're used to this type of thing."

College Dorm

I was in the college dorm. I went to the room accross the hall. There was an older lady there. I invited her to get lunch. Her English wasn't good. We agreed to meet later. Some other time. I had to coordinate with the teacher as well. I went back and forth from the teacher's office to the dorm hallway to arrange this.

I got on my broom which was a push broom. With it I could hop and jump much faster than walking.

No one else was doing this but I didn't care.

I went back to the dorm hallway. A young man was coming out of the dorm room across the hall from my room. He explained that the lady I had been talking to was only there once a month.

It was his mom who came to help him clean, and I had mistaken her for another mature student and blamed the misunderstanding on her lack of English.

Leila's clean room

Leila was living in a new place. Instead of boxes everywhere the livingroom/kitchen was pretty empty. There were some pictures on the wall that we went to look at. She seemed to think they

were very important.

Sat 14 Sep MM XX IV

Teaching Lamaze Class at University Avenue

I was on a street just on the north side of University avenue and the highway. People kept brining ladies on stretchers to teach them Lamaze.

Teaching D&D with Miniatures Underground

We were in a room underground. I had to teach the D&D game one chapter at a time. Each chapter was for a different room. I didn't know all the rules and I wasn't sure that I could fill up the entire hour.

We went into the next room which was bigger and I mad promised about all the wonderful prizes that you could get in that room. I then had to qualify that you could only get certain prizes at certain times.

Teaching D&D with a computer

Instead of a rule book you got a giant sculpture. What appeared to be a sculpture of a cat but which was actually a desktop computer thinly disguised by a piece of semi-transparent plastic. It was clear that the computer was going to be giving you all the rules. It had a button on it that said read voicemail. This then explained how to start the computer.

Once we started the game we were in a hallway. The hallway was like a hallway at school. Each room corrseponded to a different part of the game. The first chapter of the game was way down near the end of the hallway on the ground floor. This seemed counterintuitive. It wasn't labeled very well either.

Setting up a sleeping bag with a Chinese Lady

It turned out she was a lesbian. She had just split up with her fiancee. I said I hoped it wasn't because she had joined the program that we were in. She said that she wished she was with the older lady who had been there instead of me. But the older lady couldn't be there for some reason.

We laid the sleeping bag and the sheets out all square. It was something we had done before and been trained in. We were in a room like a college dorm room with windows in the south and a single door into the hallway in the northwest.

Mon 16 Sep MM XX IV

Zycad

I was supposed to go to an office place which was like Zycad, where I worked briefly as a teenager.

I had taken the bus there to the place in the north where I was supposed to go.

I couldn't find the place I was looking for. There were a bunch of other shops there, but not this one.

I was looking on my phone. My phone folded, but the fold became floppy and wouldn't stay extended so I had to hold it in place to check out the map.

It turned out that I was supposed to go to a different place in a different part of town. I stared checking the bus schedules to see how I could get there.

Wrong answer.

Gayatri wanted to know about how we were going to get the washing done in our dorm at the college. We went to the office but they wouldn't answer the question.

We insisted that they write it down on the agenda for the president.

When the president answered they had misunderstood the question. Basically it was going to be your own responsibility to do whatever it was and the college wasn't going to be doing anything about it.

When we talked to the president, catching her in the hallway outside the office, she only wanted to talk about my previous time at the college and how some of my grades hadn't been so good.

We finally hung up the the sheet with the answer they had given us. It was a submission to an art project. We had come in first place. The people who had come in second walked by. I told them it was a 'virtual tie'. They liked that. Gayatri said it was a 'distant second'.

Sat 21 Sep

Interior Design

We were planning carpeting for the walls and ceiling (not the floor) of a room in our new house.

A lady was working with us as the interior designer. A guy I didn't know was asking about the various options.

She was reluctant to wrap the carpet from one surface to another but said that they could do it if necessary by leaving a gap between four inches and two feet. The gap of four inches would cost more of course.

The guy who was choosing this with me said that he wanted the four inch option. I stayed quiet thinking about if money was not an object how much this was going to cost and if we could really afford it.

The guy and the interior design lady talked about which walls they should put it on.

The room we were in had the door in the northwest corner. There was a sink and stove along the west wall. Windows were in the east wall and they overlooked the river Thames which flowed past right outside.

The guy said he wanted the carpet along the south and west walls. I wondered how they would get past the kitchen area but I guessed that they would figure that out.

At first I said that that I liked the idea, because it was best from an aesthetic sense. But then I changed my mind and said that I didn't like it because you would have to move the plumbing. They paused to think about that.

I went over to the window and looked out at the river. People were canoeing down the river, a tributary of which flowed from rightto left (south to north) outside the window and then met the larger river further to the north.

I saw a canoe float by empty. I wondered where its owner had gotten to; if they had fallen in. Then a another canoe floated by empty and yet a third right behind it.

Exterior Shaving

Something very important was happening the next day. There would be drink there and I wondered if I should have one drink the night before so that it wouldn't affect me as much by the difference. I had to get there on my motorcycle. On the way, I stopped at a place and got out to shave. It was a barbers but I didn't want them to shave me; I just wanted to use their mirror.

But the guy kept looking over my shoulder and making me nervous. He didn't seem to understand my request just to do it myself. Because he was a barber and he figured he could do it.

I never finished as completely as I might have liked. Then I went back out and got on my motorcyle. When I did I had a hard time adjusting my backpack. It was like it was a giant wet teddy bear and it was driving and I was the passenger.

Musical Swimming

We went to an all night concert in the park.

But Trent wanted to jump into the water and play the bells that were there so he got all wet.

Then I wanted to leave early because I didn't want to have to deal with drying off.

Mon 23 Sep MM XX IV

Kids playing in the street

I was sitting in the car. I was on a city street near downtown. I thought I would wait a while and then go to the library. There wasn't any work.

It started to get cold so I started to drive away. I negotiated a right turn at the stop light ahead.

I drove along some residential streets. Two young men came out to partially block my way so I accelerated past them and just kept going faster even though the street narrowed. The streets were like those in East St. Paul (which is south of St. Paul). "The North side of my town faced East and the East was facing South" – The Who, "Substitute"

A small child was playing in the street so I just went right onto the lawn to avoid them and kept going at my same speed.

The road narrowed even more and was nothing more than a ragged path adjacent to a park.

Eventually I turned left at a place off the park that I knew to get back on the streets.

Wire Tangle

I was trying to back my car up from in the parking lot but the heater wires were tangled up with the adjacent car and I had to untangle them.

The end of the wire had a special attachement that I was able to affix to the back of my motorcycle.
