Going to visit Clayton

Sat 28 Sep MM XX IV

Lost

I was going somewhere. I had to go south along the highway over the bridge, turn left on the county road go a little ways and turn right. It was easy.

But when I got to the county road I couldn't navigate the turn. So I tried to walk through the park that was south of the county road instead. I could see the map on gps from straight above but I couldn't zoom out far enough to see the whole way to my destimation.

Some animals came and followed me through the park. There was snow in some places.

Ahead there were many many giant grubs and they were coming down the path toward us. We couldn't go that way so we tried to climb up the bank on the right (south) to get to another road. But the snow and the railings on that road got in the way.

Sun 29 Sep MM XX IV

We were going to the bank. There were lots of people waiting in line. Everyone was talking about the number of people who were just one paycheck away from tragedy and if there was a system shock how much damage it would do.

I was trying to put a fourth class below the working class – the indebted class.

It was our turn at the teller. We had a list of 3 to invest in and we thought two of them were better. We mentioned these to the teller but she just rattled off a bunch of information about each of them.

Sun 6 Oct MM XX IV

Daylight Saving

I was working from home in my bedroom in 1377. There was a video meeting that I called in to. There were a lot of people in the office. I thought to myself that I need to go in more often.

As I was watching the meeting, on mute, with the camera off, the clock on the wall moved forward from 1:00 to 2:00. The clock was set to AM instead of PM and the wrong day.

So I had been at work an hour early all the morning.

The Mugwumps

The father was like the father in Home Before Dark. He had a hard time getting his daughter to school on time and had many other symptoms of alcoholism but he never drank and never had.

His wife went to work. She didn't always tell him the truth about what she did.

Halloween was coming. His daughter was there with some of her friends. She asked him if the Mugwumps would come on Halloween again this year. The father thought no. She asked again. He said, well alright, one last time. One final visitation from the Mugwumps.

So he went over to the side of the house and started pissing into an electrical outlet.

He had to reach his hand out to open the outlet up so that he could piss inside.

After he was done with that he opened up the adjacent electrical outlet to reveal that it was a hidden compartment. From it, after some difficulty, he pulled out a pail of pebbles. The pebbles were all rounded and seemed still moist though they were dry. They had all come from the swamp where the Mugwumps lived. They were the pebbles that could summon the Mugwumps. As he walked away carrying the pail, you could see that he had gotten his hand wet and that it had started to turn green and scaly, distorted and bumpy in places.

The Mugwumps were intelligent creatures about the size of a large dog and with skin like a toad, but regular legs made for land, not rear legs made for hopping as a toad has.

They peered out over a ridge at the edge of their swamp into the nearby villiage. Will we go into the town for halloween tonight? Only if we are called, only if we are called.

The father, his daughter and several of her friends were standing in the driveway outside their house. He had the pail of pebbles. It was dusk but not yet sunset. The Mugwumps would not come until actual sunset. The pebbles were both the bait that would bring them in and the missiles that would drive them away.

The children started casting the pebbles about in the street. They were playing and doing so at such a rate that it was questionable if there would be enough pebbles left to drive the Mugwumps away after they came to get the pebbles that were being used as bait.

Other ghostly creatures of various sizes from the size of a small cat to the size of an elephant started to appear out of nothing and float down the street.

But these were not the Mugwumps and they were niether interested in the pebbles nor could they be harmed by them. Also it was not sunset yet.

Tue 8 Sep MM XX IV

Hippies on the escalator

We were leaving. We were on a carpet and it was just floating along the corridors which were like an office building or a shopping center. Everyone was dressed formally but we had beads and long hair.

We floated past the people trying to pretend we didn't care about being different and started to go down the escalator on our flying carpet.

GOTV on a bike

I continued on and was riding my bike down a street in Minneapolis. We were supposed to be doing some kind of volunteer activity like GOTV (Get Out the Vote). My partner, who was driving a car felt that it had gotten too dark to continue our activity, parked the car in an empty parking lot and left. This left me there with my bicycle. It was a long way to bike over the river back home and I didn't know the busses or if I even had any money.

Magic Tricks in my Father's storeroom

We were cleaning out my father's storeroom, which was a semi-abandoned shed on a farm. The windows and doors were all to small and you had to unfold the window and then climb in.

Inside a lady was showing a magic trick. She would stamp her feet and then disappear. You could see the switch that she stamped her foot on so you knew that was part of the trick. But when she disappeared there was a square bench where she used to be. You kind of knew that she was in there, but it was so small, it was kind of amazing that she could fit in it. And it didn't go all the way to the floor, it was like a table. We bent down to examine the underside. It was curved so that it looked thinner than it really was, but even so there was just not a lot of space for a person to fit in there.

Cleaning up Watlow Files

Leaving Watlow. I was putting all my stuff in boxes. All the Watlow team was helping me pack up. I had to be gone that day.

They put all my boxes out by the dock. I went over to get a truck to rent to hall them away. There was a motorcycle uber rider there. They offered to take me. I had to explain that I had a lot of things that I needed to take with me; I needed a truck. They were like, don't worry I have a lot of friends. We'll just get a whole bunch of motorcylces to cart you and all your stuff away.

.. and trying to get an uber to take them away

Sat 12 Oct MM XX IV

Numbers

We were in the room in the southeast corner of Vincent hall, the math building on the U of M campus.

There was a cereal commercial playing between children's cartoons That included a panel that was something to the effect of 123.234.345 it was supposed to be like an IP address except it wasn't actually an IP address they were just trying to take advantage of a tech vibe to sell their cereal.

I complained that they were using the numbers as symbols. There was no possibility of addition or mulitplication or any other operations on these numbers; they could be replaced with any other set of symbols. So I proposed – and here is where it gets tounge in cheeky – that we could create a new set of symbols. The first could be a circle, the second a line, the third a squiggle, and then two cups on their sides and so on.

They didn't understand what I was saying or couldn't hear. Someone tried drawing two cups on their sides but instead drew a cupboard on its side. It was actually a very detailed Ikea-like drawing. That person was a little older and from an eastern european country.

So I got up to the whiteboard to repeat myself for everyone in the room. It wasn't a class. It was more like a couple of different classes mixing between two classes. There was already a lot of writing on the whiteboard and I couldn't erase it. The only marker I had was red. I wrote in the lower right corner. I was afraid that it would be illegible. It was just barely legible.

I started explaining again, going over the whole story of how the cereal commercial's numbers could just be replaced by a set of symbols. For example the first symbol could be a circle: 0. Then the second symbol could be a line: 1. The third symbol could be a squiqqle: 2. Then two cups on their side: 3. Then an upside-down chair: 4. Then a sinuous line: 5. And so on. Then everybody got the joke and I stepped back down from the whiteboard.

Sunday 12 Oct MM XX IV

Leave your keys

I was in a care home. It was like Carriage House and it was also like a room in my grandparents house that I was staying in. My dad was coming to pick me up to take me to my real home. But first he was going to drop me off at Macalester.

I went to grab my keys which were lying on a shelf. I realized that I didn't need to take them with because I could just come back here from school before going to my real home and get them.

The pillars

We walked into the library in Macalester which was a huge building with four or five floors and high ceilings. The bookshelves were spaced widely. People were milling about. Some exploring the books, others getting from one place to another as this building was central for connections throughout the school. There were wide escalators going up and down that were constantly busy with people.

There were two carved brown wooden pillars that hung from the ceiling – not reaching even halfway to the floor – in the main lobby. These had been part of the inauguration ceremony for the building but were now pretty well forgotten.

One of them came loose. For some reason having come loose was related to me. Because it was all painted brown you could hardly make out what the carvings were. No contrast. And when they were 10 feet above people hanging from the ceiling any meaning in the carvings was certainly lost. A maintenance person came over to start to repair it.

My father came over and said that it was time to go.

I thought that really there was no point in repairing it. They could replace it with something much more modern. Much more colorful.

So I went to look for the people who were fixing the column so that I could explain this to them. I went up the escalator to the next floor. I looked around some of the bookshelves. A young student was debating whether this large oversized book – easily a meter – was filed under the correct place in the dewey decimal system. When I looked, apparently it was.

The building was so large that it opened out onto some park areas. There were no walls; you just went slowly from library to park with the library tables and bookshelves thinning out and grass and picnic benches increasing. This way you could choose your level of comfort if you liked to read in the park. The tables were so spread out that I thought that it would be great for some solitary study.

But how did you stay warm in the winter? This was not an issue at this time as the weather was quite comfortable. But there were no walls. Apparently they just kept the heating on blowing warm air out of the building that it was warm all the way to the end. This didn't seem very efficient or sustainable but apparently they had worked it out.

I couldn't find the people responsible for the repair of the column. It had been over an hour. I wondered why my father or the other people we were with hadn't called or texted to find out where I was.

I looked at my phone and sure enough there were some missed texts. My phone was frozen and I had to reboot it which was why I hadn't realized that I had gotten the texts.

I rebooted and went back down to the first floor to find my father and the others.

They were nowhere to be seen so I went outside to the street by myself.

Maybe not a good investment

I turned right outside the entrance to the library and walked along the sidewalk.

I was going to be recieving $100,000 which I had planned to use a good chunk of to pay for another year of school.

I was thinking that by investing in another year of school I was going to be able to exponentially increase my options. But then I thought what if that didn't happen? What if by giving myself the extra year I didn't somehow find quantitatively many new options?

Then spending the money just to float for another year wouldn't really be such a good investment.

No they were trees

I went back to the library. But this time evil people were doing bad things. I tried to get up to the top floor in the corner where it was happening.

I had to cut away at cables that were running water and other food and storage containers as I went up the escalators.

People were being led into a room in the corner and there was a conveyor belt of items including potted plants coming out from the other side of the room.

"You are killing them!" I yelled. "No, they are still alive," came the response. "They are these trees!." Bwah ha ha.

Th 17 Oct MM XX IV

Bad Uber

We were leaving Thermo King. Because I had a guitar, a balalaika and a ukelele I thought I would order an Uber instead of taking the bus like everybody else was.

So I opened my phone (it was fold sized) and opened the app. It was made to look like the dashboard of a VW and told you about how easy it was to use. Just push the button!

So well I pushed the button and the app decided that since I already had a car (which was the VW) that it would just auto drive me home instead of getting a different car to come.

Except that I hadn't put my three guitars in the trunk. So I pushed the stop button so that I could go back and get my guitars.

Except that we were in traffic so it couldn't stop right away. It just kept pulling over on to side streets farther and farther away from where I wanted to be and going further and further downhill..

9 PM Meeting

Me Dan Smith and a lady were at work. I said why don't we all go to lunch on Thursday. She said she couldn't because she had a 9 PM meeting. 9 PM?! That's too late! What she really wanted to do was fly overnight for the meeting.

We told her just ask your boss for authorization. I said she should go for the whole weekend but she seemed to think that flying all the way there for just one night was fine.

We went down a hallway which was like a hallway in Mechanic Arts and she was trying to find an empty office to study in. Tim Walker was in the office on the end. He was picking up something from under his desk. She waved to him and when she saw that his office wasn't empty she went into the office next door. I followed her in still wanting to talk about lunch and travel plans. Then Tim came in to chat as well.

[in a sleeping bad with the television on listening to The Who]

Wed 23 Oct MM XX IV

High School in Britain.

I was going back to school to try to get my high school degree. I got two tapes which had my 11th and 12th grade record on them, but it turned out that the 11th grade was just the raw score and the 12th grade was still blank. There were a lot of red numbers on the 11th grade tape so I was worried that I would have to go back for another year.

Reality show with car chase.

Somebody had been on some kind of a talent show and had been in competition with somebody else and that caused scandal and they dropped out for a long time but now they were back and they did a skit that repeated that whole episode.

Then as they were leaving, they were hitching their trailer up to truck to take it out, but somebody else took the trailer and hit it up to a semi. And then they were riding down the street. The semi didn't know that they were behind them. It was bitter cold and they were trying to get the semi's attention.

We were shouting at them to tell them it was unsafe.

sweeping up.

Karma Pole.

Sat 2 Nov MM XX IV

Driving back from Detroit

I had gone to visit my mom in Michigan, but I only stayed there one night and then I drove back overnight. I drove the whole night to arrive back in Minnesota and then I was gonna sleep and I wondered why I Had rushed back so quickly if I couldn't have stayed in Michigan longer.

Haskell

There was a class that I was in and I was going to be, I had skipped some classes so I was going to miss the final exam but I had a whole bunch of notes. I was working on a cryptographic program in Haskell and it was a more sophisticated version of the Caesar cipher and I had lots and lots of very carefully printed out notes with really nice font.

I asked this girl who for some reason was in the living room of 1377 if she wanted to help me with working on the Haskell program.

I started to take notes but I couldn't get organized.

Nap with Dog

I needed to rest after driving all night. So I lay down on the mattress. The mattress was at an angle. There was a dog there, a large dog. The dog wanted to go outside, but I was like, no, we're going to lie here and sleep for a little while longer.

Tue 10 Dec MM XX IV

Bike Trip

I was on a bike trip with my father. He parked the car and we went off biking down some trails and over hills. Along some bike paths. The path split two ways and I took the right most closet to where the highway was.

Then he said that he was tired and we'd best stop for the night. I might have continued for a while longer.

He said that we should get the car that we had parked. He asked if I could get it. I said that I couldn't. There was no way I could remember where it was and I would just end up walking the streets aimlessly for the rest of the dream which I didn't want to do.

So he went and got it. How we were going to do miles of biking accross country and into the next state all the while coming back to where we had left the car in the morning was not made clear.

We got in the car and he handed me a map. He was driving. I had to find Minneapolis, except this was't the Minneapolis in Minnesota where we started, it was the one that was a suburb of Indianapolis in Indiana where we had biked to. It was an old map with the interstate in yellow like we used to have before cell phones. I kept turning it over where it had a map of the world and turning it upside down to try to find it but I couldn't see anything except Indianapolis and other suburbs.

Finally we ended up at a restaurant with a few other people. It wasn't a fancy place, it was more the kind of place that he liked. They didn't have beer and liquour. We all ordered sweet drinks. I got the lemon lime one.
